The Human Diaspora:

In the radiant dawn of the 33rd century, humanity has conquered the stars.
From the ashes of the Great Abundance Collapse; when unchecked plenty bred decay, despair, and near-extinction, the Neo-Asceticists arose. Who rejected the poison of endless comfort, embraced voluntary scarcity, and rekindled the fire of life. Guided by purpose, vitality, and faith, they claimed their birthright: the galaxy itself.
Across billions of worlds, forty quintillion souls flourish in vibrant, deliberate diversity. The Seven Tribes of Terra: Star Peoples, Cathedralites, Black Earthers, Prophet Followers, World Dreamers, Sinocrats, and Sea Peoples, form a brilliant mosaic of cultures, each pursuing its own vision of dignity, strength, and meaning. Transhumans, adapted to alien worlds, and welcomed xenos live alongside baseline humanity, all sheltered beneath the divine protection of the Imago Dei.
Above them watches the Galactic Government, the Galov, a soft theocracy of the five faiths, enforcing two iron laws: the sacred dignity of every thinking being, and the inviolable freedom of the will. Peacekeepers stand ready, to guard the boundless variety of human possibility against any who would crush it.
The stars are humanityâ€™s inheritance. Purpose has triumphed over decadence. In disciplined scarcity, mankind has found not chains, but wings.
There is faith. There is struggle. There is endless becoming.
This is the age of the Human Diaspora. Vast, vivid, and alive.

Alternate Concise Version:

The Great Abundance Crisis was mankind's last near-extinction event.
Ninety percent were pruned;
The Children of the Lotus Eaters destroyed themselves.
Only we remain.

Much of the Collapse is unknown,
for it was Damnatio Memoriae-
scoured from record,
burned from data-vault and bone.

But from the ashes we rebuilt,
and Humanity learned a lesson we would never forget:

Purpose is paramount,
Decadence is Poison,
Mankind must reach the stars,
and claim our spiral mandate.

In the asceticism of our forebears, 
we found not chains,
but wings.

There is faith. 
There is struggle. 
There is endless becoming.
This is the age of the Human Diaspora:

Vast, vivid, and alive.

Rough Timeline of Events:
DML = Damnatio Memoriae Level, the extent which the history has been wiped out or suppressed by the Neo-Asceticists.
Pre 1990's, DML: None, nearly all of it has been well preserved.
1991 to 2008, DML: Very Low. (Preserved in Early Snapshots of the Old Internet)
2008 to 2016, DML: Low. (Notable events appear to be missing. Overall narrative still intact.)
2016 to 2025, DML: Moderate. (Major expunges. Keywords such as "Summer of Love", "ACAB", "Woke", "SJW" expunged from record. Only recorded in "Book of the Damned". Context of these terms unknown. Other terms such as "MAGA", and the "Great America Movement" are more preserved, albeit fragmented. DML drops greatly with election of President DeSantis. The Galov suspects this is part of some kind of now long forgotten culture war.)
2025 to 2040, DML: Very Low. (Ended with the election of President Victoria Cortez. Due to the DML level, the period from 1990 to 2040 is known as the Little Abundance Period. The events of the 3rd World War are very well documented.)
2040 to 2070, DML: None. (The Interwar period, as well as the 4th World War period is very well documented.)
2070 to 2170, DML: Moderate. (Beginning of the 2nd Little Abundance Period. Contradictory narratives continue to persist, with world maps and conflicting information everywhere. To the current count of the Galov, there are at least 2 major, and 4 minor conflicting narratives, each which go into different degrees of complexity. This period ends in the year 2170, with the "War for the Human Condition" beginning, a major early transhumanism war.)
2181: Meta-Man attack on Earth. DML: None.
2170 to 2300, DML: None. (Interestingly, the Neo-Asceticists did not purge the record of Earth being attacked by the Roasians, nor the occupation of Earth by the Roasians. Suggesting that their shame was not out of human pride alone, as the record of a xeno occupation of Earth is remarkably intact. Humanity liberates itself by the year 2300.)
2300 to 2350: DML: None. (Almost immediately after the defeat of the Roasians, the Transhumanism Wars kick off again, this time into the 2nd Transhumanism Wars.)
2350 to 2452, DML: Low, progressing to almost total. (Less than 100 chronological events are known from the era of 2400 to 2450. This is known as the "Great Abundance Crisis", only remembered in loose fragments, as well as the aforementioned "Book of the Damned". One of these events is the founding of the Neo-Asceticist movement, created in the year 2376.)
2452 onwards, DML: None. (No further events were deemed necessary to expunge. The Neo-Asceticists disband.)
2500's: Beginning of the Stellar Exodus.
2700's: Great Cybernetic Revolt.
2900's: Collapse of the 2nd American Republic. The last of the pre-Abundance political continuities. This marks the formal start of the age of the 7 Tribes of Terra, though others trace them as far back as the 2600's.
3000's: Conquest of the Great Khan. Near reunification of all of mankind, only stopped at the battle of Earth. The Great Assembly of the Faiths creates the modern Galov.
3100's: Consolidation of the Early Galov. Instatement of Imago Dei, and Free Will.
3300's: Second Defense of Earth. Imperial Era, crowning of the Governorship of Earth as Emperor.
3400's: Destruction of Concept Draggers, Beginning of Conceptual Era.


The Great Abundance Collapse:
"Remember always. Abundance is poison. It will lure you in with false promises. Like a drug, it will put you to sleep." -The Galov.
Galactic Society works on a basis of voluntary scarcity, not post-scarcity. Why is that? It all has to do with an event in the long distant past, and the death of humanity's last universal empire. By the 23rd and 24th centuries, much of the world was unified under the Great Universalist Empire. An entity that began in North America, and eventually took over the entire world. In what would eventually become the precursor to the Star Peoples.
By the late 24th century, consumption and traditional consumerist capitalism was entering its final stages, with what was often called the "saturation of consumption". Humanity had by and large had their needs met, their wants satiated. Nearly all production was hyper optimized. And with no more demand to fill, governments and corporations alike began to do the only thing they could think of. The inflation of demand.
The oversupply of all goods convinced the communists of the world that the day was here, refuting capitalism's claim of creative destruction, they began the "World Revolution", one which swept the world, and quickly united it around one government. But now with the drive for innovation unplugged, there was nowhere to go but to give the people what they wanted. More hedonism.
The people atrophied, men grew weaker and weaker, and the bureaucrats put in charge of "the people's factories" mismanaged them, as the standards of life around the world decayed. To satisfy the people, the world bureaucrats turned to yet even more hedonism, which decayed the minds.
It was the Neo-Asceticists, those who rejected hedonism that resisted this rot. Preserved religion, vitalism, Darwinism within their ranks. The World Revolution saw them as a threat, and they were faced with harsh persecution. But as humanity lost the will to live, and eventually procreate, the World Revolution collapsed from within. The people of the World Revolution dwindled fewer and fewer, until they all killed themselves out of despair, or died out of old age.
"Heed my words, sons of Earth. I offer you nothing... But your birthright. I offer you purpose, I offer you dignity, I offer you... The stars and the galaxy." - Oby Collins, one of the leaders of the Neo-Asceticist Movement.
The entire era, from the 24th and the 25th century was Damnatio Memoriae, of humanity's spiritual low point. The Galov does not like to talk about it. And most have aggressively expunged what their ancestors were up to during the Era of the Lotus Eaters, except those who had joined the Neo-Asceticists.
And the Neo-Asceticists would go on to settle the stars.

Voluntary Scarcity:
It should be important to note that Voluntary Scarcity is not a ceiling, it is a kind of puritanism. It does not say "we should voluntarily produce less", but "we should voluntarily limit our consumption". The Neo-Asceticists, and later thinkers in the "Spiral Mandate" would demand more for the sake of more, to mobilize and outproduce as much as they can, but to not channel this overcapacity towards consumption, but instead massive megaprojects, and star-spanning infrastructure, in what is known as "monumentalism" or "ideological capitalism", using one's wealth to either push a cause one believes in, or into grand monuments.

///
The following is a retelling of one nation among many in the Post-Abundance collapse world. The world clearly exists outside of America, but the nation serves as a good representative sample of the re-emergance of humanity after the Great Abundance collapse.

Post-Abundance Collapse America:
The now defunct United States is probably one of the most influential pre Stellar Exodus nation states, still exerting a silent influence over human space. Though some lines of institutional continuity was continued through the Abundance Collapse, some draw a distinction between the pre-collapse "First" American Republic and the post-collapse "Second" American Republic. The catastrophe of the Great Abundance Collapse acted as a "Great Filter" for the American population. So when the stars and stripes set sail for the stars again, it could be described as a "Techno-Puritan Democracy". 
Techno, for it was unapologetically, sometimes aggressively pro-technology. Puritan, for it was both religiously and ascetically fanatical, rejecting comfort for "will to power". A democracy, perhaps last time humanity attempted to apply democracy on a universal scale. Though American-style democracy still survives as the local governance of several planetary-scale regional governments. Many the result of American colonization.
The United States has long since collapsed. But it was one of the states that many future states would look back towards. Perhaps saying it was as Rome was to Europe is not quite accurate, Ancient Athens might be a more apt metaphor, given how large humanity eventually became.

The Americans that left could be categorized into many groups, as the demographics of America were fundamentally changed by the Great Abundance Collapse:
-Magnolians
--Caveliers (Magnolians but more militarized)
-Tidewater
-Breadbasket Culture
-Mayflower Culture
-Puritans
--Techno-Puritans (The de-facto elite group, stemmed from the remnants of Silicon Valley)
-Low Tech Groups
--Amish
--Mennonites
-Mormons
-Texans
--Frontiermen

The Fall of America:
The United States, in the form of the 2nd American Republic survived another 500 years after the Great Abundance Collapse. The problem was just that humanity got too large. What used to be a continental monopoly that made it the most secure nation on the block became too small to govern a humanity that was now spanning hundreds of stars. By this point, Earth was transforming into something nigh recognizable. New cultures rose and fell, and the US proper was now reduced to the area around Washington DC, roughly the states of Maryland, Virginia, and West Virginia. To the south was an aggressive, expansionist empire that had grown out of the American Southwest, and the emergence of the Castillo culture. Neither American nor Mexican. 
To the north, nearly the entire Arctic circle had been taken by the Illumirians, transhuman mutants adapted to the cold, from the world of Boreas who had come to claim its throne at the roof of the world. And to the West, were a series of separatists that had parted ways with the American experiment. From the Deseret Mormons, Cascadia, the Breadbasket Peoples, and the Confederation of the Lakes. Now as distant from America as the West Europeans were to Rome.
America had long outlasted any of the peers of its time. It lived to see a world where there was no longer a Russia, nor a France, nor Mexico. Even China had gone the way of the dustbin, a completely new, yet familiar Sinitic dynasty had replaced it. The nation was small, only ceremonially the leader of a vast diaspora.
There was a time when the call to arms was sounded one final time. When the vast diaspora, spanning a thousand stars came back to Earth one last time for the defense of the mother of their culture. But when they finally arrived, they found that DC had finally fallen, and America was no more. With that, America finally passed from nation to myth.
But in the vast diaspora of the Star Peoples, Mother America had given life to many beautiful children. Many of which would surpass even her legacy across the stars.
The United States, as marginal as it was in the later years of its existence, was the last link to the pre-Abundance Collapse past. None of the nations that existed during the Great Abundance Collapse existed anymore. Earth was now a world ruled by warlords, nascent peoples and mutants. The Old Peoples of Earth had all finally left Earth. This date is considered the end of the Post-Abundance era, and the dawn of the 7 Tribes of Terra.
(Explicit note: While the Americans have one of the larger diasporas among the stars, they are only a subset of the greater Star Peoples, which are in of themselves, one of the 7 co-equal Houses of Terra.)

The 7 Tribes of Terra (Sometimes called the 7 Houses of Terra):
Much of the human or posthuman diaspora can trace its origins to one of the 7 seed groups that emerged from old Earth. These groups, while normally near-baseline can have notable variation. These are known as "Terrans", and primarily live on Gaia worlds (Worlds that are similar enough to Earth and her biomes) or Gaia stations. (Huge orbital stations or O'Neil cylinders made to emulate Earth climate.)

Sinocrats (Sino/Confucian)
The Sinocratic core is consisting of two things. Meritocratic Legalism and Bureaucracy. Only somewhat balanced by the addition of Confucian values. Those who break away exist, and are directed towards Buddhist or Taoist philosophy. The Sinocratic Core is almost unified by default, with periphery cultures (Mainly Korea) occasionally breaking away. The Celestial Kingdom continuously falls and is revived, being the longest continuity of heritage dating all the way back to ancient times.
The Platinum Emperor (AI) is more of a ceremonial figure. The secular god of the kingdom, his dictats are absolute. He is fragmented and tired. Only on occasion does the current Celestial Emperor (human) consult him for advice, to which it will respond cryptically.

Lost Tribes:
The Lost Tribes are a kind of "lost 8th tribe" of sorts. Not lost because they're actually lost, but because they are normally grouped in with others, and some advocate for them to become the 8th tribe. Though due to everything from the flag, to the mythos, and everything else referencing the number 7, and general "good vibes" of the number 7, there is much inertia in the way.
The Lost Tribes are normally categorized as parts of the Star Peoples, and while some people of indigenous heritage are fine with being part of the "New Worlders", alongside Sub-Saharan Africans, North and South Americans, others ask for a categorical distinctiveness.
Compared to the other subgroups of the 7 Tribes, these groups are fairly small, and somewhat underrepresented in the Human Diaspora, due to their lack of population base during the time of the Stellar Exodus.
The Lost Tribes are divided into two groups. The Primitivists and the Modernists. The Primitivists seek to preserve live before some pre-defined time, normally the age of colonialism. Modernists seek to advance their culture forward into the future. Unless otherwise noted, all groups have both primitivist and modernist variants.
-Caretakers
--(North)
---Sky-Watchers (Great Plains)
---Wind-Walkers (They really like flying and aviation, apparently.)
---Mound Builders (Mississippi)
---Redwood Culture (West Coast)
---Ice-Walkers (Inuit)
--(South)
---Riverroot Culture (Amazon)
---Canopy Culture
---Mountain Shapers (Inca, they really like the Mountains)
--Dream Watchers (Aboriginal Australians)
-Gift Givers (They use voluntary scarcity economics to create the gift economy)
-The Architects (A more modernist take on Indigenous culture, based more on Ecological preservation.)
--Solarians (Extreme environmentalism mixed with extreme techno-optimism.)
---Xenolects (Preserve xeno ecology)
---Terralects (Spread and preserve Old Earth's ecology.)
-Hearth-Fire Cultures (Indigenous African, Primitivists only. Modern African diaspora are seen as "Star People", and to the Hearth-Fires, are "Black Europeans".)
--Iron Tongues (Oralists, have banned writing.)
---Tongue-Speakers (Iron Tongues who have reintegrated with modern society, but kept the prohibition on writing or memory devices.)
--Old Griots (Abstrains from the Great Confederation.)

The Gift Givers, the Architects, and the Solarians:
These three are the "Big Three" of the Modernist side of the Lost Tribes. While the Primitivists are contetn with returning to the glory days of the past, the modernists are not content with simply returning to the past, they seek to actively build the future that is unapologetically theirs. Not just a crude imitation of the futures already forged by the white, black, or yellow man.

The Other Worlds:
Though the "7 Houses" are a useful way to categorize the 7 seed groups of humanity. They are far from all inclusive, even if we're solely talking about baseline humans, not even touching things like transhumans yet. The state of the galaxy is so pluralistic, fragmented, and so many permutations of hybrids exist that the following exercise can be attempted.
Imagine for a moment, any reasonable permutation of human culture, so long as it is physically possible, and stable enough to not collapse within a generation. That likely exists somewhere in the vast expanses of the "Other Worlds". Every permutation can you imagine of people coming together and creating hybrid cultures, likely exists. There are variants of Swedish-Thai, Turkmenistani-Botswanan, an Taiwanese-Tibetan-Paraguayan-Dinkan amalgamation culture, so on, and so forth.
And there is not even a limitation of primarily drawing on real cultures. Entire worlds have been founded on fandom, or fantasy concepts, creating new cultures from fiat, ideology, or new stories. The "Big 5" of religions dominate, but new religions have been founded based on ideology, or secularism, or humanism, to a misinterpreted fandom interpreting fiction as real, or a comedic misinterpretation of "Lord of the Rings". A splinter emerges from a splinter from a splinter until it no longer resembles the original. It is said nearly every permutation of the human condition can be found in the Other Worlds.
For reference, it is estimated only about 40% of the baseline human population is "cleanly" part of the 7 tribes. The rest is a ever evolving fractal of human creativity and new ways of living. The main "organized megaculture" or "organized structure" outside of the 7 tribes is the Yanko-Ring, and many of these "Other Worlds" are located in what are sometimes called "the Brilliant Worlds". Or the "Middle Ring" between the core territories of the 7 Tribes, and the Yanko Ring.
The primary limitation is that they not violate the Galov's mandate of Imago Dei, nor the mandate on free will. More on that later.

Notable examples:
-The Contract States (No direct lineage from the 7 Tribes, instead a libertarian voluntary contract state.)
--Treaty Keepers (A specifically indigenous focused crypto contract state. Good luck breaking the treaty when they're enforced by code.)
-Union of Workers Darwinist Republics (Darwinistic Cyber-Communism. Seen with suspicion by the Galov, but decided they were acceptable after they found out they promoted weight lifting and collective action as opposed to hedonism.)
-The Other Houses (Lots of crackpot monarchies carved out by a military warlord, who later created an aristocratic form of governance, and accepted an honor code, softening greatly as a result.)
-The Technocratic Unions (Core group splintered from the Prophet Followers, originating from Mesopotamia-descended peoples.)
-Cities of Light (Tourist trap, the planet. There's one in every sector. They bloom and die like mushrooms, sustained entirely by hype. In 100 years, they will be gone, and more will have taken their place.)
-Fable Makers (Apparently a bunch of artistic types intentionally celebrate fandom culture, and indulge in creative/expressive excess.)

Union of Workers Darwinist Republics:
"Luxuries are a bourgeois decadence. The purpose of a worker is to work, to rise above, and become strong enough to demand their own liberation. The capitalist class wants a weak and docile working class. We call for them to train, to rise as the director of their own destiny, to tear down the system of capital with their will and strength alone. Workers of the world, unite! You have nothing to lose but your chains!"
An absolutely bizarre ideological movement, this is the one form of communism that the Galov has been able to tolerate. In contrast to most communist movements, which devolve into hedonism, decadence, and societal collapse from the overindulgence in automated luxuries, the UWDR views them with utter contempt. They believe in empowerment of the self, the cultivation of strength, and the belief that work is a virtue, one which makes you stronger. And urges all workers to toil for the sake of the revolution, that all workers may find empowerment through their own strength.
The entire population is a population of "shock workers", and have achieved almost superhuman abilities through sheer training. They believe decadence to be capitalist poison, as luxury and wealth. They believe the capitalist class becomes obsolete when the workers empower themselves through training, and see most "Western progressive" communists to be capitalist subversions. The Galov is utterly befuddled by this movement, but as they do not advocate for hedonism, their one cardinal rule, they have mostly been left alone.
The UWDR has dominated weightlifting competitions for decades now, and weightlifting is one of the nation's most popular pastimes. Ironically, or perhaps uniquely for any communist movement, this has created a hyper-meritocratic form of communism. Where private property is abolished, all people start at an even footing (all start with nothing but their own bodies and minds), but your destiny is your responsibility and yours alone. They straight up desire to completely render the capitalist class obsolete by making the workers so strong they can do all the work of the capitalists, ending class exploitation.
The weak and the disabled are given augmentations, but they are still expected to overcome with willpower. It is okay to be born weak, it is not okay to stay weak. All are expected to improve, to dominate, not necessarily to compete with others, but to compete with your self.

Half-Xeno Worlds:
These are human-dominated worlds with a large xeno minority, or even plurality/majority. If even the Other Worlds don't fit your desire for pluralism, this is here to spell it out explicitly. You can also craft hybrid worlds (or pure xeno worlds) based on any alien found here, or heck, one you make up yourself.

The Pact of the Sons of Man/the House of Man:
Though these groups generally bicker a ton, there is a collective agreement that if human civilization, or the Earth itself comes under threat, then every group will put aside their differences and come together in common defense of the species. This agreement was invoked exactly twice. Once during the conquests of the Great Khan, when his armies finally came to the doorstep of Earth, and once again when a galaxy eater came within 3 light years of Earth, and almost 20% of the galactic population pitched in to participate in the Leviathan battle to come. Terra is sacred, Terra is holy.

Transhuman Groups:

"Transhuman" here is not used to prefer to humans who modified their genes (Almost all groups do that). Instead, it's an almost pejorative term to refer to those who are biologically human-descended groups which trace their lineage to something other than an old Terran culture. (Though this includes the minor peoples such as the Sublimians or the Jews.) Instead, Transhuman groups trace their lineage to the first settlers lab grown and engineered to settle difficult to settle worlds. Most transhuman groups are specialized for a single world, and then continuously transplanted to new compatible worlds. Most transhumans are planet bound, unable to take advantage of economies of scale due to their heavily genetically splintered nature.
Due to their utility as a tool, as opposed to being people, they are seen as tools or "less-than" normal Terran groups. The Transhumanist League is a major transhumanist rights advocacy group that promotes transhuman interests. Just like the Terran groups, they descend from several seed groups, usually from life-compatible, but not human inhabitable worlds near Earth, and splintered outwards as well.
Outside of these main groups, basically every "near-habitable" world has its own transhumanist culture that is usually exclusive to just that one world.

Lunarians (Creator: Star Peoples)

Luna was settled by near-baseline Star Peoples, and specially engineered Lunarians, made for low gravity worlds. Their culture is said to be quiet, cold, and sterile, much like their environment. Though they were outside of the "mainline" 7 tribes, their close proximity and eventual massive political influence bought them a seat at the table. They're the strongest culture outside of the 7 tribes.
As well, Luna received a lot of influence from the early Omnithecia, adopting a large East African influence, and importing the Omnithecian library, which eventually became the Lunar Library.
-Luna (Discovered to have moderate amounts of water in Lunar regolith)
--Regolith Culture (For drier worlds)
---Mercurians (For even hotter, drier worlds.)
---Dust Culture (For colder, drier worlds.)
--Lunar Lavatube Culture (Colloquially called "Lunar Molemen")
---Blackwater Culture (For wetter, airless worlds. They live in cold underwater aquafirs.)
--Star Dwarves (For when they were sent to even lower gravity dwarf planets.)
---Specklers (When they were basically sent to inhabit asteroids.)
----Void Dwellers (Low energy, resource efficient which move slow motion near in the stellar depths. Isolationist, barely moves, very fast time perception.)
--Gemstone Culture (See Diamond Belt below)
-Omnithecians (Loosely/incorrectly translatable as "the All-Library")
--Librarians
--The Lunar Library

Dust Eaters/Original Martians (Creator: Star Peoples)

Dust Eaters was the original group sent to colonize Mars, barely seen as human at the time, mostly there just to filter the air before the real human settlers came in. Displaced from their holy homeland of Mars, and sent across the stars to colonize other "dust worlds". They claim to be the original Martians.
-Mars
--Dust Raiders (Syncretism/Alignment with Sand Raider Culture)
--Dry Oasis Culture (These people brought around their own water retaining plants to create local dry oasis)
--Dust Sailors (Those who ride duststorms)
--New Red Army (Martian Nationalists who want to retake Mars)
---Sons of Mars (Extremist terrorist organization, a la ISIS.)
--Noachians (Found a niche operating "half-terraformed" worlds where water has been ported, but no soil yet.
--Martian Lavatube Culture (Same as Luna's, but on Mars, with different customs)

Illumirians (Creator: Black Earthers)

Illumirians were first created to settle the cold, icy world of Illumir, with temperatures akin to Antarctica. Since then, they've become the go-to species to colonize anything too cold for baseline humans.

-Illumirians
--Lantern Cultures (Veneration of light)
--Empire of Light (Illumirians became powerful enough to eventually form their own empire, and even bring the Terrans to notice them.)
---Starlight Culture (Empire of Light Remnants that eventually found and allied with the Void Dwellers and some Speckler peoples. Wants to bring back the Old Empire of Light Culture.)
--Twilightism (The most popular religion among the Illumirians)
--Anglerfish Culture (Illumirians who settled cold/frozen oceans.)
--Ice Settlers (Similar to specklers, but with more ice.)
---Shard Children (Similar to the Void Dwellers.)
---Dead Moon Society (Those who settle REALLY distant Oort cloud-equivalent planets. There are dozens in the Solar System alone.)
--Penrosers (Those who settled around black holes.)

Europans (Creator: Cathedralites)

Europans are aquatic transhumans sent to settle the icy moon of Europa. They now specialize for both deep oceans and sub-glacial oceans.

-Europans
--Seaweed Culture (Grew to be cooperative with the Tonope xenosophonts. Are humanity's go to to interpret Tonopean thoughts, though most of their expressions cannot be translated into human language.)
--Deepfire Culture (Users of deepfire, an exotic kind of combustion that functions at extremely high underwater pressures.)
---Abyssal Societies (Eventually they went so deep into the cores of their ocean worlds they lost contact with humanity.)
--The Great Schools (Supercolony/fish-school like instinctive phermonal markers that have created transplanetary empires with little/no communication. Divided into many.)
--Aquatic Diaspora (Europans sometimes live above surface in specialized body suits in non-Europan communities)
---Sea Merchants (Starfaring Europans who largely sell goods to other Europan worlds or sometimes other humans.)

Icarusians (Creators: Cathedralites)

Humans modified with wings, made to navigate atmospheres with oppressing, dense atmospheres. Have the ability to sleep in the air. Are close enough to human mythological angels that they're liked, though they hold little real power. Liked, because they're not a threat.

-Icarusians
--Avians (Bird-like)
---Heaven's Palace (Jovian space station, Icarusian cultural nexus. All near-human)
---Heaven's Periphery (Lots of smaller bubble-domes around Jupiter.)
----Celestials (Those who stayed more true to their human appearance)
----Neo-Avians (Those who leaned more into their bird-like appearance)
----The Diaspora ("Oh wow! A real angel! Can I take a photo?")
--Vampirian (Bat-like)
---The Cabal (Meritocratic organization trying to hijack high ranking governments.)
---The Undersociety (Broader Vampirian society, secretive.)
--Faerian (Insectoid Wings)
---Butterfly Culture (Expressive artistic.)
---Fairydust Culture (Faerian, but way more into psychedelics, experience, hedonism, and drugs.)

Tokians (Creators: Prophet Followers)

Tokians were created to deal with the high CO2 heavy atmospheres of the world of Tolkien. Made to be very strong and durable. Do a lot of dirty and frankly dangerous work, as they are seen as inherently polluted, and dirty. Typically seen as brutes, but are, like every human group, more complicated under the surface.

-Tokians (Humanoids with thick, scaly skin. Looks a bit like the Thing.)
--Smog Eaters (Subgroup specifically made to work in hellish factory worlds.)
---Smog Singers (A group trying to prove Tokians were more than just brutes. Intentionally live an ascetic life to produce beautiful music and art. Quite detached from normal life, so their songs end up being inwardly focused, out of touch, yet weirdly compelling.)
---Calligraphers (Tokian branch) (The Calligraphers have most of their transhuman members come from the Tokian group.)
--Gravity Hogs (AKA Hogs, made to do heavy labor in high gravity conditions. Ancestors to the later Gravity Men and Beasts.)
---Gravity Men (Made for heavy worlds, they eventually reverted to breathing oxygen, so we call them man.)
---Gravity Beasts (Almost exactly the same as gravity men, but because they still breath C02, we call them beasts.)
----Gravity Compact (The gravity people themselves had no time for human BS, they formed a partnership nation with equal representation between both.)
--Black Hole Culture (Those who settled very close in to black holes and neutron stars, surviving their dense gravitational pull when no one else could. Conflict with the Penrosers.)

The Other Transhumans:
The above 6 groups are known as the "Core 6", the largest and most numerous transhuman groups, created during the early days of the Stellar Exodus, and therefore became most widespread throughout the passage of time. However, they are not the only transhuman groups, as others have been created. As going through them all, just like with nations, or subcultures would take ages, instead they can be grouped into broad categories.

Temperants: Made to adopt to certain temperatures.
Void Humans: Made to adapt to the vacuum of space. This is a whole category in of itself, with countless adaptations. Void Dwellers of the Illumirians are sometimes included in this group.

Gravitants: Made for heavy gravity.

Grafthumans: A catchall to refer to when the Galov, or some other organization finds a planet with pre-existing life, and engineers a race of humans to "graft" onto the native ecosystem. These Transhumans are almost single-planet by design, though as humans do, they will try to spread and adapt where possible. These grafthumans tend to be anything from "90% human translated into another ecosystem's equivalent of DNA, because other ecosystems don't necessarily use DNA", or "50% human, 50% whatever we could find", or "pretty much 0% genetically human, except the brain and psychology, which is modelled after humans".

Atmospherants: A catchall to refer to when humans had them breathe different atmospheres.
-Methane-Breathers: Exactly what it sounds like.
-Hydrogen-Breathers: Also exactly what it sounds like.

Sun Suckers: (The 7th unofficial major Transhuman Group, they're separated from the Core 6 since they're not planetary-based. An arbitrary a distinction as can be, but since when has that stopped humanity?)
An absolutely crazy idea when people engineered people to both live in the void, have high heat tolerance, resilience to radiation, and obtain energy from photosynthesis. They like to create "sun-rafts" floating around stars. Sun-raft civilizations are known to clash with energy utility boards when someone finally decides to set up a Dyson Swarm around a star. There are different variants who each enjoy a different kind of star. There is an even crazier group who likes living around pulsars or gravitars. Humanity tends to leave these ones alone because they're crazy bastards even by THEIR standards.
They tend to be entirely separate from the dominant Galov mainstream society, both the 7 Great Tribes of Terra, and the 6 Transhuman Groups. They like forming their own sun-raft societies around stars, and they tend to run into conflict should Galov-aligned society wish to use a star as well. The most successful of these by far are the red dwarf sun suckers, who have an effectively infinite amount of stars to choose from, and a galaxy too apathetic to care about the 10 billion-th red dwarf star.
Sun Suckers tend to absorb light through photosynthesis cells on their stomach. If they ever integrate back into "mainstream" human society, the Galov sells hard light diets where you just add heat to release the light back into its photonic form. Comes in different colors and radiation types as well. Sun Suckers report it "tastes" (They don't really taste, but close enough) artificial and a bit flat, but it's fine enough.

The Diamondgrass Revolt

As was probably expected by this point, this level of suppression was not without resentment. A while (as in a few hundred years) after the conquests of the Great Khan was finally defeated at the Battle of Earth by a coalition of all of the 7 Houses of Terra, the transhuman groups rallied around a leader called Diamondgrass, a Lunarian princess and de-facto regent of a powerful world, and powerful psychic that successfully bridged the vast communication gaps between each of the transhuman species. And rallied them to force the galaxy to take them seriously, and demanding galaxy-wide equality before the law. Her campaign began falling apart as the heir came of age, and bickered with her over the direction of the war, leading to its eventual defeat. Though it was not all for naught, as the area around her kingdom effectively seceded from the rest of humanity, forming the Diamond Belt.

Diamond Belt

The Diamond Belt is a transhuman-majority region meant to act as one cohesive political bloc to advocate for transhuman equality, as well as serve as a "homeland" for diverse transhumans. Heavy terraforming and geo-engineering was required to fit all the new immigrants, resulting in a population density higher than anywhere but the Solar Region. It currently controls about 2% of the inhabitable volume of humanity. The Diamond Belt is still extremely reliant on the Diamondgrass Family for its cohesion, as the succession passes into its 4th, and now 5th generation, as they are the only group of psychics powerful enough to unify the transhumans. Some fear about the latest heir's relative lack of psychic ability has fueled fears of fragmentation.

The Diamond War

The fragile peace kept by the Diamondgrass family has splintered, with the tragic infertility of the Diamondgrass family being their ultimate downfall. Despite being pregnant 12 different times, the last member of the Diamondgrass family was unable to have a heir in time before their untimely death. Almost immediately, the realm became engulfed in a succession war over the strong and powerful empire, one of the strongest in the entire galaxy. (Humanity was splintered to such a degree that 2% of human space is enough to make you at least a top 5 great power) When one of them finally came out on top, they needed a way to unify the disparate peoples of the Diamond Belt, and the way they did it, much like in real history is to rally them against an outside people, being the 7 Tribes of Terra. This war lasted a while, but ended up in a massive tribal confederation pushing them back to Diamond space, but not wanting to risk having such a massive rebellious population on their hands, the tribes ended up putting one of the other contenders to the throne in charge, and left them alone.

The Gemstone Culture:

Though the Diamond Belt started out as a major alliance of transhuman groups at first, over time they created their own kind of status hierarchy. The colors of the gemstones were borrowed from the Terran's own classification of each transhuman group with a color. Lunarians were white, Martians were orange, Illumirians were black, Europans were blue, Icarusians were red, and the Tokians were yellow. The transhuman groups in the Diamond Belt eventually evolved into the Gemstone Culture, as the color distinctions used by Terrans was eventually adopted by the Diamond Belt itself, and the tiered society increasingly resembled a caste system. These gemstones ended up becoming a new group of people around the Diamond Belt, while still in touch with their transhuman brothers, were increasingly distinct.
As these identities hardened, entrenched interests/guilds/unions in all castes began pushing for the excluding of outsiders from their profession, wanting to avoid competition, entrenching these divisions further, a few generations after the Diamondgrass Rebellion. The stifling of innovation and calcification of these identities is probably why the Diamond Belt eventually lost its technological edge over the rest of the galaxy, though not entirely.

-Diamonds (Lunarians, Rulers and Psychics)
-Obsidians (Illumirians, Bureaucrats)
-Ambers (Martians, Soldiers and Warriors)
-Rubies (Icarusians, Priests)
-Sapphires (Europans, Merchants)
-Opals ("Other Transhumans", Somewhat outside the system)
-Citrines (Tokians, Manual Laborers)

Of most note, the Sun Suckers have largely opted out of the Diamond Belt, and are happy with their sun raft civilizations far away from Galov civilization.

Coming of Age Ceremonies:
While for many worlds and cultures, they live largely stationary, stable lives. In many others, especially in the more cosmopolitan or individualist ones, it is customary for young adults, normally around 15 to about 25 to engage in a period of exploration or adventuring as a coming of age ceremony. In Galovian documentation, it is officially termed "the Great Transition", or the liminal space between adolescence and adulthood. Though in various cultures, it is known as "Rumspringa", "Walkabout", "Vision Quest", and many, many other names.
The exact names and rituals differ by culture, but in general it works like this. A young youth leaves their local home, and goes out to the stars for some kind of quest in order to complete their transition from youth to adult. The purpose of these differ. For some, it is to trace the paths of their ancestors. For others, it is a way to allow a choice between their home culture, and the outside world. For some, it's just networking or information gathering, a hero's journey in order to gather the knowledge of the galaxy, and to bring it back to one's familiar home. Nearly all serve as a "test" of one's self sufficiency and honing of their abilities.
Some examples of rituals:
-"Slumming it out" on a limited budget. Sometimes fasting, in order to grow empathy for the poor. (Common in World Dreamer traditions.)
-To visit a world of all 7 Tribes, in order to open one's mind to possibilities.
-A pilgrimage to Earth, or at least one of the older worlds as a way to reconnect with the roots of humanity.
-Living among the ways of another culture. You can take this even further by living with a xenosophont, which will give you even more prestige back at home.
-Living with a religious institution as a part of growing up, to give back to the divine, and to connect with a higher power. Some end up becoming priests, nuns, or monks as a result. The religious institutions themselves support this.
-To go on some kind of dangerous adventure. To go exploring in an unknown space. This can either be planetary (exploring an uninhabited planet) or interplanetary (exploring empty space in a ship). In a sense, this is "space colonization training".
-To hone survival skills.
-To be deployed on a foreign mission as part of a regional militia. If you can become a Galactic Peacekeeper, that's seen with even more prestige on militaristic worlds, though the Peacekeepers aren't interested in taking anyone.
-To study at a prestigious institution.
-To develop a new skill, usually creative or innovative.
-Starting a business in a different environment, to teach self sufficiency and bootstraps.
Mix and match any of the above. Plenty of sedentary cultures do also have coming of age rituals, but they are more planet-bound, though they almost always usually feature the same ideas.

The Martian Jihad

One of the most destructive wars in human history, by the time of the great Martian Jihad, Mars was already a major hub for many cultures. Specifically the New American Republic, a major power of the Solar System covering about half the Martian surface, along with various Magnolian, Roman, and PMC influences. These were frequently named "New Americans", and will be referred to as such. Mars was very well politically connected, having the ear of half the mercenary groups in the entire galaxy.

The Dust Eaters did not care. They had gathered a jihad of magnitude not seen since the days of the Great Khan. They didn't have an army as large as that, but they didn't need to. They weren't here to wage war on humanity.

They were here to take back their home.

As a populated world, there was a degree of common courtesy, a kind of "international law of war" that forbade planetary bombardment, especially as Mars was ancient. To both the New Americans and the Old Martians, Mars was sacred. Neither of them would lay a finger on it if it could be helped. They wanted Mars intact. Unfortunately, it is hard to keep something undamaged in times of war.

Massive fleets began appearing in Mars orbit, as news rang out that the Solar System had become a site for battle. The Martians had rallied half their entire diaspora for this war. One great attack to take back their home, take back their holy land. The New Americans did not come unprepared, mercenaries were on their way, from every corner of the galaxy. Mars was an important hub for business, and was not a small world in terms of how many forces it could marshal. The New Americans had military experience, but the Martians had almost religious fanaticism, zeal, and numbers. The Martians had to fight a military. The New Americans had to fight an entire people group.

The New Americans tried to invoke the Pact of the Sons of Man, arguing it covered the entire Solar System, not just Earth, but everyone else was far more hesitant. This wasn't an existential matter. Mars was not Earth, the Martians were not here to destroy humanity. As such, most of humanity just watched from the sidelines, even the rest of the House of Star People largely remained muted on the plight of the New Americans, with the Mayflower culture's ambassador issuing "an official condolences".

A collossal pile of ships began piling up around Mars, the New American spacefleet blockaded Low Martian Orbit from below with the Martian Surface, and from above by its spacefleet. The Great Martian Siege had begun. There was now a huge spacefleet consisting of a massive Martian population trapped in orbit, running out of supplies, while the New American navy seemed content to starve them out. So close to their homeland, yet so far. Whenever a Martian starved to death in low Mars orbit, they would deorbit themselves and orbitally bombard the Martian surface with their space vessel, so at least in death their body could return to their holy land.

This sparked outrage all over the galaxy. News reached the Diamond Belt, where transhuman populations began to protest and decry what they called a mass starvation campaign. Images immediately went out of people in hollow containers running out of food, still staring longingly at the world below. It was declared a humanitarian catastrophe. On the other side, some of the deorbiting vessels were intentionally filled with explosives. One of these landed in Providence City, the capital of Mars, instantly killing 300 people. Causing the New Americans to radicalize and demand the galaxy bring them to justice, invoking the Pact of the Sons of Man. Several times the New American Navy ordered the besieged Martians to leave, several times they declined.

This is perhaps why the Martian struggle ended up winning the PR battle. The 7 Houses were largely neutral. The Diamond Belt was not.

The tactic used to end the war was a brutal one. With public opinion around the galaxy souring, and more and more pressure piling in from the outside, and the entire galaxy polarizing on this issue. The New Americans intentionally caused mass Kessler Syndrome to begin occurring around Low Martian Orbit, causing an extreme chain reaction that began destroying the Martian ships. After many, many months in a siege, these ships were low on fuel, and sometimes unable to evade the Kessler debris, even if they were trying to. This is without a doubt the most controversial moment of the entire war. But without a doubt, it worked, with the remnants of the Martian Jihad scattering.

It is estimated that 5-10% of the entire Martian Diaspora died during the siege. In the aftermath, the Kessler debris was eventually cleaned up, and Mars was reopened for business, but transhuman boycotts of Martian/New American businesses continue to this day.

Of note is the fact that the Ambers of the Diamond Belt were certainly the loudest among decrying the atrocity being perpetuated on their brotherly Martians, but suspiciously few went to fight for them, and they were already used to treating Martians as slightly "less-than". More likely than not, the Ambers only cared so much as it boosted their social standing.

Star Types and Civilization:

O and B Stars: These are used for two things. One is massive energy harvesting initiatives, the entire star is harvested for its light to produce hard light batteries. The second are "Maximalist Systems". Every time some hyper ambitious governor wants to create "the greatest system the world has ever seen", just pack it with as many orbital stations as a star can handle, and consume as much energy as it can handle, blue stars always had a seductive appeal. They would come in with possibly an entire galaxy sector's worth of settlers, purchase the star from the local energy utility board, and make a Matrioshka brain look quaint.

A and F types: These are known as "Bright Worlds". No habitable worlds are expected here. But they are targets for massive terraforming initiatives. If you want a custom planet sculpted here, or you want to build Eden, then you look here. Extra sunlight is always a nice plus, and so is extra energy. You just need the startup costs, so this kind of attracts the upper middle class of the galaxy. F types are preferred to A types, because everyone likes the yellow suns on a psychological level.

G and K types: "Gaia Worlds". These places actually have Earth like worlds, and on occasion the rare xenobiotic life world. Xenobiological zones are turned into stellar observatories, harvesting zones for orthogonal ideas. They're also the easiest to settle, (Especially if plants have already broken up the soil nice and well) and contain the bulk of the human population. And besides, everyone just psychologically prefers a yellow sun. Orange worlds are more likely to have xenobiological life, and contain more xenos, making them stigma'd somewhat as being a place for the lower class.

M types: There are so many of these that they're cheaper than dirt in cosmic terms. The Galactic Government just likes to hide all their secret projects on red dwarves. Because any orange dwarf or higher will attract attention, but barely anyone cares about red dwarves. Some are settled, but no one really likes living around one. There's practically no population density, no infrastructure, and humans just tend to skip over them during colonization. The main people who settle here do so for ideological reasons. The "Spiral Worlds", who believe humanity will ascend, think ultra long term, and want to get ready for the Heat Death of the Universe. Also people who want to get cryogenically frozen for TRILLIONS of years.

Autotranslators:
Invented in 22nd or 23rd century India, using psychic intent to translate one's words into another language, it was first created to accomodate India's vast multicultural society and variety of languages, but it eventually went global. Today, autotranslators are about as common as the spoon, and about as unremarkable.

Language:
The autotranslator created a revolution in language. English was the last time there was a lingua franca. The invention of the autotranslator removed most of the incentive to learn how to speak other languages other than the one you were familiar with. Many people still learned English, if only to make sure their business contracts were up to scratch, and as a sense of being "cultured", long after it lost its practical purpose. But in the centuries since the Great Abundance Collapse, the languages of old have been massively splintered.
Only a few universal languages remain. First is Celestial, or Mandarin, still the standardized language of the Celestial Kingdom, who restricted autotranslators to maintain their monolingual culture, much to the chagrin of many linguistic minorities living under the Celestial Kingdom. But the usage of this language is heavily regionalized.
Aside from that, the only universal languages are largely liturgical languages. Old Arabic, needed to read the original Quran remains in use in order to translate from the Quran, and has diverged from the countless dialects of "Neo-Arabic", whose branches have now reached into the thousands, and become increasingly less intelligable by the decade. Latin has emerged as the "cultured language" of the Christian sects, with the Roman Catholic Church now making official rulings on the Latin language. Greek, Sanskrit, and Hebrew have also been preserved for similar reasons.
From English, it has split into at least three branches, which in of themselves are vast language trees. Yanko, the language family of the Yankee-American descended branch, Magnolian, a more Southern branch which fused with AAVE, Anglo-Gothic, what the English and their descendents ended up speaking, and Anglish, a rough bridge tongue between Yanko and Anglo-Gothic. Each one of these trees have dialects, some of which are not mutually intelligable. The difference between Yanko and Anglo-Gothic at this point is comparable to the difference between English and Dutch. You will get some words, feel some familiarity, but be lost in actual meaning.
This is before we even consider the fact that the autotranslator has liberated language from strict meaning, and language has increasingly become something for the sake of artistic and personal expression, as the autotranslator only cares about your intent, not actual wording. Language has become increasingly musical in nature, created for audial beauty, not actual intelligibility, letting the autotranslator's intent filter do the heavy lifting. Languages where you don't speak words at all, and instead just try to sing as beautifully as possible, are known as "singer languages". There has been a language that one "speaks" solely by saying the word "tan" over and over again, and then letting the intent filter do the rest. The autotranslator can even translate sign language, and xeno languages. (Recall intent)
The main thing that stops the entire galaxy from just permanently devolving into this kind of linguistic madness is that the autotranslators have a limited battery life, which thankfully means one does have to worry about if they can communicate even after the battery runs out, and renders the "tan" language more of a party trick than serious endeavour.
Some ditch the audial component of language entirely, speaking entirely in thoughts. This is known as "Sylepathy" (From the word psychic and telepathy). The Galov is increasingly worried that humanity may be growing too dependent on the autotranslator, and has created its own language, "Standard" as a mandatory language for its government agents, drawn from a fusion of Latin, Anglish, and Greek, seeing overreliance on the autotranslator as potentially extremely dangerous as a single point of value.
Though everyday speech is generally fine, some cultural references, and subtle nuances still get lost. There's a standard monotone for when the autotranslator is trying to translate a concept that does not exist in your native language. And for important business contracts, the languages of choice are Anglish, Standard, Latin, Swingli (Standardized Neo-Swahili, for knowledge work), or Pancasian (Connected to line traders, more for trader/merchant work).

The Galactic Government (Galov)

The flag of the Galov is "The International Flag of Planet Earth", but with the Blue swapped for a dark pale purple. The 7 rings represent the 7 Tribes of Humanity. Humorously, it is said every single tribe claims its own tribe is the one in the center.

In an era where humanity is extremely divided by nationality and ethnic group, the one thing that can unify appears to be religion. And in this universe, there is actually a single entity that does claim the right of "Galactic Government", though their reign is very loose. Nations and worlds can and will defy the orders of the Galactic Government, and ultimately the Galactic Government can only pressure a world to do as they wish with military force.
The Galactic Government is a soft theocracy, but can demand very little of its subjects aside from occasional tax collections (Which are carried out with middling effectiveness.) and threatening them with military force. They're probably stronger than any one subtribe, but not the galaxy as a whole. For example, they could likely defeat any single member of the Prophet Follower subtribes, but are about the same level of strength as any one of the 7 tribes.
Unlike the Terran Tribes and Houses, the Galactic Government is unified enough to carry out big organizational tasks, and is probably the largest bureaucracy in the galaxy. The Galactic Government's main ideological purpose is to enforce the two iron laws. The law of human dignity, and the law of free will. Everything else, they are probably stretched too thin to do much for.

Their structure can be broken down between their 5 constituent faiths. Each faith has a symbolic capital, back on Earth which in theory they are linked to. In practice though, all 5 have vastly outgrown their symbolic capitals, and now have their true headquarters spanning entire planets.

The Moralintern (Ecumenical Christian Group, Strong influence over Star People)
-Symbolic Capital(s): Atlanta, Georgia. Port-au-Prince, Haiti.
-Actual Capital: Orthello, though their bureaucratic capital is Orthello's moon, Lithone.
Great Roman Catholic Church (Roman Catholic, Strong influence over Cathedralites)
-Symbolic Capital: Rome, Earth/Italy. (Also claims over Constantinople, Jerusalem. Less accepted than Rome.)
-Actual Capital: Petram. ("The Rock" in Latin.)
Faith of the Crescent (Strong influence over Prophet Followers, Weak influence over Sea People.)
-Symbolic Capital: Mecca and Medina, Arabia.
-Actual Capital: Al-A'la. ("The most highest" in Arabic.)
Faith of the Wheel (Some influence over the Sinocrats, Weak influence over Sea People.)
-Symbolic Capital: (None, various holy sites across Nepal and India.)
-Actual Capital: Shunya. ("The Great Void" in Sanskrit.)
Faith of the Om (Strong influence over the World Dreamers)
-Symbolic Capital: Delhi, India.
-Actual Capital: Akshara. ("The Imperishable" in Sanskrit.)

There's also the scientific and military wing of the Galactic Government, who regulates technology and makes new breakthroughs.
-Researcher Corps (For Research)
-Technician Corps (For Maintenance/Engineering)

-Galactic Peacekeepers (Galactic Military)
-Galactic Agency (Special Forces, Galov Agents)

Which are sometimes said to form the 5 + 2 constituent ideologies that make up the Galov. With the Researchers and Technician Corps sometimes representing secular empiricism, and the Peacekeepers and Galactic Agency being militarism.

The Galov has a set of allied worlds, either worlds their 5 Faiths own directly, or that of an aligned government. All allied worlds pay tithes and give soldiers. (Standardized for directly owned. Negotiated for aligned governments.) In return, they get first priority on protection from the Peacekeepers, and the Galov are decent enough governors and managers. Becoming an allied world is semi-permanent, filing a request to cease being an allied world is difficult, both because the Galov is already slow, and because the Galov has a vested interest making sure no one leaves.
Their military arm are known as the Galactic Peacekeepers, a coalition of forces marshalled from allied worlds directly owned by the 5 constituent faiths, as well as friendly/allied governments. The Galactic Peacekeepers are the largest military force in the galaxy, though spread incredibly thin.
To maintain an idea of what's going on, they normally have their peacekeepers or agents go on "surveys" of local worlds to check what they're up to. On top of on their allied worlds, they have people who can report up the chain. Basically a "hey, we're still alive, things are chill" or "invasion inbound, please send help". The whole military is built on an "immune system" type response. No permanent occupations, only interventions when required.

Estimated forces of the Galov:
10 million Galov Agents (Biblically accurate angel, or Star Fighter power level. A single agent is normally enough to hold down a typical planet. These are sent on special missions.)
3 quintillion Peacekeepers (Ordinary soldiers. Generally top quality for the galactic average soldier. Armed with cutting edge technology and technologically advanced gear, though generally treated as infantry. The difference between Peacekeeper and typical world infantry can be thought of as the difference between American and Iraqi infantry. On paper, about 80,000 per world. In practice, most of them are on bases. The vast majority of worlds only has a thousand at most, for ceremonial roles and for recruitment drives.)

The doctrine of the Peacekeepers can be thought of like this. They're not intended for long-term occupations, nor are they intended to hold down worlds. But are instead normally stationed at various galactic bases owned by either the Galov, its Unifaiths, or other friendly entities, and are deployed as needed.
100 is recognized as the "golden number" of the upper limit of people who can be reasonably managed by a higher up. The structure for reporting up the chain of command looks like this.
There are 3.55 billion human inhabited worlds. (The Galov has self admitted "blind spots" around places such as the Black Earther zones, the Celestial Kingdom and the Sinocrats, and finally places like the Diamond Belt. Leaving about 2.7 billion worlds.)
These are then split up into about 270 sectors, with extra attention given to the fringes, or spaces outside major allied powers. Each sector commands about 10 million worlds. Peacekeepers are allocated to these sectors based on historical stability of the sector. Some have as few as 100 million Peacekeepers as a kind of "skeleton crew", brought out just for morale boosting or recruitment. The Galov is already thinking ahead to add another layer to the tree of scale, by grouping these 270 sectors into 3 "megasectors". Clearly anticipating for the day they may have up to 100 megasectors, before they need to start making mega-megasectors.
Each sector is then split into about 100 subsectors, which manages about 100,000 worlds each. From here, you have the star cluster offices, which manages about 1,000 worlds each. And then the star system offices, which can oversee 10 worlds each. Even the star system offices are mini bureaucracies, with hundreds of employees reporting on what's going on. (Normally just by connecting to the local planetary intranet and scrolling on the news.) From here, any information about an ongoing crisis or genocide can be relayed up the chain of command, and the lowest ranking capable of dealing with the issue is dispatched.

Due to the extreme decentralized nature of both the Galov, but also the peacekeeper core, officers from the star system office level all the way up to the sector level can have different philosophies on how to deal with local issues, leading to wildly different governing philosophies. Generally, the Galactic Peacekeepers try to mitigate this with a standardized civic education curriculum, with the civic education schools scattered across the galaxy. But even then, different schools have begun becoming known for being centers of different ideologies.

There's also the Transcribers Union, whose goal is to manage to culturally translate the religious works of the Great 5 and standardize their beliefs across every language, biology, psychology, etc. One of their greatest jobs is to transcribe a human-centric, Earth-centric religion (For example, Christianity) to millions of potential xenosophonts, and every configuration of human and transhuman possible across the galaxy. Digging into the purpose of metaphors, and finding appropriate equivalances in other cultures.
Notably, even this structure has severe blindspots. They have only moderate influence over the Sinocrats, who act mostly independently, they have a weak primarily cultural hold over the Sea People, and absolutely zero leverage against the Black Earthers. All nations act autonomously, or even independently at times, and they only have the ability to influence the galaxy, not govern it. They have no sway over the Diamond Belt, which are their own separate power bloc.

How the Galov Works:
The Galov maintains a larger scale than any single empire. Due to the fact that instead of nationality, or administration, the Galov's authority is derived from religion. And religion, generally speaking scales up much better than administration or ethnicity. The largest empire outside of the Galov, built on a more traditional empire model is likely the Celestial Kingdom, which contains about 4% of the human population. In comparison, the Galov is estimated to have about 15% of the galaxy's military power. (Both due to higher quality forces, but also because the Galov is able to draw on a thin wedge of a much larger pie. As well as the fact that the majority of states need to spend on social programs, while the Galov is primarily focused on military matters.)
The Galov operates on three streams of revenue. Tithes, core worlds, and direct revenue. Through its affiliated "Unifaiths", it draws tithes from about 30-40% of the population. Though the Unifaiths keeps much of this tithing revenue for itself, giving about only 5-10% to the Galov. The Moralintern is perhaps the one who is the most generous, giving about 30-35%. (Largely betting on the fact that this is an investment which will pay off from outsized galactic influence.)
The Galov also maintains core worlds, both ones influenced indirectly by its Unifaiths, and owned directly by the Galov itself. For these worlds, they can more directly tax them, though in return these core worlds get more direct management by the Galov, first priority for security breaches, and a more direct opportunity to influence galactic politics. These core worlds also provide much needed tax revenue.
Finally, direct revenue largely comes from donations, but also taxes levied on their Unibrands, which are allowed to operate at scale with the Galov's blessing. (Lest they be broken up forcibly by the Peacekeepers, or a hefty court case.) The Galov's single advantage is scale, it alone can operate at the scales it is currently at, and locks the gate for anyone who wants to scale up to the galactic level. It has a monopoly on scale through religion, and as all 5 of the Unifaiths are part of its coalition, it is nigh impossible to build another Galov of its scale.
The Galov largely thrives as the vast majority of people don't see a reason to challenge its rule. It doesn't take much in taxes, nor is it coercive. The Galov intentionally limits itself to enforcing two rules among all (human dignity, free will), and only a few extra rules among its own affiliated organizations. (Merchants must provide safety nets, warriors must have honor, priests must have humility, bureaucrats must have sortition.) As most people don't have an issue with its core two tenants, most people follow along. Even should the 5 Unifaiths splinter, the Galov is loose enough as an organization that they don't feel constrained by its dictates.
The tax revenue ends up being about 2-3% of the galactic GDP. While staggeringly massive in absolute terms, this is tiny for any government. As a result, the Galov adopts a nearly minarchist form of government. For one, it provides absolutely no social programs. Social programs are the responsibility of the local worlds, and while they are sometimes managed by the Galov, sometimes doing monetary transfers from one planet to another, they are not paid by the Galov. Other social programs are provided for by the Unifaiths (which have their own religion-based social safety programs) or by the Unibrands. (Who, by mandate are required to provide social safety nets once they reach a certain scale.)
(For a quick realism check, if the US government stripped out all social programs, and only focused on military and federal administration, you'd also get about 2-3%.)
The primary things the Galov spends money on are administration and its military/law enforcement, serving as an almost minarchist theocracy. It also scales back hard on which laws it enforces. By narrowing its focus primarily to human dignity, and free will, it leaves the vast majority of law enforcement to the local worlds. And given that 95% of worlds will not try to violate human dignity and free will by default, this is already a 95% cut. The brunt of their military is focused on suppressing, and punishing the remaining 5% (or perhaps 1%) who do intentionally try to challenge the rule of the Galov.
As the Galov does not levy direct taxes on most worlds, leaves almost everyone largely autonomous, and genuinely won't get in your way unless you do a genocide or mind control, most worlds just don't see an obvious incentive to anger the Galov. Those who do pay taxes join voluntarily, and also get more oversight from the Galov.
The rest of their budget goes to administration, which largely just manages the logistics of the Peacekeepers and the agents. The current balance is about 30% goes towards bureaucratic administration, and 60% goes towards the military, though this also includes R&D, pensions, and military administration. The last 10% goes towards miscellaneous costs such as education (Only for internal, not external training), hosting the Galactic Olympics, and things like that.

The Galovian "Exit Clause":
The Galov requests that no planets issue death penalties except in enforcement of its two iron laws. But not trusting simply telling them to do it, they instead give an incentive. They request if a planet wishes to deport any "undesirables", they can contact the Galov, and the Galov will pick them up by the thousands, and in exchange, the Galov will send over some pocket change. (The rough equivalent to about a hundred dollars a person. Not nothing, but would almost certainly be offset by a human being's contributions in tax revenue. They're both making "report it to the Galov" the most profitable way of human disposal (so bureaucrats don't just mass murder people as the cheaper option) but also make the reward low enough that no one is deporting people unless their expected value, whether for moral or economic reasons is worth "only" getting a hundred dollars for it.)
The reason the Galov does this is because it's aware it is very loosely governing a lot of truly regressive backwards worlds, and wants to give an "escape hatch" for regressive planets to vent out their undesirables and potentially relocate unorthodox individuals who are being persecuted to a more stable, open minded environment. The Galov uses the euphemism of "processing" so it actually gets viewed by the regressive worlds as a punishment, when what the Galov does is more complex than that. While also being more transparent to progressive worlds on what they're actually doing.
Once the "undesirables" are gathered up, the Galov begins sorting them. Some of them are genuine undesirables, probably shipped off to the Pleasure Worlds or some kind of prison/processing facility. But others are just bright individuals who had the displeasure of being born in a regressive area. The Galov basically offers them to be relocated to a nearby planet of their choice, rehabilitating them, giving them relevant training, informing them that the Galov does not condone the treatment they received, only asking that they eventually pay back the relocation costs (Probably worth about a few months worth of labor), or sometimes they'll just offer to recruit them outright.
The point of the Galov is not to enforce their way of life on everyone else, they don't have a way of life, though the Moralintern's weirdly cosmopolitan humanism is the closest thing to a "moral core", alongside the two Iron Principles. This is more to make sure that people who were abused on one world are eventually handed over by monetary incentives, so the Galov can apologize on behalf of the entire human race, then give them a second chance on a world of their choice.
The Processing centers tend to be pluralistic worlds with a generally inoffensive culture, where the "processed" are given medical treatment, education, therapy whatever they need to make a decision on where they want to choose as their final destination. Though plenty stay on the processing worlds themselves, seeing it as a perfectly good choice, and sometimes even volunteering to help out the processed people after them.

Aspects of the Imago Dei:
The Imago Dei are the attributes of God that have been found around the cosmos. It can interchangibly refer to the fundamental rights of dignity given to all sophontic beings, the marking of God upon the human soul, or the likeness or image of God. This focuses on the last one, as many different traditional aspects of God have been found across the cosmos. Of note, aside from the Rationalitas Dei, all of the following attributes seem impossible to evolve, and impossible to achieve if one does not have them innately. One simply has them, or does not.

Rationalitas Dei (Rationality of God) - This is the baseline for the Imago Dei, those with a level of intelligence and rationality akin to that of a human being. In accordance to the doctrine of the Imago Dei, all entities with such a level of intelligence are cherished and beloved creations of God, that must be respected as such. The only reason to intervene, in the Galov's eyes is if they are threatening the dignity of another child of the Imago Dei, or if their existence is unusually cruel or violates free will. This is how the Galov justifies the forced augmentation of monohumans, they consider their existence a violation of dignity that must be amended.
The Galov has an exceptionally large list of entities they consider to be under the umbrella of the Rationalitas Dei, and are therefore bound to the standards of human dignity, or some kind of rough equivalent.
Entities protected under the Imago Dei:
-All Humans, and all Human-Derived/Emulating Entities. (Transhumans, Orhumans, Monohumans, Human Digital Copies, Terramachines.)
-Any Xenosophont with a sense of self preservation.
-Any digital or artificial being with true consciousness (measurable by presence of a soul/qualia) and self preservation.
Those without any sense of self, or self preservation are considered outside the Imago Dei. To degrade a member of the Imago Dei to a level below the Imago Dei (torture, de-evolution, lobotomization) is considered among the gravest of sins.
"All are beloved, all must be respected. They are children of God. We correct sin, *because* they are children of God."

Facultas Creandi (Ability of Creation) - Ability to create new things, to partake in creation as God does. Humans have this ability, as do human-built intelligent machines, that seem to inherit this ability through the Imago Hominis. Most of humanity's civilization-building, non xenoexotic cousins also have this ability. Notably, the Angels and the Demons do not, and this seems to be an ability mostly limited to the civilization building species.

Claves Creationis (Keys to Creation) - This is the ability to think and reason abstractly, to grasp rationality enough that one can re-engineer the rules of the universe. This allows for the formalization of science, mathematics, and the laws of physics. Though many of humanity's cousins are holders of the keys in some form, humanity's psychological makeup seems uniquely capable of intuiting the axioms, forming perfectly explanatory mathematical models. Many other species instead use very close approximations, or brute "trial and error" science as opposed to mathematical extrapolation.

Humanity possesses the Rationalitas, the Facultas, and Claves. But there are two more that have been discovered, that humanity does not possess.

Omniscience - Found in: Luciferians (Local), Lucifer (Universal). Defined as Hyperturing awareness, having the answer to any question not involving free will, or logical paradoxes. The Luciferians that predated Lucifer had the ability to gain omniscient knowledge by interaction, gaining total knowledge about any physical object. The fusion of the gestalt consciousness into Lucifer took this one step further, giving Lucifer total present knowledge. Lucifer also gained the ability to read minds, though not perfectly predict the future, or see what decision one would make. (which was unknown, due to free will.) Lucifer did not possess the Facultas, nor the Claves. As a result, he was reliant on another race, known as the "Constructors" to build anything. Lucifer could only copy or corrupt, never create.

Omnipresence - Found in: Angels. The Angels are enigmatic entities, not locally bound, and having the ability to manifest anywhere in the universe both in space, and time. Despite this, the Angels are largely observers, lacking the creative drive nor ambition to do anything with this power. Angels do not possess the Facultas, nor the Claves.
Note: While these entities are functionally immortal, destroying the body of an Angel in a specific location will prevent them from manifesting in that location again. The "field" their manifestations are disturbances of are anchored to local gravity wells, meaning that regardless of a planet's movement in space, destroying an angel's body at say, the White House will prevent them from manifesting again at the White House. More interestingly, you can force them to manifest with certain techniques.

There are two more theoretical aspects of God, that have not been found anywhere in the universe.

Omnibenevolence - It appears all races sin. An alternative explanation, proposed by some Darwinian philosophers suggests that capacity for love grows as one gets stronger. Love is only possible when you are in a strong, and secure enough position to love others without risking your own existence. And that no species has achieved the level of infinite power needed to become omnibenevolent. This power therefore seems to be the sole domain of God.

Omnipotence - God is alone in this. Though some suggest that those who have the Rationalitas, the Facultas, and Claves may begin to approach this as they advance. These thinkers tend to align with the Spiral Mandate thesis.

The Council of Cayenne:
The discovery of extraterrestrial life shocked the Christian world, leading to a scramble for a ecumenical consensus. What became a few isolated examples became a flood, as humanity came upon tens, and then hundreds of xenosophontic species. In light of this overwhelming discovery, the Christian churches convened for an ecumenical council for the first time in millennia, at the Council of Cayenne in the year 2671. Chosen for its symbolic location in the New World, but also its close proximity to the American Spaceport in now American Guiana.
The denominations that adopted the doctrine are known as "Cayennian Christians", and are the vast majority of Christian denominations. Including but not limited to the Roman Catholics, most Protestant Denominations, and most Orthodox Churches. Non-Cayennians are a fringe minority, mostly of human-exclusivist sects or other heterodox interpretations.
Their Findings:
1. To our dismay, the fallen state of the world is not only limited to Earth. We have observed the fallen state extends to the entire universe.
