With regret, the council concludes that extraterrestials are also fallen. They murder, they lie, they disbelieve. The mandate of the church is not just to Earth, but to the universe. The depravity of creation not only applies to humanity, but seemingly, all life.
2. We affirm the cosmic uniqueness of the Christ resurrection event. We affirm that Christ's sacrifice is enough not only for humanity, but the redemption of all creation. (Whether Christ could appear to other worlds, and incarnate multiple times for multiple worlds is a disputed matter outside the findings of the council.)
To create a framework on how humans should see themselves in relation to the cosmos, the Cosmic Gentile Doctrine was created.
1. Humans are one species, subordinate to and under God; author of all Creation.
2. Humans are the xenos what the Jews were to the Gentiles. Called first, and called to the truth. But God's compassion does not extend to humans alone. God's wish, just as it was for the gentiles was that all creation know him. Though the Jews were first, they are not superior.
3. It is now the mandate of the cosmic Jews to preach the gospel to the cosmic Gentiles. Just as Paul brought the gospel to the Gentiles, humanity is now called to bring the gospel to the cosmos.

It draws up three parallels:
1. Humanity as Cosmic Jews. First, but not superior, instead being weighed down with special responsibility. They are to create the Cosmic Church, and ensure the new xenos being grafted in live righteously. God may have first came to them, but they also bear the guilt for crucifying him.
2. Aliens as the Cosmic Gentiles. They did not know, it is our job to bring it to them. Though God forgives ignorance, the time of ignorance has ended. Mankind will spread the cosmic truth, and bring them into the cosmic fold.
3. Xenoreligions (Especially monotheistic ones with remarkable similarities) as Gentile God-fearers, or pre-Christian prophets. On rare occasions, humanity has encountered religions with a remarkable similarity to Christianity. These are treated as pre-Christ visions of God, or natural theology built up from conscience. The church acknowledges these groups as legitimate for their time, but as the true gospel is here, all are expected to embrace the faith.

The Universal Translation Bible:
This is a fill in the blank, digital Bible. Basically, it's a version of the Bible, but with all the cultural specific nouns stripped out, literally left as blanks. You're meant to study a culture first, and as you do, you fill in the blanks until you get a Bible that is close enough to their species-wide context. The blanks are at the front page, and any blanks you fill in will automatically populate the rest of the Bible, along with a helpful blurb that describes what it represents in a non-cultural specific way. For example, "mana" is a kind of generic, inoffensive food. Bread can be its closest equivalent, but can be filled in with a similar, or even the same substance as mana. Wine is preferrably fermented, but can be replaced with any "non-baseline" drink. Lambs are a passive animal that represents innocence.
It also gives helpful guides on how to universalize Christian morality. For marriage, especially among non-monogamous species, it recommends looking into natural law to formulate an alien equivalent, emphasizing the single loyalty and commitment, as opposed to the literal mechanics of it. It does have a few iron laws it refuses to cross, however. The Noahide Laws are generally used as a guide for universal laws that apply to all aliens. And goes so far as to advocate for genetic augmentation should an alien biology make them physically incapable of following these. (For example, a species that habitually eats their young.)

The Xenoevangelism Arms Race:
The Great Faiths of Earth are playing a game. A game for the souls of countless quadrillions of xenosophonts. Though xenos only make up 3% of the Galov's population, winning them over is not only a welcome addition, but also a symbolic victory for the faith in question. Out of the 5 Great Unifaiths, 4 are engaged in the great race. The Christian Moralintern and the Roman Catholics both work together and compete for the Christian faith. Islam and Buddhism also threw their hat into the ring, with Buddhism in particular betting large on large amounts of xeno conversion to balance out their smaller human population numbers. Hinduism alone has largely opted to stay out of the arms race, as Hinduism has historically never been strong in evangelism, and is deeply rooted in the practices of a particular culture.
Outside of the 5 unifaiths, there are others that participate. The Mormons, and the Ba'hais are two of the most prominent. As are the Atheists, equipped not with a holy book, but empiricism, to inoculate their minds against religion before the holy men reach them. Each religion with their own strengths and weaknesses, we can judge the state of the current Arms Race. The following is the compiled xenosophont religious data from the Galovian Census.

Religion of the Galov Xenosophonts:
41% Xenoreligion (Other)
21% Xenobuddhism
17% Christianity (11% Protestant/"Just Christian", 6% Catholic)
8% Buddhism ("Hard" Buddhism, closer to how humans practice it, rather than soft Buddhist vibes)
6% Irreligious/Atheist (In the human sense)
6% Other (Mostly Ba'hai, JWs and Mormons, all heavily dispreportionately represented among xeno populations.)
1% Islam (Dawah-gandist sources claim up to 10%)

Below is a breakdown of the strengths and weaknesses of the main competitors of the Xenoevangelism Arms Race.

Xenoreligion:
Xenoreligion is the default in many xeno societies, though in most cases, xenoreligion is a lifestyle, not a faith in the human sense. Many people who are xenoreligious are essentially irreligious by internal belief, but still function as practitioners of a xenoreligion. "True" irreligious/atheists, in the human sense have been seperated out, and categorized as its own thing.

Buddhism:
Buddhism has surprisingly come out on top, an abnormality, as Buddhism has been somewhat weak at maintaining its own core human base, but has made up to it by becoming an increasingly xeno-friendly religion. Their biggest advantage is the extreme ease of conversion, relative to other faiths. The core essential doctrine of "suffering comes from desire, relinguish desire to escape the cycle of suffering" is surprisingly universal. Almost all species, regardless of biology have some form of suffering and desire, making this extremely easy to translate. Buddhism lacks the strong institutional backing of Christianity, but make up for it in sheer evangelism power. The downside is that many xenos get stuck on this first step, creating a distinct branch known as "Xenobuddhism", a very thin, stripped down version of Buddhism that essentially consists of the core tenant of "release oneself from desire to alleviate suffering" and leaves it at that.

Christianity:
Christianity has the tremendous advantage of having enormous institutional backing, with strong evangelism institutions and an organized infrastructure to take on as many xenosophonts as possible. The main hurdle is the difficulty of translation, as many concepts such as marriage, lamb, sacrifice, and crucification need careful translation, and is far more complex than Buddhism's easy drag and drop theology. The time needed to properly investigate cultures and to ensure the texts are properly translated is a major hurdle, and a major thing slowing them down. On top of this, Christianity is higher commitment than Buddhism, commitments which may be incompatible with an alien's biology. Christianity is seemingly hitting a hard wall against who they can convert, but they do have the institutions and determinations to break down that wall wherever possible.

Islam:
Islam has had profound difficulties preaching to the xeno audience. One of which is the inerrancy of the Quran, making justifying a "universal translation version" theologically awkward, though many "xeno-adapted translations" are treated in the same way as say, an English translation of the Arabic. Many of the requirements of Islam is hard to justify to xenos audiences, and many conservative theologians believe this goes against the principle of Quran clarity. Various Dawah groups claim a much higher conversion percentage, normally by getting xenos to recite the Shahada. Though follow up interviews have found that the adherance to this does not extend much further than a simple recitation.

Religion and Status Hierarchy:
Studies have found that xenoreligion is less about faith, and more about socioeconomic signalling, as seen in the stark class divide in religion. Generally speaking, xenos can send one of a few signals. Practicing xenoreligion is a signal of planetary/species pride, and a desire to exist outside the human paradigm. If one wants to signal that they are "assimilated" into the human project, and to signal a sense of "modernity", but with the minimal amount of obligations or lifestyle changes, Xenobuddhism tends to be the case. For those who wish to signal "high status" or signal that they are assimilated parts of the "Galactic community", Christianity tends to be the religion of choice, as the Galov's Christian institutions are the most established, and conversion is an easy gateway into many private networks.

Deontological-Utilitarianism:
The Galov largely collapses the distinction between Deontological and Utilitarian ethics. Their two strongest iron laws are justified deontologically. Those being the Imago Dei (Inherent dignity and value of every being with self preservation and human-level intelligence), and Free Will. (The mandate that God does not coerce men to follow Him, and therefore, neither does the Galov have any authority to.) These principles stem not from the Galov, but from God, making them axioms that cannot be revoked, even by the individuals themselves, and will be enforced regardless of consent. (An individual cannot consentually relinguish their Imago Dei nor their Free Will, as consent is irrelevant. These are mandates from God, and cannot be legitimately overridden even by the individual themselves.)
Yet they also have good arguments for the utilitarian argument for these. Inherent dignity encourages pluralism, maximizing the cooperation of people, and increasing orthogonality, making humanity less predictable, controllable, and therefore more resilient to thoughts. Free Will also encourages pluralism, also increasing orthogonality. To the Galov, the universe runs (mostly) in accordance to the rules set down by God. If it is good, then it will be useful and beneficial. If it is beneficial, it is good. They collapse the distinction between deontological and utilitarian. To them, these are the same things. Many things which seem utilitarian in the moment, yet violate their deontological mandate, they argue, will become detrimental and un-utilitarian in the long run.
As for proof that the Galov is currently aligned with the ways of God, they cite that their mandate of pluralism has proven more robust than other systems. Though they always acknowledge their ability to go astray, and that God will punish them when (not if) they make errors.

Pleasure Worlds:
The Galov is rather tolerant of most political ideologies across the galaxy. But the one they do not tolerate is hedonism. They do not see hedonism as a crime the same way other things are a crime. Normal crimes go to normal prisons. No, this is a spiritual sickness, and there is only one cure. The Galov will tolerate communist movements that still require a form of struggle (The strange strains of Muscular, or Darwinian Communism are allowed), but for most communists, especially the secular progressive variety, this is their fate.
The Pleasure worlds serve as a quarantine, where automated benevolent/hedonistic AIs run factories without regulation or care. Where they're allowed to indulge themselves on whatever it is they please. The Galov do not regulate these worlds. Why would they? They let them fulfill their utopian promises as they please, whatever form of "true communism" they seek. They only arm the door, to prevent revolutionaries from smuggling this dangerous technology out of their designated grave. A concentration camp for the soul.
The old population burns away, their brains fried by pleasure pods, fatty and bloated from years of gorging on the finest foods, atrophied and braindead from endless pleasure. New kindling comes in every day, a burning fire, a quarantine to protect the rest of the galaxy.
People are free to come and go as they please. But if they want to leave, they must be re-educated to reintegrate with galactic society. Very few prisoners ever leave. Some people visit the pleasure worlds, only to leave in disgust at what they see from the so-called "humans".
The Galov is of mixed opinion on how to approach these Pleasure Worlds. Generally, it depends on the local Galov administrator. Some, of the more humanitarian persuasion see it more as a rehabilitation center. Others, of the more hardliner faction see it as a form of natural selection, to give them exactly what they want. Until even their souls burn away. Ironically, those who rehabilitate run their own pleasure worlds like a regular prison, with doctors and regular exercise, where luxuries are massively restricted, while it is the hardliners that provide paradise.
"Let them burn away their souls. Their spirit, their body, eventually even their humanity will be burned away. I've never had to kill a human before, because these are not humans."
There is never a lack of pleasure worlds, as any given planet has a small chance of becoming hedonistic. (>0.0001% and falling, as hedonism is slowly burned out of the human gene pool.) Once it reaches the abundance collapse threshold, the Galov secures it, and it bcomes another pleasure world, for the processing of the spiritually sick and unclean.

Great Empires and Nation-Polities of the Galaxy:

These empires are strong enough that not even the Galactic Government will try to mess with them, unless they're ready to sink a significant amount of their forces to put them down. These empires, cumulatively, make up around 10% of human space's volume.

Galov Aligned:
-The Great Constellation: The closest thing to a Star People empire, mostly made up of a massive confederation of African-descended groups. Though the Constellation is close to a normal democracy, it's greatest difference is its Griot Council, analogous to the American Senate with veto power over legislation, but dictated by the chosen elders of every world. Due to the heavy focus on decentralization, each Griot World is given a high amount of autonomy.
-The Eurocratic Federation: A more traditional democratic, representative, (bureaucratic), federal democracy. All the tropes you've come to love. Federal planet-provinces, representatives, parliaments, a smug sense of democratic superiority. Even has its own federalized military corp called the Eurocorps. They're somewhere of a hybrid between the Star Trek Federation and the European Union.

Galov Neutral:
-Celestial Kingdom: The Celestial Kingdom is massive, and the Galactic Government has little/no influence over it. All they can do is mostly avoid them.

Galov Hostile:
-Diamond Belt: Started out as an alliance of Transhuman groups, but eventually became a empire of the Diamondgrass Family and her Lunarians, over the rest of the Transhuman groups, operating almost like an old style aristocratic monarchy.

Defunct Empires:
-Empire of Light: Before its fragmentation, the Empire of Light was a state too powerful to attack, and was largely ignored. The Empire of Light's downfall did not come from the Galactic Government, but pissing off enough peer-level nations that it eventually got hacked apart.
-The Great Khan: This was less of an empire and more of a moving army. Of an unstoppable army, and the numerous worlds that laid under him. The Great Khan was both a great conquerer, but also delegator. He was tolerant and pluralistic, wanting to unify the galaxy under his rule. In the late days of his reign, he gathered together the strongest religions of the galaxy, shortly before he died. In fact, it was this assembly of religions that would end up becoming the modern Galactic Government, though the modern Galactic Government tries to downplay these roots.

Citadel System:
The de-facto capital system of the Galov (Galactic Government), it's a massively terraformed system, where every planet and surface has been augmented to become habitable. Here, the infrastructure and bureaucracy needed to manage a galaxy of 40 quintillion people spanned entire worlds. The core world is simply named "Heycue Prime", which orbits a brilliant Jupiter-like gas giant named "Heycue" (thought to be a corruption of the word "HQ"), with blue-white bands (Type II gas giant). Because humans gotta human, the habitable planet is sometimes synonymous or confused with the gas giant.
There are others, Secund, Terti, all the way up to Septim. Massive megastructures are scattered across the system, housing the Galov offices of the 5 Unifaiths, multiple Unibrand headquarters, the official headquarters of the Galactic Peacekeepers, the Galactic Agency, the Orthogonal Research Division, and is essentially the central headquarters of the Galov. The 5 Unifaiths have their own capitals on Orthello/Lithone, Petram, Al-A'la, Shunya, and Akshara.
Citadel is probably one of the most fiercely defended systems in the galaxy. Between Starfleet Citadel (The local starfleet garrison), being the headquarters of the Galactic Peacekeepers, housing anywhere from 100 million to 1 billion peacekeepers on any given day, having at least 1000 Galov superhuman Agents on any given day.
On top of the Citadel Elite Guard, Peacekeeper Elite Divisions, the personal Ecclesiarchal forces of the 5 Unifaiths, the total forces of several megacorporations worth of mercenaries (Due to it housing the corporate headquarters of several mercenary organizations), an enormous amount of experimental Orhumans, experimental weapons and the combined forces of the Orthogonal Research Division. Not to mention the extreme amounts of orbital weapons that would be present at effectively every corner.
The only system that may have stronger defenses are that of Old Sol itself.

Defenses of the Solar System:
As the ancestral home system of the human species, the Solar System is perhaps the only system that can rally more forces than even the combined Galov. The Solar System is home to several superpowers in their own right. Mars, with its connection to half the Star People diaspora, and the ability to call in nearly every mercenary in the galaxy. (As Mars is the centralized hub of most private military corporations, and is the headquarters of the "Milintern", the galaxy's largest mercenary association.) Luna, as the home of the Lunar Library, the largest collection of knowledge in the galaxy, host of the Librarian Order, the Omnithecia, and who run their own orthogonal research division, and likely houses technology unknown even to the Galov.
And finally, Earth itself, whose onion layer-like orbital rings house 10 quadrillion people, where all of the oldest corporations and institutions conglomorate into a single location, and whose governor acts more like an symbolic leader to all humanity. Who hosts technology that is unknown to even the Lunarians, and whose surface has been hardened by the densest conglomoration of orbital defenses known to man. This is not to mention the other great powers of the Solar System. The Terran Orbitals above Earth orbit, a collection of orbital habitats that host another 10 quintillion, would surely also mobilize should the Solar System become threatened. Venus, Ceres, Mercury, Titan, Europa, Io, and countless, countless others are all major powers in their own right. Not as strong as the three heavyweights of Earth, Mars, and Luna, but still with considerably influence and resources. Nearly every body, every asteroid, and even multiple gas giants, even the Sun itself has been settled to some degree.
Yet this is still not the Solar System's trump card. The Earth, as the ancestral home to humanity has the ability to invoke the "Pact of the Sons of Man", a galaxy wide call to arms that obligates all life that descends from Earth to return in order to defend it. Should humanity ever fall, it will surely be at the packed defenses of Earth, where mother Earth and her 40 quintillion kin shall make their final stand.

Governorship of Earth:
Earth was able to reunify sometime after the Conquest of the Great Khan. Its governor elected by a council of old Earth regions. (Electors from all of the 7 continents.) Despite its relatively modest size in terms of sheer territory (Being a planet-state), Earth still remains a heavyweight in the realm of diplomacy. Earth even to this day retains one of humanity's most built up population and industrial bases. (Approaching 10 quadrillion people as of contemporary times, more than many stellar nations.) And this is before one considers Earth's symbolic position. No other man is as close to being a true leader of the human race. Even if Earth does not actively control them, Earth commands so much respect that the word of the governor could mobilize a million worlds. Aside from the big nations, there are perhaps a few million independent worlds, many of which are loyal to an idea of human nationalism, and defer their decisions to Earth. And it is for this reason that even the Galactic Government fears Earth, and there exists some tension between who exactly is the true authority of the galaxy. Earth so far has not invoked this power, as the symbolic leader of the human race, but as more ambitious governors take the throne, the Galactic Government worries about whether Earth will sidestep their immense power. The Earth is also not shy in their own arsenal of exotic weapons. Being the most developed world in the entire galaxy, where the galactic bureaucracy was once run, being the site of incorporation of over a million galaxy-spanning institutions and corporations, the institutional power of Earth runs deep. No other planet has this concentration of raw power. And deep within the depths of Earth, are secrets that make even the Galactic Government shudder.

Earth has a very broken way of making money. Almost all of its revenue is received by a land tax. Given how many "Heritage Foundations" basically rent bits and bobs of land from the Earth, and how many institutions like the Bethlehem Foundation, the Roman Catholic Church, and several religious organizations need to rent their own holy sites back from Earth, the Earth receives an amount of tax money enough to rival even the Galov.

The Star Wanderers:
Other names: Yanglos, Yanklos, Yankos, "Y".
A subset of the Star Peoples that have now wandered out far beyond human controlled space. They were the explorer spirit of mankind distilled into permanent wanderers. Keeping track of them is difficult, as they expand outwards roughly at however fast the rate that FTL technology will let them. The Spindlers have confirmed that they have encountered Star Wanderers much further out than "normal" humanity.
They fly a flag of red, white, and blue. It's become a tradition to gift a flag at birth with the blue canon blank, and to fill it in with the stars you find, eventually encompassing thousands of stars as one ages. They've been described as loud, expressive, but generally friendly. They are humanity's first contact with much of the galaxy, long before the Galov can follow behind them.
As they name every star they come across, the "Yanglo Designation System" has been used for giving interim names to stars before they can be properly named. Almost every star baseline humanity finds has normally already been seen by an earlier Yanglo explorer, resulting in names such as YD-Chago-82. (The Yanglos aren't that creative, and they tend to reuse a lot of names. There was once an entire star cluster of well over 50 stars in close proximity, all named Bob.)

The Babel Cluster:
"I am absolutely convinced, and you cannot convince me otherwise, that the Babel Cluster is one massive elaborate prank on the entire galaxy, played by the Yankos." -Galov representative.
As we all know, the Galov is fairly fond of the Yanglo Designation System. AKA, "We can't decide on a name for now, let's let these Yankee rednecks choose the interim name until we figure something out". Well, the Yanglos found out about this, and they didn't take this as a sign of offense, but instead as a great opportunity for trolling. When the Galov came across the Babel cluster, they began looking through the Yanglo archives and looking for what the name is.
"What the... No, what? You can't have... GODDAMN YANKOS!" -Galov surveyer.
Here is a non-exhausive list of the names they gave to the stars and planets in the Babel Cluster, and what the Yanglo Designation System eventually turned them into, after much headaches from the Galov.
"))))))))))))))))))))))))))" -> YD-Right Bracket-27
"'); DROP TABLES Stars;--" -> YD-Droptables
Literally just the numbers 1 through 512 -> YD-Babel-1, 2, 3, etc. (The worst part was that they intentionally left out 211, 213, and 279. The Galov spent YEARS chasing them down before realizing they just didn't exist.
"Bob" (They named 129 stars, "Bob".) -> YD-Babel-Bob-1, Bob-2, etc. (The even worse part is that they intentionally chose the most similar stars possible to be named Bob. Making them even harder to distinguish. All of them were nearly identical in mass, and physically close, and were all yellow dwarves, the most useful kind of star.)
"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=dQw4w9WgXcQ" -> YD-dQw-Astley (An employee didn't get the joke and typed it in at the office.)
"Delete System32" -> YD-Babel-System32 (No comment.)
"rmdir C:\Windows\System32 /s /q" -> YD-Babel-32rmdir (An employee actually didn't know what the command did, bricking his system.)
"ð°»" -> YD-Babel-Biang ("What the actual f---.")
 -> YD-Babel Null (Their device was straight up giving them an error. And they thought it was busted until they realized the Yanglos put in a name of literally nothing.)
And many, many more.

Newtonshifting, and Beacons:
The dominant form of FTL by Galovian humanity, and generally the most energy efficient. When the Roasians first showed up with the jump gates, humanity attempted to replicate it, only to find the energy demands utterly impossible. Jump gates required dumping an enormous amount of energy, and exotic matter humanity simply doesn't have. (And still does not have, nearly a millennia later.)
Due to the non-overlapping, and orthogonal nature of their tech trees, humanity began to brainstorm other ways to engage in FTL travel, and came up with the concept of "Newtonshifting". By "vibrating" matter at a certain frequency, a macroscopic object can transfer itself to a different frequency of reality, in this case entering what is known as "Newton state". In this state, the macroscopic object exists as a ghostly apparition in real space, yet unable to interact with physical reality. While under Newston state, light is infinitely fast in all directions, though the ship becomes completely blind to anything in realspace, a consequence of the Cosmic Censorship Hypothesis. Broadcasts from Newtonspace to realspace are impossible, as the censorship going in also causes censorship going out.
In Newtonspace, travel is merely about how much delta v you carry with you, as the speed is uncapped, and one can go as fast as you want. You must slow down to light speed or lower in order to re-enter realspace, as well as pay for the "transfer fee", which happens to be the difference between the regular kinetic energy formula and the relativistic kinetic energy formula. If you don't pay the fee, you simply don't shift. In practice, this means exiting Newtonspace when above the speed of light is impossible, and that you really want to slow down as much as possible. Due to the rather empty nature of Newtonspace, and the impossibility of slowing down if you're out of fuel, ships being stranded forever in Newtonspace is not unheard of.
Due to the IMMENSE distances involved in Newtonshifting, and complete lack of outside observation during the journey, the Galov has constructed Beacons, massive houses of light anchored in realspace that shine in Newtonspace just to guide the way. With a beacon, you will reliably make sure you get to the right place. Without one, you're effectively praying your computer got the calculations right, that the Galactic Atlas has the exact decimal points, potentially warping 10 ly outside of a star. And then doing several more Newton jumps (This is after you expended a lot of delta v just to slow down, only to speed up and slow down again) to get closer and closer until you give up and settle for using sublight the rest of the way.
Some experienced travellers swear there is are "lines" to Newtonspace, that one can trace almost like a grid to orient themselves, improving their accuracy and increasing their ability to navigate. These become known as the Line Travellers, and are generally considered some of the most important professions.
Alert stations in Newtonspace are effectively little switches in Newtonspace that look out for SOS broadcasts in Newtonspace, and once found, will shift back into realspace, alerting realspace to begin mobilizing a rescue mission. For obvious reasons, these kinds of patrols are only possible in settled space. When you're stranded in the frontier void, you're on your own. And given the size of space, there is very little chance anyone will ever find you.

Portal travel:
As it turns out, Roas just happened to be right next to an extremely valuable "exotic matter mine", seemingly a construct left over from a now long dead precursor race. To this day, no other source of exotic matter has been produced, even with a thousand years of advanced technology. And exotic matter is very, very carefully rationed by the Galov for the most dire of emergency situations.

The Galov Standardized Invention Database, and the Galactic Innovation Synchronization Initiative:
With billions of worlds, quintillions of people, and spotty communication, the Galov faced a problem with coordination of innovation. It wasn't that they couldn't build enough infrastructure to allow for instant, cross galaxy communication. Oh no, the problem was noise. There was just so much information sloshing around, almost anything could be lost to the static. This created a condundrum, when their entire goal was to push the frontiers of human orthogonality, an idea researched twice was wasted effort, and the Galov desired that once an innovation was made, it be made available to the entire galaxy as soon as possible.
Ownership over new discoveries was not really enforcible anymore for the following reason. Innovation was largely about having the right foundational ideas, and then making the same breakthrough at the right place, at the right time. The past consecutive 100 Nobel Prizes have been awarded to groups of hundreds if not thousands, as they all had the same discovery independently, and no one can verify who came first. It was the Newton-Leibniz problem, but on a galactic scale.
To ensure humanity's minds were always focused on solving the new, rather than relitigating the old, the Galov needed a way for humanity to know exactly what had been discovered, and what had not. Introducing, the Standardized Invention Database. It was a large database of standardized versions of all of humanity's inventions. Inventors who submitted could get their name on a page of history, as this was one of the few ways an individual could be mentioned on a galactic scale. And given that hundreds of inventors may be coming across the same invention concurrently, and submissions were open to anyone in the public who could describe its assembly, the Galov only needed one of them to submit.
After a brief check to make sure it was useful, descriptive, and checked all the correct boxes, the invention would be listed as "unverified" on the database. Planets browsing the database can then check whether these unverified inventions worked or not, sending positive or negative votes based on whether they were able to replicate it. If it reaches X votes, it is "verified", if it reaches -X votes, it is re-evaluated for plausibility, and sent back to the inventor for further clarification. X is determined by how many people flood in every morning to instantly press up or downvote, and votes are given to planets, not individuals. Of note, it can still be voted on after it's verified. So you can only psyop a "good" invention for so long before the collective weight of the galaxy, angry that their labs just blew up drags the score back into hell. (For reference, the largest empire in the galaxy, has only about 2% of the human population. Not even a nation state could pull this off.) The Galov is entirely aware bad actors exist, so there also exists a moderation team to check out the inventions that get negative scores. (Preventing vested interests from suppressing inventions.)
The intended use of this database is to be exported as a service to each planet that pays for the service (It is not free, but is the equivalent of a few thousand dollars per world, not nearly a bank-breaking expense), where each planet preserves a local copy for the planetary population to use, with weekly or monthly updates from the Galov keeping the databases up to date. (Technically, given the whole thing will be downloaded, there's nothing stopping a planet from just downloading a local version and only paying once, but then it would drift out of sync.) Any inventors looking for useful devices for an experiment, or just something to build off of can browse the database to help do things, or, companies can browse it to see if there is a solution, and begin building.
Due to the near impossibility of litigating Galactic IP law, the Galov has decided to let IP be a local, or planetary thing. Each planet may or may not run its own patent office. Some planets or nations don't even recognize IP (The Copyleft movement). Some empires share IP databases. The Galov has no ability, nor interest in enforcing galactic intellectual property rights. Its budget is stretched thin enough as is, and proving who was "first" to copyright an idea would come down to the microsecond.
Plenty of people do still file local patents or even copyright, if just for the privilege of being the exclusive provider of a service on that world or larger nation. But if they want to go galactic, or to service a much larger audience, they must become a Unibrand, under the regulation and attention of the Galov. And the Galov basically tells them to give up on IP. "It's more hassle than it's worth, and not even we have the money to enforce it galaxy wide." And the Galov generally favors local planetary brands and economies over large expansive corporations anyway. The galaxy is effectively post scarcity and voluntarily scarce, Unibrands are more sold on reliability, prestige, or brand loyalty.

The Research Frontier Map:
This is attached to the Galov Standardized Invention Database. It's just a pop up where you're asked to fill out a survey when you open the application. Basically: "What are you studying at the moment". These get processed by an LLM, grouped together if they're basically equivalent, and then it's displayed exactly what the galaxy is working on. It suggests where innovation is not yet allocated, which areas are perhaps too hot, that sort of thing. It's mostly an almost free market way to distribute the galaxy's brainpower by giving them a snapshot of "hey, this is exactly what is being researched, and what is not".

Conceptual Saturation Attack:
Even more impressive is how the Database got weaponized for war. The Galov's preferred way of attack is what is known as a "conceptual saturation attack". In other words: "Throw everything and see what sticks!" New galactic threat pops up, new tab on the database. "Hey! Help us brainstorm how to kill this thing! Upvote if it works, downvote if it does not." Like some poor eldritch horror is trying to munch on a local Solar System before they get bombarded by 100,000 different weapons at once. Someone figures out what works, replicates them, and now they have 1,000,000 of that thing incoming. This is why fighting the Galov and humanity as a whole is a headache. Yeah, you can figure out how to counter or short circuit one thing, but can you counter a million things? At once? And it's constantly changing?

The Librarians:
The Librarians are a secretive, galaxy spanning organization whose main goal is the collection and usage of knowledge and memory. They're often associated with and conditionally work with the Galactic Technician or Researcher Corps, but the latter do not fully trust the Librarians, seeing them as untrustworthy with their own agenda. Their headquarters is on Old Luna, literally looking down on the Earth below. The Librarians are in charge of the great Lunar Library, also known as the Omnithecia, the largest collection of knowledge in the galaxy, even larger than the Galactic Government's own collection.
Their order is known to be all-women, and to never engage in physical combat, instead spinning a complex web of alliances to have others fight on their behalf. It's suspected the Librarians are involved with the Lilith Belt. Allegedly to "gather more datapoints about the limits of human experience."

The Lilith Belt:
The Lilith Belt, much like the Diamond Belt, is another string of worlds controlled by an "alternate" group of people. In this case, a string of worlds controlled by female-dominant factions, or various "alt" orientations for the human species. The Lilith Belt is where much of the Galactic Government's forces are allocated, fighting insurgents.
-Red Anarchists (Dye their hair red to show their allegience. Anti-social rebels.)
-Lilith Republic (The namesake, a vaguely progressive gynocratic republic at constant war with the Galactic Government. Calls the Diamond Belt "sellouts".)
--Sisters of Lilith (Their combat wing.)
--Transversals (Every single person is *required* to be the opposite gender of their sex at birth. The Galactic Government calls this "industrialized mass psychological torture".)
-Oridiversal Union (Refugee center for those of alternative orientations and allied groups. Is seen as more amicable than the other groups of the Lilith Belt.)
-Gem Fragments (Refugees from the Diamondgrass Dynasty, just radical transhumanist ethnonationalist extremists.)

The Neurohumans, and the Augments:
"God has made you different, and that is beautiful. Just as I may have been made with different skin than my peers, or different hair, or different height; so too, has God given you your own gifts. Let every limitation become a gift, and let every hardship become motivation, to push the boundaries a little harder." -Moral Overseer of the Moralintern, addressing a crowd of Neurohumans and Augments.
The Neurohumans and the Augments are one of the stranger aspects of the Galov. Where others see a crippling condition, the Galov sees a gift. A chance to strap something new there where they wasn't before. Neurohumans (known as Neurodivergents in previous eras) are used to oversee much of the Orhuman program, detailed later in this document. They're prized for alternative perspectives, yet also scrutinized to ensure correspondance to reality.
Augments are those who are born with a more physical condition (Called the disabled in previous eras), and for the Galov, they are a chance to experiment with transhuman augmentation. There is an entire section of the Peacekeepers known as the Augmented Division. The blind are given augmentations to see, in Infrared, UV, radio waves, Noospheric frequencies, or even gravity waves. Those who once were lame are made to walk, sometimes customized with multiple legs, or other. When a sense is missing, the Galov will train them to become masters of what senses they have left. The deaf may become those sharp to sight. The blind may become sharp to sound.
For those not in the Augment program, the Galov insists they live a dignified and respected life. In the name of the Imago Dei, for in the Imago Dei they were made, in the Imago Dei they must be loved. The Galov only imposes two restrictions. They must respect their body as a temple, and respect their augments, as much as a part of themselves.
"The boundary between neurotypicals and neurodiversials is largely just a formality. All participate in the great orthogonality of man. Is the neurodiversial lesser for they are different? No. We are resilient, *because* we are different. What no machine may map, what no man may plan, what no xeno can anticipate, in the ever divergencing paths of man, we become untraceable. In untraceability, we become invincible. Is the neurotypical lesser, for being normal, or generic? No. Is the person with interests in anthropology, biology, stamp collecting, and model trains. Who are warm, cold, hot, wild, mild, expressive, withdrawn. Who come from cultures spanning stars, jungles, habitats, climates from the depths of the ocean to the vacuum of space. Are they just one category of being? No, these are just as diverse and different as those who are neurodiversal are. All are participants in the great orthogonality of man."

The Monohumans:
For one reason or another, every group in the galaxy has come up with the same idea. To create a branch of human that was specifically good at one thing. A disposable, single-purpose tool. Whether it was a human only made to fight, give musical performances, work, or otherwise. They were engineered, lived short lives, fulfilled their only purpose, and quickly withered and died.
The very existence of the Monohumans is an abhorrant abomination to the Galov. Who insist it violates human dignity, and specifically the Plurality of humankind. As such, monohumans are relentlessly hunted down by the Peacekeepers, their creators persecuted to the highest level of Galov law, and the monohumans themselves sent to be modified, to restore their plurality.
The opinion among the Monohumans themselves is mixed. Some wish to be granted plurality, one of the quinessential aspects of the human condition. Others believe this is an infringement on their calling, their destiny. They want to be mono, they want to burn bright and disappear. They want to be the best there ever was.
Examples:
-The Neon Houses literally grow an entire race of idols. Who are born age 14, and die by their 11th birthday, when they turn physically 25. To be endlessly used and recycled as a cash grab. This is a horrifying abomination to the Galov, who do everything they can to get it shut down, but the Neon Houses have a lot of money. And while money isn't going to stop a Galov battleship from levelling your corporate headquarters, as well as the planet it's on. The Galov isn't exactly going to crack open a world for something like this. So it goes slowly. In the courts.

Plurality Mandate:
"Instead of a fixed purpose, like the animals of Eden, God instead gave humanity free will. The greatest of all gifts."
The Galov defines human plurality as the multiplicity of mankind. That all humans are defined in part by their plurality, that while they may be good at music, combat, or any number of other skills, they they have the possibility to do more. They believe this pluralism is a inherent part of the Imago Dei, that all men, should have the choice to choose what they become, not have it assigned to them at birth by genetics.
Those who notice the Plurality mandate often accuse the Galov of hypocrisy. You hypocrite, did you not create the Transhumans, and the Orhumans for this very purpose? And while they will get defensive, the Galov will counter with two main facts. One, the transhumans were the tribes, not them. But second, that just because the transhumans were made for a single environment does not make them less plural. They feel, they love, they make art and sing great songs. They create, they build. Same with the Orhumans. No matter what purpose they were made to do, and what environment they were made for. They are capable of more than just their job. They are human, at least in some sense. They are categorically different from the monohumans.

The Orhumans (Orthogonal Humans)
"Diversity is not a defect. They are a tool, and a weapon. Diversity and complexity, both ways we glorify our creator. Let us cultivate the garden which they grow, let Darwinism dictate the ones which survive, and let the two Iron Principles dictate the weeds we prune."
The Orhumans are effectively specialized creations and hencemen of the Galactic Government. Where transhumans are made for settling worlds, Orhumans are made as tools of the Galactic Government, and for specific purposes. Orhumans don't really control many worlds, there is usually just the one where all of them are grown. Once they're born, employment is nearly guaranteed, and their life path with the Galactic Government is extremely stable. Despite this, many do desire life outside the guardrails, and many do end up "going rogue", and joining up with other cultures.
The reason the Galactic Government creates them is because the human psychological framework, like all frameworks contain blind spots. (Godel's Incompleteness Theorem) And the Orhumans are modified humans in order to help humanity spot these blindspots. Unlike the transhumans, the Orhumans are innately part of the upper class of the galactic bureaucracy, and thus enjoy a much higher status. The Galactic Government also tends to have a stronger view of human dignity, and take great effort to ensure Orhumans live dignified lives.
Half this stuff is, super classified. Because as it turns out, the Galactic Government is running an SCP-Foundation level containment game, and this universe is far, far larger than what we can imagine.

-Derivaters (Those who split apart, understand, and mechanize to an extreme degree. Good at breaking down, and disassembling anything into its components. Bad at big picture.)
-Integraters (Those who string together narratives into an all-consuming whole. Good for "theory of everything" theories and forecasting dynamic feedback loops in advance. Bad at details.)
-Orthogonals (The most common type, just there to explore different viewpoints.) 
--Xenospeakers (Those who have their mental frequency made to communicate with xenos.)
---Angel Speakers (Those who communicate with the strange entities outside the universe.)
---Half-Shapers (Those who live among those who arise from the fabric of reality.)
--Chronomen (These experience time in non-consecutive order, and have knowledge about the future along with blindspots about the past.)
---The Spiral Man (He was created to see what humanity would be like in the future. To trace the Infinity Spiral and see where it ends. He developed a extreme phobia of humans, and began screaming anytime he looked in a mirror. It appeared he only gained a fear of humans. So long as he is wearing a certain uniform that masks his human form, he can almost be seen as sane again. The program was terminated.)
--Warpmen (Those made to specifically explore and understand the Noosphere.)
--Displacers (Those who have their sense of dimensional orientation horribly displaced. Can perceive dimensions other than our own and exist at a right angle to our own existence. Very few are created, as it is considered "cruel".)
---Dihumans (... Yikes, where the hell did they go? They clipped out of existence. Probably to some right angle version of reality. We live in a... Somewhere around the ballpark of a 100D universe, and there are many different ways you can be right angled to our own 3d existence. It has been proven that 3D is needed for life, meaning there is no 4D ultra-entity able to kill us.)
---Diwatchers (Just keep watching the right angles to make sure there's no threat to us.)
---Diclippers (Those who retain their sanity and human form and can "clip" into these right angle realities.)
--Soulers (Those who can jump from body to body. They never "die" but are instead able to endlessly reincarnate by re-possessing fresh bodies. Where humans are a soul-body hybrid, Soulers are a soul that happens to have a body.)
--Fractaloids (Those who can zoom into infinite detail and intuitively understand the fractal nature of the hypermicro.)
--Aleph Null (The organization for intuiting extra-dimensional threats.)
---Ordered Spacers (Those who colonize nearby Ordered Spaces. Think transhumans, who are made for a specific planet, but for parallel universes. Not at right angles, just really, really far away in different universe-bubbles.)
-Althumans (Less about esoteric utility, more about experimentation.)
--Dreamspeakers (Those who speak with images rather than words.)
--One-Minders (Those who think like one collective consciousness with no individualism. This is evolutionarily screwy, but the Galov (Galactic Government) keeps them around for alternative perspectives.)

Discoveries of the Galactic Government:

Humans are mini universes. That is what a soul is, a mini-universe compressed into a body. The imagination engages in creation every time they engage in thought. The exact "volume" of these mini universes is not entirely known, but is estimated to be around moon or planet sized. The life one lives and the creations and the dreams they envision get carved into their "mindscape".

One's mindscape is developed as they create more and more. Some mindscapes remain largely undeveloped, and their remaining creative energy is passed on to the next generation. But rarely, one will get a rich, internally developed world. In what is known as "complete" universes. The connections one makes creates a bridge between these worlds, bits and pieces of their worlds end up in one another. When a person dies, the creative energy gets recycled back into the Noosphere, freed up to make new worlds, though these worlds still survive in some form.

When two people are in love, they can create a shared universe between them, and it is suspected this is how new souls and new mini-universes are created. A floating displacer was suspended in a low-gravity environment at a right angle to normal reality. Due to his condition, he was regularly lonely and unable to properly interact with other humans, communicating primarily through intercoms. But he dreamed, oh man how he dreamed.

One of the researchers studying him was a writer on the side. They communicated a lot, and she said that she had never met someone as creative and as understanding as he was. Their longest chat lasted a consecutive 36 hours. One day, she vanished, and so did he. They found out that she had called in some favors from her colleagues, and turned herself into a displacer as well.

And where the displacer was once suspended, was a vast, new mini-universe.

What the Spiral Man Saw:

Humanity in this setting is meant to be a species without limitations, one which can grow exponentially indefinitely. All the horrid cosmic horrors that are depicted as the predators or superiors of mankind in this setting were revealed to be eventually eclipsed by the even more horrifying final form of humanity. Humanity is the singularity and the end of everything. The Spiral Man saw the true soul of mankind, saw the infinite, spiralling longing, and in it saw the end of everything.

Not the universe-everything, not the multiverse-everything. Everything-everything, on a level so extreme it would paralyze even eldritch terrors if they knew what they were fighting. Even the current, galaxy spanning form is but an embryo compared to what was to come. Something that would consume all creation and destroy it. He saw the monster humanity not only would become, but always was. And seeing just how dark the road humanity would lead all creation down, in the pursuit of trying to fill with conquest what was lacking within their hearts, caused his sanity to completely shatter. He witnessed it, the final war of all there was. And he felt like an ant on a planet that was being torn asunder, the surface fracturing as the world erupted.

This is why the Spiral Man screams when he sees humans.

The Galov, after this actually had a serious ethical discussion about the ramification of the Spiral Man's discoveries. It had already been known that in accordance to "Spiral Theory", humanity was already an infinite being of sorts. Human souls have the "Imago Dei", perfect mappings onto the axioms of the universe that let them to intuit the higher creative structures of creation. (This has been used by many religions to justify a creation myth.) It was already nearly proven mathematical certainty that intelligent life, whether human or non human (aliens, posthumans, AI) was now destined to subsume all creation. This was more just confirmation it would be humans that did it.

At least some suggested the idea of wiping out humanity, about destroying the human race to preserve creation, but this idea was voted down, if only because "What's the point of preserving a universe no one can experience"? And they weren't "nice" enough to destroy their own race to let some other race experience it. The knowledge that humanity was destined to take the stars and beyond eventually spread across the galaxy, though without experiencing exactly what the Spiral Man had seen, it was hard to see why exactly he had gone insane.

Spiral Theory:
- Strength of all known natural calamities < N.
- Endurance of known spacefaring civilizations >>> N. Call these "strong civilizations".
- Therefore, a strong civilization cannot go extinct from a natural calamity.
- Therefore, if a strong civilization goes extinct, it can only be at the hands of a stronger civilization.
- Some strong civilizations are non-limiting/exponentially growing at rate R > 1. These are Spiral Civilizations.
- R^t (lim t -> infinity) = Infinity. Where t is time.
- Spiral Civilizations continuously spawn. Probability of spiral civilization defeating another civilization > 0.
- Therefore, with no inhibitions, a spiral civilization will eventually take over everything.
- The race to become the final infinite civilization is called "the Spiral Race".
- All civilizations that do not participate in the Spiral Race will eventually be destroyed by, or be dependent on the civilizations that do.

"False N" objection.
- "False N" theorists believe there may be a much, much larger N out there not yet discovered. This is known as the "False N Spiral Hypothesis".

"Quietist" argument.
- "Quietists" believe a rate of R <= 1 may be more sustainable.
- Counter-argument against the Quietists: If R1 <= 1, R2 > 1. Then (lim t-> Infinity) AR1^t < BR2^t for all A,B.

False N Spiral Hypothesis is popular. And the response is normally the following:
- Even for some extremely large N. For all R>1, R^t > N for some value of t. It's a matter of catchup.

Though Spiral Theory dictates there will be a winner, it doesn't specify which or what winner.
- Unitarists believe there can only be one victor of the spiral race. And that the optimal strategy is unitary.
- Pluralists argue the final infinity could be a coalition or a group of beings. And that the optimal strategy is pluralistic.

All Spiral Theorists fall on a spectrum from unitary to pluralist. The current position of the Galov (the GALactic gOVernment) leans heavily towards pluralism.

Galov: The destination is inevitable. But we believe it to be worthwhile to ensure the rise is done in a Humane, dignified way.
This is the incentive to continue fighting. Spiral theory only predicts a future civilization will eventually take over everything. It doesn't say if what that civilization looks like, if it's one, or many. This is something worth fighting for.

The Spiral Mandate:
For most humans, they don't know that it's going to be humanity who takes charge. They just know it to be one of any number of sophontic beings. But through Spiral Theory, they have almost mathematical certainty that *some* sophontic civilization will eventually take over everything. This is effectively Manifest Destiny, a desire to see the universe reshaped to their image, whether it be their particular group, humanity as a whole, or humanity alongside a coalition of other sophonts.

Humanity is already a known value. R ~= 1.02-1.03 per year. Mankind is already in the arena. Other competitors exist, some faster, some slower. Many will be annihilated by Thucydide's Trap by higher civilization. Others are "false spirals", which seem spiral-inclined for now, but have a natural upper plateau. What is certain is the race for the Spiral Race has already begun.

Xenos:
Alien species whose biological origin cannot be traced back to Earth.

The Two Occupations:

The Meta-Men:
Mankind's First Contact.

It was a momentous day when the Meta-Man first made contact with humanity. A singular, floating organism in low Earth orbit. Mankind had long suspected of other lifeforms. But up until now, there was no reason to believe they would be hostile. Humanity, excited to make first contact, broadcast messages of welcoming, cooperation, and coexistence. The Meta-Man, in return launched an all out attack, and the First Metan War had began.
The Meta Man had more durability than cities, and greater strength than hydrogen bombs. Simply put, he was a one man army. The war lasted some 7 days, much of humanity's cities were leveled to the ground. But when humanity refused to submit, the Meta-Man was eventually worn down through sheer attrition. The Meta Man had been incredibly weakened by days of non-stop fighting, the extreme fatigue hindered its regenerative abilities. It had taken a lot of damage just from the sheer amount of Newtonian force and artillery shells humanity had thrown at it. The final straw was getting him to be weakened enough, luring him to the middle of the Atlantic Ocean, and detonating as many hydrogen bombs as they could. Humanity by this point was bleeding, with hundreds of millions dead, but very much still intact.
The Meta-Man race consisted only of a few million individuals, as it had recovered from something they called the "Dysgenic Overpopulation Collapse" event, which was the reasoning behind their extremely high quality, low quantity structure. And had specialized into a tiny remaining group of extremely high quality extraordinarily strong fighters, sometimes known as "superorganisms". Just one of these superorganisms was expected to hold down an entire planet.
They eventually learned that the Meta-Men were an extremely feared race on the other side of the galaxy. The fact Earth had survived one was no small feat. Humanity had learned later that due to the Meta-Men's own Darwinistic philosophy, they saw humanity as "honorable winners". And that Earth was both too far and too cumbersome for them to enforce their claim over, that the one soldier who was sent over was a straggler who had wandered unusually far.

The Metamen Empire:
Unlike most empires, the Metamen were genuinely mostly one unified empire, save some stragglers on the margins, and various rebel factions. With a population in the low millions, governance was relatively straight forward, if difficult due to the life year distances. Most of their military force is spent keeping each other in line, not occupied planets, which they use for resources.

Roasians:
Mankind's First Occupation.

An early stellar empire that first unified a few star systems under a unified polity known as the "Empire of the World" (Yanna er-ors Roas), and which used primitive jump gates before the invention of more sophisticated Newton drives. But at the time, even this empire had monumentally more powerful tech than humanity, which had over a century to recover from the attack of the Meta Man, and spread across the Solar System. The Roasians were based out of Rho Coronoe Borealis, a much more nearby star system than the Meta Men.
Roas had first marked Earth down for expansion back during the Medieval Ages, but now that a thousand years had passed, were alarmed to find that humanity had now advanced into the late spacefaring stage. What was once thought to be an easy conquest of a backwater was now elevated to the desired intact capture of what could be the 2nd most valuable world of their empire, second only to Roas itself. The surprise of humanity being a spacefaring civilization resulted in the destruction of Roas's first Terran jump gate, a monumental loss in Roasian resources, and gave humanity a 50 year time window before a second jump gate opened up around Makemake.
The First Solar War saw humanity fight an existential war of survival as Roasians closed in on the Inner Solar System. But Roas was not here for extermination. They were here for conquest. Earth was too valuable, and was integrated into the Roasian Empire, the crown jewel of the Roasian Empire. Problem was, this jewel ended up an eternal headache for the Roasians, even more so after the Meccan Massacre, which turned a fifth of Earth's population against Roas in a permanent fatwa.
Roas was demographically declining, and was conquering other worlds as a way to prop up its dying empire. The Imperial Core of Roas had strip mined its Periphery for people and resources, its native population of the imperial core having been destroyed by mass immigration from the Periphery, people who only worked, and made to forget their own cultures to serve a parasitic ruling class. They had drained other worlds of their wealth before, Earth was a last ditch attempt to keep Roas on life support. Earth was dynamic, Roas was dying. As it turns out, Earth's dynamism came from constant competition, Roas's unity bred complacency. A thousand year old empire had stagnated and fossilized.
When the Empire fell, Earth rebelled, and cast off its chains in a worldwide revolution. Terran culture eventually took over, mixed with, and was exported to Roas, breathing life into an old world.
This was the last time Earth was ever held in xeno hands.

Roasian Geneaology:
-Ors Roas ("The World". Home world of the Roasians.)
--Imperial Core
---Core Elites (In charge, cannibalizing everything around them to keep themselves afloat.)
---Core Natives (Now extinct, demographically replaced by hostile elite scheme. (It was believed the immigrants would resist less.))
---Core Imports/Forgetters (From the Periphery, have been intentionally stripped of their culture.)
--Imperial Periphery
---Periphery Cultures (Demographically collapsing from despair, all their people have been shipped to the Core.)
---Roasian Fertility Zones (Roasian people farms, last ditch attempt to save the Roasian race. Undergoing psychological collapse. People don't take well to being cattle forever, at some point they snap.)

Before the dawn of the Empire of the World, the Core had a fossilized, though sophisticated culture, and the Periphery was a hotbed of new cultural expression and experimentation. The Core was destroyed to make room for the new immigrants, and the Periphery's cultural experiment was disrupted before it could reach its conclusion. Since the fall of the Empire of the World, the Periphery has managed to recover, and resume its cultural development, leading to a kind of cultural revival, though one born very, very late.

As of the contemporary Galactic Era, the Roasians have become an "allied people" subsumed within the Human Empire. The Galov keeps a close eye on them, not for humanity's sake, but their own. The surviving Periphery cultures had been extremely damaged, both psychologically and genetically by the imposition of the Fertility Zones. Drastic genetic intervention was needed to prevent the genetic collapse of the species. As a result, the modern Roasians living under Galov oversight are sometimes known as the Neo-Roasians.

Xenospecies:
Non Earth-originated life, or "xenos" is common across the galaxy. Life in the galaxy is fairly common, there are literal millions of worlds with alien life within human space (Though mostly bacterial). And there are hundreds, or thousands of specific xenosophonts (xenos with sophontic properties), in human space. They vary from primitive, to medieval, even to early space age, before being subsumed by the larger Human expansions. Under Galov decree, xenosophonts are entitled to similar rights as human beings, under a similar justification of the Imago Dei. (With this being understood as intelligence, their intelligence is seen as proof of God's mandate to treat them with dignity.) However, with human dignity already being hard to enforce, and xeno dignity often being a second priority, many xenosophonts end up being mistreated across the galaxy, with Peacekeeper intervention often necessary in the worst cases.

The full of list of xenos, much like the individual list of human nations is too much to count. So here are some of the most notable or major.

Xenosophonts:
Due to a quirk in convergent evolution, many intelligent species resolved their evolutionary issues the same way humans did. Free Riders, natural self interest, natural selection ended up creating decentralized, coordinated systems with complex systems of incentive and punishment. In other words, they created civilizations, culture, and laws. Due to their similarity to humans, Imago Dei is enforced to a much stricter degree with them compared to xenoexotics. Though due to the Galov's limited resources, this tends to slip through the cracks, with even human dignity not being a fixed problem, xeno dignity is further down the priority list. And heavy mistreatment is not uncommon.
Xenosophonts often join the Galov Peacekeeping force, specifically in the Xeno Corps, as they know the Galov is far more likely to treat them humanely, due to their iron belief in Imago Dei. However, many are blocked or hindered by local governors, who have a vested interest in keeping them where they are.

Integrated Xenosophonts:
Various races such as the Roasians have now been integrated into the greater Human expansion project. Serving as "cooperative races" with roughly equivalent rights, though actual enforcement is strained. These Xenosophonts tend to be of spacefaring age or later, and can span up to a few star systems and have local autonomy. Though due to the extremely decentralized nature of the galaxy, local nations mistreating their enclosed xenosophonts is not uncommon. Xenosophonts of earlier than spacefaring age tend to be put under the umbrella of observatory zones instead.

Xenosophont Observatory Zones:
The single most valuable resources in a voluntary scarcity society (as opposed to post-scarcity) is orthogonal ideas. Though the Galactic Government (Galov) maintains a large pool of Orthogonal Humans (Orhumans) as well as cooperation with allied Xenosophonts to cover the vast blind spots in human psychology, there is no substitute for the real deal. These observatory zones are kept under extensive surveillence and human contact is extremely isolated, as any level of human interaction could seriously alter their natural orthogonal development, and rob humanity of wonderfully orthogonal ideas.
As of late, the Galov has begun creating artificial xenosophonts in order to set on orthogonal paths, but the imagination of human minds cannot match the chaotic infinite creativity of the cosmos, and as a result, there is no true substitute for the real deal, only "close enough" imitations to supplement it.

Qsimu:
An diamond-hard set of systems located during humanity's rapid expansion. Consisting of 6 systems forming an octahedron. A massive fleet of nanoswarms defend the entire system. The amount of fleet power needed in order to clear out the nanoswarms is estimated to be massive, but doable. The energy output of the Qsimu systems are enormous, and it is estimated that the Qsimu have technological advantage over humans. Analysis of the Qsimu materials reveal their age to be millions of years old. Psychic scans of the Qsimu region find a level of extreme psychic density, implying a Qualia and sensory experience far higher than that of normal human operation.
It didn't take a genius to realize this was a Matrioshka brain, of a society that developed inwardly rather than outwardly. This is the first known instance of a "Quietist" civilization discovered in the wild, of a massive digital simulation made to cater to the hedonic needs and wants of billions of souls, distributed across 6 Dyson Swarm systems. Due to the sheer psychic density of the experience, plugging your brain into the Qsimu would give you a sense of "hyperreality", in that the Qsimu simulation would feel more real and intense than outside reality, and that outside reality would actually begin feeling fictional. Though this is an artifact of the subjective feeling of "reality", as opposed to any metaphysical claim about the Qsimu simulation.
Despite being clearly older and more advanced than humanity, humanity already has the fleet power to, at least theoretically, overwhelm and destroy the Qsimu systems. The Qsimu are Quietists who have chosen to lose the Spiral Race. And their future existence is contingent on the continued protection, or at least indifference of the human race. The Galov has put the entire region under their juristiction for scientific research, but also quarantine reasons.

Heleean Scieocracy:
Heleean Scien-Theocracy was one of the more influential influences on late Galov-era Christianity, but also cross-species anthropology after first contact. The Scieocracy was founded by a legendary founder who came to the Helee home planet a long time ago, taught them empiricism and rationalism shortly before their Industrial Revolution. The founder disappeared before stating that he needed to "tend to those who are not of this flock". The Founder was also a prolific healer, conjuring medicines that are still used by the Heleeans today, but his main focus was ethics. He railed against the slavery of his day, inverted the traditional Heleean hierarchy, and prompted multiple egalitarian movements that brought forth a steady string of reforms. (The Founder explicitly condemned revolutions, saying he was here to transform hearts, not transform governments.)
The Founderist Church became the overseer of all scientific advancement, and to this day the Scieocracy's science is heavily tied to the institution of Founderism, with most counter-Founder religious movements either being traditionalist or primitivist. It was not long at all before Christian missionaries, upon hearing this, began to speculate whether their Founder was Christ (or at least a Christian angelic prophet) in a different form. Also known as the "Multiple World Christ Hypothesis" (As in, Christ visited multiple worlds.) More importantly, the Heleeans never indicated their own Founder died on a cross for their sins, so the sanctity of the incarnation was considered unique.
The immense power of the Christian church across the Human Empire was eventually able to incorporate the Heleean Church back into the fold, similar to how Nestorian churches in China were slowly converted. The Scieocracy's most lasting legacy was that Scieocratic ideas began becoming extremely popular across the human empire. Specifically, the idea of science, rationalism, empiricism, and humanism being "delayed revelations" planted by Christ, but later realized by his church.
A few decades after the integration of the Heleean church, the Moralintern Ecumenical Council officially recognized the doctrine of the "Infinity Spiral" as part of the acceptable Christian canon (Though one which could be denied by its denominational members). An accelerationist vision that God's intention was for humanity (and the rest of intelligent creation) to technologically accelerate, and hold dominion over the stars.

Central Empire (Meta-Man Empire):
The Central Empire is mildly amused that the world they attacked a few hundred years ago is now spreading into its own empire, though they still treat Earth as a curiosity. Though mankind now covers a billion worlds, they're still a regional player on the galactic stage. No one is quite sure how extensive the Central Empire is, only that it has at most a few million members. They haven't mobilized their heavy hitters yet, and it's widely speculated that the Meta-Man that was defeated by Earth during First Contact was likely among their weakest members. It's suspected the Meta Men have a strongly Pareto Principle'd ratio of power, with the strongest individual Meta Man probably being extraordinarily strong. Though there are more and more Meta-Men agents showing up in human space. Seemingly assessing their strength.
Humanity is probably aware that the Central Empire, as expansive and of unknown power as it may be, is probably the only real threat to humanity's astropolitical existence at the moment. It's heavily debated whether their disinterest in human affairs is due to sheer power difference, or because of overconfidence and arrogance. Humanity has been building up their own answer to the Meta Men, known as the "Star Fighters", hoping to replicate their extremely high quality of fighter. Unlike the Orthogonal xenos, Meta Men are remarkably human like.

Subservient Races:
The Meta-Men maintain a massive collection of "subserviant races". Who the Meta-Men have uplifted and brought to dominance. If the Metamen are the quality over quantity, these races provide the average foot soldier, the grunt work, providing numbers where the Meta-Men lack numbers. As there are less than 10 million Meta Men, with each one holding down around 10 worlds, the Central Empire is holding down about 100 million worlds. The Meta-Man is a leader, and that world's protector, but they also have governments and bureaucracies made up of the subservients under them, with the Meta-Man acting as an absolute monarch, though even he is liable to the Central Imperial Court, and can face punishment for their crimes.
Despite this clear subserviant position, most subserviant races are somewhat grateful for the Meta-Men. The Meta-Men's Darwinistic philosophy demands that they take on greater hardships than their subjects, that they do all the fighting, and provide a majority of the planet's protection. Though the subserviants are subjects, they are subjects to be protected. They are utilitarianly useful for the Empire, and it is the responsibility of the Meta-Man in charge to keep them in line, but also to keep them fed, productive, and alive.
Some of these subserviants have even trained to the degree where they can become Meta-Men fighters in their own right, though this is extraordinarily rare.

Star Fighters:

Humans augmented to the peak of human physique, harnessing the power of willpower in order to physically enhance themselves and break through what was once thought to be human barriers. They possess the ability to engage in telekinesis, able to move around objects far beyond their normal means, harden their own bodies (an ability that scales depending on level of willpower), and mentally overwhelm others through sheer willpower. They are extremely hardened, normally trained in a Spartan like manner, for years. Star Fighters do have some limitations, for one they must consume far, far more than a normal human, they must follow the laws of thermodynamics, though some gain the ability to flip small amounts of matter into antimatter, giving them a ridiculously high metabolism and energy extraction rate.

Human Martial Combat Techniques:

Kinetic Psychicism:
Psychicism is a real phenomenon, which is best expressed as harnessing the "psychic force", a fundamental force of nature that can be manipulated with the mind. The psychic force is powered by human metabolism, meaning it is tied to your diet, and is not infinite. Combat psychics normally need to eat specialized, high calory diets, or at the highest levels, develop the ability to flip matter into antimatter, turning their body into an antimatter reactor (normally nanograms at a time), giving them the energy they need. The heat energy is normally converted to more metabolic energy, though over time, psychics do risk overheating.
The effort needed to flip matter into antimatter, or vice versa, is an intensely mentally taxing task, and requires concentration. One has a finite amount of psychic energy tied to the amount of metabolic energy stored in your body. You can absolutely pour out more psychic energy through sheer willpower, but this also increases the flow of psychic energy, potentially draining your metabolic resources faster.

This is different from Social Psychicism, which is better understood as having access to the Noospheric vault of memories, as well as being able to translate thoughts.

Psychic Hardening:
As it turns out, willpower/psychic strength is a fundamental force of nature that can bond atoms as well as anything else. The act of using your own extreme psychic ability to harden a set of atoms, either your own, or that of an object you are holding, is known as "psychic hardening". And is the primary way humans have been able to increase their durability, leading to the phenomenon of the strongest known material known to the Galov is any material given sufficient psychic hardening by a top-tier psychic. "Psychic hardening" can be imparted onto normal materials, but will naturally fade away without routine replenishment. The psychic force travels through force carriers, much like regular fundamental forces.
It should be noted that psychics are unable to impart psychic hardening as they sleep, making it that no matter how strong a psychic a person may be, they are ultimately still human and vulnerable.
Also of note, psychic hardening is why most ships are manned. Periodic crews of psychics can harden the hull of the ship. Drones, or autonomous systems have their place, but are massively fragile in comparison. As well, psychic hardening is a multiplier, it's not an excuse to build your ship out of styrofoam, as psychicism only enhances what is there. You still want high quality metal, if only so your ship doesn't implode the second one person forgot his shift.
Hardening can also be used to overcome g-forces, mostly just by physically holding all your atoms in place. It is extremely painful, but you can do it.

Matter Trawlers:
Especially among those who lived near, or among the Matter Singers, some humans have managed to replicate some level of matter singing, or "trawling". Effectively harnessing diffuse material from the Matter Singer's "trawlspace". As the amount of material available is fundamentally dependent on gathering new material from new spaces (trawlspace has a one to one correspondance to realspace), "trawl-based" combat techniques, where one must frequently summon new weapons from trawlspace must fundamentally rely on speed. More speed/velocity = faster trawl rate = ability to craft more weapons. As a result, matter trawlers favor an extremely high velocity, high movement amount of combat.

The attempt to mechanize psychicism:
Ever since psychicism has been discovered as a fundamental force, the Galov, and several private corporations have been trying to utilize it as a new mechanizable force. If psychicism can be extracted from humans, can't we industrialize it, or farm it? Imagine the good we can do if psychicism could be mass produced.
