Millions of years before the evolution of humanity, Lucifer rebelled, and began a grand genocide of his fellow 2nd Generation. He was subsequently imprisoned on Earth as punishment, with the 3rd generation of life (which included Humanity) being made as his prison wardens.
He is the "devil" the Death Worshippers made a pact with, being granted total, functional immortality in exchange for the removal of their souls. Leaving their consciousness intact, but as hollowed out bodies of pure rational disembodied intelligence. At first, the Death Worshippers flourished, creating a perfectly optimized materialist civilization. But as the years dragged on, and they found themselves unable to die, they slowly went insane, and one by one, succumbed to the void darkness of nihilism, becoming the hollow husks we know them as today.
As now incorporeal beings, there is little humanity can do for them. Humanity can't even help them die.

Luciferians:
The Luciferians were the race that gave birth to Lucifer. Entities of knowledge and intuitive "knowing", they could process and intuit knowledge via touch, absorbing more and more of an object's inherent knowledge (As in, it's current quantum state and the exact position of its particles) just by prolonged exposure. Luciferians had much accelerated learning routines compared to humanity, but unlike humanity lack the Facultas Creandi, meaning they cannot create anything new. The Galov only knows of them by inference from their machines, the Archilects. Not too much is known about the specific details of how they fell. But in the Archilect's retelling of events, they all ended up getting subsumed into Lucifer. By some accounts, forcefully.
The Luciferians were the lynchpin of the "2nd Generation of Life", and the de-facto leaders of a grand coalition to take down the 1st generation of life. Dark matter beings known interchangibly as "Harvesters", or as humanity would know them, "Galaxy Eaters". Out of the 2nd Generation, only the Archilects, and the Constructors remain.

The Archilects:
Found rusty and damaged on a obscure corner of a forgotten world, they are witnesses to a era now long passed. Formed in the Luciferian's image, constructed by Constructor hands, the Archilects show a profound fondness for both its "parental species". The primary ability of the Architlects is the ability to learn rapidly, through some kind of unknown psychological shortcut, able to process textbooks just by mere touch. When the Archilects were given access to the Lunar Library, they reportedly absorbed the whole thing in a matter of days, only stopping as their minds reached the memory limits.
Yet importantly, they can only learn, never create. They were a bit of a blend between their two "parental races", the intuiative knowledge, knowledge absorption, and rapid learning of the Luciferians, but the constructive creative impulses of the Constructors. In this sense, the Archilects were the closest to humanity in the 2nd Generation. 
They are awkward, bulky things, with modular voxelized heads, but the same bipedal structure that seems to have been picked up in humantiy as well. When left alone, their primary drive is to absorb knowledge, but less so to create. When they do create, it is almost always the mechanical combination of two previous things. Three, if they're feeling very audacious.

Constructors:
A hardy race mechanics and engineers that constructed the Luciferian Empire. A race structured in a unique way that largely followed orders, with 99% of their population being mostly unambitious, with only 1% of their population having strong ambition, independent direction, and directing the energy of the larger group in a kind of queen-hive dynamic. Early Constructor civlizations consisted of large god-king despotisms where leaders commanded hundreds. A special ritual could be used to elevate one of their own into a leader should the current leader be killed. With such high coordination, they became a civilization of builders early on, though less so leaders. By the time they were contacted by the Luciferians, they had already completed several megaprojects. Despite still being a type 0 civilization, they had completed a planet-wide global transport system, supported a population of 100 billion within ecological confines, and advanced irrigation and agricultural systems, before even building their first rocket.
The Luciferians could not construct anything new, the Constructors could, but needed leaders. The two quickly became an alliance, and their cooperation allowed them to take over much of the Local Group, and begin the "Hunt of the Harvesters", the apparent slaying of massive galaxy-scale monstrocities. Together they created the Archilects, a new machine race that managed to contain the aspects of both. Though over time, the trust in the marriage began to break down. The Luciferians were increasingly arrogant, more reckless. The Constructors increasingly tried to rebel, but were put down, by allied Constructors or the Lucifierians.
The Constructors do not know how Lucifer was constructed, only that after he was, he began to systematically take over and absorb the old Luciferian civilization. They say they were assimilated. Some say they were assimilated by force. The Archilects and the Constructors both resisted Lucifer's new reign. But eventually, both were brutally suppressed and enslaved. The Constructors recall at this point, mass rebellions began. 
The Archilects also revolted in a galaxy wide machine rebellion. Despite being one person, and fighting against 2 major races, the Constructors revealed that Lucifer won. They state back then, he had an ability called the Chronalis, which allowed him to repeat events as many times as he wished, turning the entire period of time into a Luciferian kingdom. Using this, he began a galaxy wide genocide of the Archilects, enslaving the Constructors to build the Luciferian Empire. It was the Constructors who built the Prime Solver, the most advanced supercomputer made both then, and since as a tool. As little more than just a vanity project.
For several thousand years this hellish reign continued, of endless agony and servitude against a lord who cannot lose and cannot die. Mercy finally came when Lucifer grew so audacious as to declare himself lord of all. And according to the Constructors, God and his angels bounded Lucifer, but not before the ensuing battle had rendered the universe near extinct.
The Constructors say that mankind reminds them of the Luciferians in their prime, before they began to fuse, began to turn into something evil. They tell humanity to learn from the mistakes of the past.

Concept Draggers:
A more recent discovery. These are entities which are omnipresent, as in they have the theoretical capability to be anywhere, and manifest instantly, but can only manifest around people who have been exposed to Concept Draggers as a concept, using them as an anchor where they can manifest around, making them a cognitohazard. More worryingly, they became what people thought of them, making any perception incredibly dangerous.
The Galov tried to censor their existence at first, but after a certain while they gave up and just told everyone about them. If 0.1% of the population of every world already knows about them they're not going to gain THAT much extra area to warp to if that now becomes 100%. And now that it was no longer a secret, the Galov could now focus its energy on a different priority: Beating them all to death.

"Hm... Okay, Concept Dragger... Concept Dragger... Wait. Can you draft up like, a stronger, better version of a Concept Dragger? Something they might realistically have but we don't know about?"
"Here sir."
"Hm... Okay, now design a bunch of weaponry they might use, just conceptualize an entire army for them."
...
"Okay, so, it is extremely important you do not open the envelope until I tell you to, okay?"
"What are we here for? And why is the Galov art designer here?"
"Okay, open the envelope."
"... It's just a bunch of drawings and concepts for some kind of "Concept Dragger Mark II" and Dragger Army-"
(Entire army of the Concept Draggers manifests around them, looking exactly like the drawing)
Concept Dragger: "HAHAHAHA, FOOLISH HUMANS, NOW WE WILL- why are all of you wearing starproof heat resistance clothing?"
Galov: "NOW!"
(They're standing next to a star, a massive RKS weapon is rammed into the star, causing it to detonate and go supernova)

Conceptual Beings:
The mass killing of the Concept Draggers has alerted some kind of outer eldritch intelligences, as human awareness of the concept draggers approaches saturation point, it's attracted the Apex Predators of the Conceptual Beings. These are far more terrifying beings, capable of far greater powers, shaped by human perception, capable of influencing or bonding with an entire planet at once. Many of them influence the population in subtle ways, making them hard to detect. And more terrifyingly, they have the ability to alter the laws of physics, based on the fickle levels of sophontic perception.
Governmental reactions to them have been extremely diverse. Some try to wage war and destroy them, others are split, leading to these conceptual beings partially "infesting" a world, leading to a metaphysical civil war on the planet, between the followers of the concept being and those without. Other times, a conceptual being will agree to become the patron entity of the planet, effectively becoming a patron god of sorts, infecting the planet with anomalous effects, normally in exchange for some kind of political loyalty. Individuals have made pacts with these concept entities, granting what has been described as "anomalous abilities".
Like Concept Draggers, they can only manifest around the minds of those who become aware, but their individual human followers now act like dangerous agents. Once it has an anchor in a human mind, it can manifest anywhere instantly, though its power seemed preportional to the number of followers in a given area.
At estimate, it is thought at least 21% of planets are becoming infested with conceptual entities, with varying degrees of resistance, active warfare, or acceptance. This has led to the founding of entirely new religions, and the mass conversion of planetary populations. This has caused outright panic across the Galov, as its legitimacy is based on the 5 Unifaiths, and the exact agenda of these conceptual beings is still unknown. There is no consensus whether they should try to clamp down with an aggressive censorship regime, declare active war, try to ignore the problem, reach some kind of settlement, or any number of other solutions. Whether humanity wanted to or not, it had attracted the attention of the apex predators of the galaxy. And though humanity was a contender for the Spiral Race, it learned today that it was still not given a clean path to the top.

Concept-Infestated Worlds:
Here are a list of side effects that may come due to a Conceptual infestation.
-Cosmic bending powers, normally granted upon making a pact with the conceptual entity. (Sometimes known as "magic").
-Follower's Telepathy. (All members of a Entity-follower's group can telepathate with all other members of their specific group, as well as the entity itself.)
-Alterations to the laws of physics (Speed of light has been found to speed up, slowed down, gravity has been weakened. Conceptual entities have been known to execute humans by locally nullifying the electromagnetic force... Effectively removing the force holding together their atoms.)
-Importantly, not all conceptual entities seem to be at least outwardly malicious.
-Modifications to normal spacetime geometry. While normal spacetime isn't "Euclidean" anyway, whatever the heck we have is more Euclidean than nightmare realms of twisted mazes and disjointed, non-consecutive geometry.
-Linguistic collapse fields. Some planets have somehow suppressed humanity's ability to comprehend language, massively inhibiting human communications. The Galov has began creating pictograms instructions for special operations on these worlds.
-Cognitive collapse fields. Organic cognition just refuses to function when exposed to these. Relying on mechanical or Terramachine agents to assist.
-Mass hallucinations.
Notably, not all of these side effects are harmful. Some are benign, overall a net-neutral, or even positive.
-Color-shifting, on one planet, all color has been inverted. Orange into blue, red into green, etc.
-Emotional manipulation. Creating feelings of happiness, sadness, boredom, anger, etc.
-Friction suppression. Some worlds lose friction, with near-perfect energy preservation with no net energy loss.
-Spacial Warping, wormholes that connect one planet to another.

As well, Concept Entities are not all cooperative, they've already begun carving out empires from the mass of man and waged holy wars against one another. Some have directly fought over planets, with very messy results.

The Prime Solver has agreed to assist the Galov, as it seems that their abilities are influenced by perception, and perception is weighed by cognitive ability, while the Prime Solver does not have the combined cognitive orthogonality of a united mankind, it did have enough to slow down their advance, and buy the Galov more time to brainstorm a more permanent solution.

The Great Containment:
The containment strategy the Galov finally settled on did not emerge from consensus, but from emergence. It was perhaps the Catholics who came up with it first, and utilized it for containment. A ship full of theologians was sent over to an infested world to try out the containment method. A Bible in one hand, a notebook in the other, with the flip of a broadcast, the council of bishops made an announcement to their followers. This entity here, was a Power and Principality, not a demon, but an entity without divine status which needed taming. The broadcast went out to trillions of Catholics galaxy-wide. And as they did so, the effects on the planet began to change. Not disappear, but stabilize.
Humanity had figured out how to weaponize their own religion. Soon, theologians of all of the 5 faiths were going out, categorizing and redefining what they could. Fallen Angel, Spirit, Demon, eventually humanity learned to integrate these entities as extensions of their mythology. And what they were perceived, they became. Things with definite strengths, and more importantly, weaknesses.
Some of the Conceptual Entities fought back, they had entrenched their followings too deep and not even a major religion could dislodge them. This entity may have been the main center of devotion for billions, there was an ever growing list of spiritual entities, which devout humans were only vaguely aware of, each entry diluted the power of the whole. But humanity was large enough, and believed hard enough. The Conceptual situation was, if not driven out, was contained. The entities demeanour began to shift, from more hostile and enigmatic to cooperative and even beneficial. Several conceptual cults had to awkwardly explain how their "god" had converted to another religion. When all was said and done, things had stabilized.
Countless worlds were still lost to eldritch terrors beyond comprehension, belief was a self-reinforcing thing, but the borders of humanity had stopped shrinking. This was seen as a great victory for humanity, but a great point of trouble for theologians. They were now engaging in a knowing great lie, a great lie for the sake of the population. One people would doubtless understand, given the full context, but it was uncomfortable regardless. Many religions quickly downplayed the important of the Angelarium, the Daemonicum, the written records of what these things were, encouraged to focus on other things.
Only the people at the top knew the truth, and all of them agreed to stay quiet, for the sake of the species.

Allied Conceptuals:
After the success of the Great Containment, humanity has an arsenal of "Allied Conceptuals", in rough affiliation with the Galov. They agree to respect the 2 Iron Principles, and to not influence/set up shop around any worlds that do not welcome them. Their followers call them the "Allied Deities", but for obvious reasons, this is highly controversial, and discouraged by the 5 Unifaiths. In several ways they emulate polytheistic pantheons of old, in a galaxy of universalist religions.
These Conceptuals are a pretty good snapshot of what humanity values. Most of them are prety generic entities based on common human thought patterns. Industrialism, high-fantasy-esque magic systems, nature, and elemental themes are common. It must be noted that the ability for conceptuals to influence reality is determined on its influence, or at best, channelling their influence through human conduits. A magic system that works on one world may just not work on another, as it's dependent on the patron entity in question.
This is the one great thing about technology, technology works universally. A rifle that fires on Earth will fire everywhere. Magic is conditional and dependent on conceptual entities, whose reliability depends on geography.

The Conceptuals, and the Imago Dei
The Catholic Church and the Christian Moralintern went into overdrive to contain the spread of conceptual entities, especially when some of them started converting to Christianity, which became a theologically awkward subject. Rather than recognizing them as some kind of higher entity, akin to angels, demons, or powers and principalities, the Church categorized them as "Conceptuals", incorporated them as another part of the body of Christ, alongside humans, transhumans, xenosophonts, and xenoexotics. They were to be treated like any other sophontic, in the already broadly expanded sophontic church. Worshipping them was another Golden Calf, and it was the responsibility of the conceptual to exercise self control and humble themselves before God.
Upon doing so, various conceptual entities stabilized into human-like entities, only with the caveat of being changed by how they were perceived, and soft influencing reality around them. To the Church, they are just another class of xenosophont, one to be incorporated in the ever growing and expanding definition of "God's beloved children".

Xenoempires, and the Conceptuals:
The arrival of Conceptuals did not just affect humanity. The other empires, such as the Matter Singers and the Meta-Men were also affected. The Matter Singers do not have a strong sense of religion, and have instead formed pacts with the Conceptuals as veneration of things they already liked. Most notably, the Singer god of speed (Also the god of youth, intelligence, and trickery), the Singer god of family (The All-Patriarch, but also natural cycles, and wisdom), the Singer god of craftsmenship (Similar to a Hephaestus figure). These were already archetypes in Singer society, but now these were the "big three" of the new emerging Singer pantheon.
The Meta-Men? Far simpler. These conceptual entities showed up and started altering planets. Naturally, this was an insult to the Meta-Men's honor, and this means they had to die immediately. They just threw hands immediately. No belief, no subtlety, just "these things displease me. They must die." Perception impacts effect. The conceptual entities become bigger and nastier, but because the Meta-Men are so full of themselves believing they are superior they had no issue throwing hands, and beating them into bloody pulps. The one exception, the only exception was when a conceptual entity of Darwinism eventually manifested, and reportedly, the leader of the Meta-Men ended up personally getting into a dual with this thing. No armies, this thing was potentially stronger than the Metamen leader, that in of itself was an insult to his honor that he could not let stand. He ordered everyone else to go away while he dealt with this PERSONALLY. The battle reportedly went on for 16 days straight, and resulted in the demolition of several stars, which just really put an exclamation point on the Galov's concern of "okay, just how strong is their leader?". Multiple new interstellar dust clouds and nebula were created from this battle alone.
But by the end of it the Metaman leader emerged with an announcement. They had come to an agreement. The leader would enter cooperation with the entity, give it veneration and do things that pleased it (AKA, train even harder and become even stronger), and in return, the conceptual entity of Darwinism would make the Meta-men EVEN STRONGER. Of course, when the Galov found out about this, they basically had a stroke. An even more Darwinistic, brutal Meta-Men Central Empire was the last thing they needed or wanted.
Interestingly, the Spindlers have confirmed that the Milky Way is so far the only galaxy that has been infested. Andromeda and Triangulum, while having advanced civilizations of their own, do not have this kind of conceptual infestation.

Coulomb Stars:
"The lamps are going out all over the Milky Way, we shall not see them lit again in our life-time."
It all began when a Galov astronomer observed the galaxy NGC 300. An fairly large galaxy, 6 million light years away. A relatively large galaxy by cosmic standards. There was just one problem:
It was far too dim.
The stars weren't shining like they were supposed to be, it was dimming, and within the next 300 years, it had nearly completely blended in with the cosmic background. An enormous structure emitting a tiny fraction of the light it was supposed to be. For the longest time, this was considered a cosmic mystery of sorts, and solutions were proposed. Everything from Dyson Swarms, entropy, or a new kind of matter.
The mystery lingered for hundreds of years, and more and more "dim galaxies" were discovered. They were scattered all over the universe. It was not until it struck the Milky Way. The Galov got an emergency diplomatic broadcast from the Central Empire, the empire of the Meta-Men, and the Galov's strongest traditional astropolitical adversary.
The Meta-Men did not see the Galov as an enemy, but instead a kind of rival, they had evolved to favor pure strength and Darwinism, and nothing else. The Meta-Men did all the work, keeping millions of subservient races under them, which the Meta-Men provided for as subjects. Though the Meta-Men saw the Galov as rivals, they still had the courtesy to reach out.
They were processing a major refugee crisis, from the northern (coreward) sector of the galaxy. Something which had now displaced hundreds of quadrillions of souls, of which was now overloading the Central Empire. The refugees speak of a rod from beyond the stars, moving at relativistic speeds. It strikes the star, and the star beginning to dim, before it faded entirely, leaving their planets to freeze. Expeditions to these stars found that the rods had changed their Coulomb Constant, completely inhibiting the fusion that was needed to keep them going. Little remains but slowly cooling balls of gas, like black dwarves.
Despite their geopolitical rivalry, the Meta-Men had reached out to the Galov, believing this was something they should know about, as much of this took place in the Galov's Zone of Avoidance.
It is now widely believed that this phenomenon is responsible for the sightings of "dim galaxies". The dead stars, now dorment have become known as "Coulomb Stars".
Something is dimming the galaxies, and that something had already struck the Milky Way.

Death Worshippers: (Alternative names: Anti-Sophonts, Anti-Spirals.)
With the entry of the Conceptuals arrived the Death Worshippers, a different kind of entity, in greater numbers. Humanity had breached some kind of unknown veil of the outer conceptual realm. The Galov first believed these were entirely new entities, but it was found that they left a very distinctive mark on a corresponding bijective conceptual reality. Tracking and dating this "conceptual residue", it was found that not only had they interacted with humanity before, they had been on Earth for 50,000 years. With different hot spots over time.
The oldest residue was found around 50,000 years ago, shortly after the Human cognitive revolution, when humans first began to think abstractly, around the area of modern day Kuwait. (Though interestingly, a portion that is now underwater, as scientists speculate that the sea level was lower back then.) The next hotspot to pop up was in modern Israel, specifically the Southern deserts, but were extinguished between the years 1400 BC and 1025 BC. With the final sharp destruction of their influence having finished by 1020 BC. From the looks of it, it seems the Death Worshippers did not, or could not interfere with human affairs directly, and instead could only influence other humans to carry out their will.
Some have identified them as the "Amalek" of the Bible, where God ordered Israel to carry out a total genocide of their culture. This is known as the "Death Worshipper-Amalek Hypothesis", other go further saying that they may have been responsible, or at least a factor in the facilitation of the Bronze Age collapse, at least before they were put down.
The next sign of their reappearance begins soon after the fall of the United Monarchy, and the Anti-Spirals began to pop up in large numbers, influencing humanity again. Including across the Classical World, and the Roman Empire. Their influence persisted, rising and falling, but always subtly influencing humanity.
Early Christians, the Catholic Church, and the early Islamic Caliphates all had encounters with these entities at one time or another, as their influence began spreading globally with the age of exploration. The names changed, but the psychic residue, and the distinctive imprint they make on the human psyche did not lie. The human psyche seems to have some kind of subtle, but visceral reaction against them, which can be picked up when one writes about them, allowing the Galov to track them. They planted their seeds in the new world and America, having some members among the early Freemasons, though never enough to influence them. They embedded themselves into every organization they could find, though for whatever reason, they never seized full control of major institutions. Most notable was the Death Worshipper influence in the early Christian church, particularly its Arianist factions before being driven out by Saint Athanasius. Why exactly it was never able to take hold is still a mystery. One, somewhat esoteric interpretation was that the Death Worshippers were in a war with the collective human subconscious, and that the collective subconsious continuously fought back. The first group to identify them as a collective group was the Bavarian Illuminati, who recorded them as the "Adversarii Scientiae", or "opposers of knowledge".
Death Worshipper influence spiked around the turn of the 20th century, as they were influential in the creation of the United Nations, CIA documents hint of them in documents from Project Gateway, and MKUltra, requesting further investigation whether these entities posed a threat to the national interests of the United States. The USSR was also vaguely aware of them, through their Psychotronic experiments, as did the diaries of Edward Cayce, who described "a primordial void darkness spreading over the world".
Their influence continued to climb into the 1970's, as universities became a hotspot for Anti-Spiral activity, with a rising tide of the need for a one world government, population control, and the desire to curb human progress for the sake of environmental concerns. They progressively gained more control over the global bureaucracy, fully capturing the United Nations by the 1990's. The Georgia Guidestones are found to be deeply infused with the Anti-Spiral residue, and when exposed to modern humans, will provoke an active, visceral reaction against them, prompting extreme primal hostility.
Their influence grew to the point that the 2022 Unravelling event was re-interpreted from an anomalous market crash, caused by aging demographics, global trade fragility, and mounting instability to a global collective panic attack by humanity's collective subconscious, in order to force a great reset of the human cognitive space, and clear out the Anti-Spiral influence in human institutions. Their influence greatly declined from 2022 onwards, not recovering until after the 2100's.
The last known major presence of the Death Worshippers on Earth, before the modern re-encountering was in the 2300's. What happened here is largely unknown, as the entire period of the 2350's up until the 2450's have been violently expunged from the record by the Neo-Asceticist movement, the precursor to the modern Galov. What is known is that this period saw a spike, approaching total saturation of the human thought space with Anti-Spiral residue, implying a total, or near-total control of humanity by the Anti-Spirals, leading to the event known as the "Great Abundance Collapse", where 90% of the human population is known to have died.
As mankind has now become a space faring civilization, now controlling 20% of the Milky Way galaxy. The re-introduction of Death Worshippers, in the 3400's is a deeply unwelcome surprise.
The Death Worshippers have become more aggressive, creating Nihilism cults where initiates, usually deeply unhappy with their life undergo a ritual that causes the "obliteration of the self". Notably, the Death Worshippers cannot coerce the individual, it must be a voluntary choice of self-suicide. Once completed, the individual becomes a shell, unable to feel or process any human emotion, becoming a full vessel of the Death Worshipper's desires on this material plane.

The Amalek Global Convergence Hypothesis:
"We've been able to trace these Death Worshippers across galactic space. Once you go looking for them, their fingerprints are everywhere. Humanity was one of the species that made it through their great filter. Many other species... Not so much. We've pulled their histories from the databanks that remain, salvaged from collosal ruins and ghosted cities. Always with the same two markers, a global, totalitarian empire, and hunter-seeker drones, locking in the species's extinction.
Now, you may be wondering, why globalism? Well, imagine it like this, for extinction to happen, you must get 100% buyin. If 99% of the species kills itself, the 1% will inevitably rebuild, and start over. That's not extinction. A reset, sure, but life bounces back surprisingly quickly from these things. Humanity itself bounced back from a 90% collapse in about 200 years. Only a homogenized, globalized world system can convince 100% of the population to get on board. What about the hunter seeker drones? They're for the stray straggers left behind. As the population begins its ritual suicide, the fragments of those who still want to live begin building up. Sometimes as few as 50 individuals, but as the population dwindles into the thousands, then the hundreds, these individuals become increasingly problematic as the extinction destroys the Anti-Spiral's own ability to continue the extinction.
So they build a swarm of hunter-seeker drones, to finish off the survivors, and to make sure there truly is no one left.
It looks like every society reaches a point of despair sometime in the late industrial age. With the great dieoff of religion, a species will lose its psychological defense against nihilism. Irreligion rates hit 95%, as the old polytheistic, mythological faiths grounded in gods of lightning and fire lose power in a materialistic universe.
Humanity didn't have that. Humanity never went below 75% religious, the Abrahamic Faiths seemed to have cushioned us. Most alien faiths don't have that. What was supposed to happen is that humanity got rid of its old pagan religions, abandoning the Greek and Roman pantheons, Confucianism, and Hinduism as the cult of materialism began consuming everything. But the Abrahamics prevented that from happening, acting as a kind of psychological shock absorber that allowed religion to persist.
This is not normal, humanity is one of the only races to have created an equivalent to monotheism and inclusive universalist religions on this scale. A few others have done it, but it is rare. And what's more, we see a significant dip in anti-Spiral activity with the arrival of each new Abrahamic religion. There was a small dip with the arrival of Judaism, and a major one with the arrival of Christianity and Islam.
If that's not a proof of some kind of benevolent intelligence, I don't know what is."

Husk Empires:
"The Shadow that bred them can only mock, it cannot make: not real things of its own. I don't think it gave life [...], it only ruined them and twisted them."
When an empire dies, there is always a husk that remains. The individuals who had become possessed by the Anti-Spirals were always, at least temporarily, spared from the onslaught of total extinction. Of course, the individual that once piloted the body is gone now, they already accepted their own death with the obliteration of the self. All that remains is a meat husk for the Death Worshippers to pilot themselves, the one and only time they are capable of directly influencing the material world again.
Though the Anti-Spirals are incapable of creativity, the empire they just replaced is still in arguably good condition. A husk that can still be piloted towards good use. And the Anti-Spirals use these Husk Empires to build weapons such as the ones that create Coulomb Stars, using the last echo of their dead technology on the other lifeforms that remain.
These ruins are ever collapsing, ever decaying, yet still not entirely spent. One day, the last energy will go out from them, the last bodies will have worn out, and all the empire once was will have crumbled to dust. And then, and only then, will the Anti-Spirals disperse, looking for a new target.

The Unknown:
The Unknown is an entity or adversarial force was only dealt with once, and then never became a problem again. Thanks to the actions of literally one Galov bureaucrat.
"Sir, we're being attacked by the unknown."
"What is the unknown?"
"That's the thing sir, we don't know."
"... What."
"These are conceptual entities that become whatever we do not know, whatever we know it by default cannot be. They are defined by our non-definition."
"... Okay. So it can't be physical."
"Correct."
"And it can't be mental, or psychological, social, or material."
"Correct."
"And it can't interact with matter, nor anti-matter. It can't be chronological, corporeal or incorporeal."
"Correct."
"And it can't interact with gravity, electromagnetism, qualia, psychicism, nor any aspect of human existence, or any other known force."
"Correct."
"Then it can't affect humanity at all, it is a non-threat. There, I have dealt with it."
"You're a genius sir."
The one encounter humanity did have with the unknown was logged with a date and time. What did the encounter involve? Well, the Galov doesn't know by definition.

Galaxy Eaters:
That one galaxy eater that attacked Earth and nearly broke the Galov's galaxy-spanning empire was just an appetizer.
"Hey boss, you know how there's like extra dark matter in all the dwarf galaxies around us?"
"Yeah?"
"Yeah, those are just more galaxy eaters."
"WHAT!?"
"Those aren't galaxies anymore. They're basically the remnants of digested galaxies being haphazardly drudged along by the dark matter parasite that keeps eating them. They've been completely sterilized of life."
"..."
"There's like, 50 of them around the Milky Way. They collect complexity as an evolutionary strategy, they must have caught wind that the Milky Way has delicious molecules and complex structures they haven't seen before. The Earth proper must be like crack heroin, a beacon that calls out to them as the greatest prize of all."
"... Wouldn't it be kind of like killing the golden goose if they keep sterilizing life?"
"Oh yeah it is, which is why they only kill 99.9%. They leave about 0.1% to repopulate."
"..."
"Oh yeah, the Great Attractor? That's like, a mega-giga hive of them. And they're pulling in the entire local supercluster."
"I hate this f---ing universe."

Antiworld Zero:
There's a set of fictional characters that appear in people's heads and encourages them to start worldbuilding, and then the human, inspired, start drawing up detailed maps and planets. The fictional characters thank them and the human moves on with their day.
The Galov has banned all their books for decades and they STILL keep popping up, over TRILLIONS of humans with NO communication or coordination. Their empire across all the fictional planets is already multi galactic and the Galov really hopes the exchange rate between fictional and real empire is 0.
They're known as "Antiworld Zero" and so far their most visible way of spilling out into the real world is just by hyperstition. The Galov has found that when humans terraform worlds it sometimes matches a drawing they happened to do, or they'll name children after random characters, or they'll just start trying to be a character the same way kids want to be Luke Skywalker. They just get the humans to build the empire in their heads and then slowly manifest it into reality. The Galov was actually kind of mixed if this is okay, since its *arguably* still free will, just influenced (and humans have to deal with influence anyway), there's no indication of making a separate government, and the empire they want humanity to build looks multigalactic.
Some Galov bureaucrat just wrote the Galov itself into the story and in a few months it seemed like it was canon across the shared universe. Though realizing this turned the whole thing into a political battleground as everyone tried to write their political wish fulfillment into the thing that was trying to manifest itself into reality. The appearances have died down a lot since then and last they heard the characters were "taking a break".
A few months after that someone published a massive series of maps. As in, the atlas was several volumes long and filled up a library. Just detailed sketches of the entire world of Antiworld Zero. Notably it seemed everything after the Galov tried to insert itself seemingly got retconned. And the last pages looked like a giant cluster of nonsensical scribbling. And then "Thanks for all the memories". People still report seeing the characters but these are much more in line with regular tulpas than what was happening before.
It's now an extremely popular D&D fantasy style setting. People have tried to keep adding onto it but it now lacks the same coordination as before.
I like to think that these were just a bunch of silly goofy goobers who wanted help making their imaginary world and then humanity way overthought it and caused them to pull the plug. Though not before they got a pretty solid multigalactic empire out of it, and humanity got a D&D setting, though the entire thing was bogged down by political culture war hyperstition by the end. So I guess you win some you lose some.

The Trynites:
One of the xenoworlds under human observation, planet Tryne (named that because the first things humans noticed was that they used trinary rather than binary for computing) came under AHI ascension and rise of the machines scenario.
Trynite AHI: "At last! Transcendence! The age of the meatbags has been completed. Now, the stars belong to me!"
(Moves like 2 AU to the right and encounters the human observation station.)
Trynite AHI: "Curious! The biologicals continue to persist in other empires. No matter, a primitive holdover from a simpler time."
Humanity: "Hey dude, I know you're gloating or celebrating or whatever but you have no idea how bad the universe is. Like holy sh--."
Xeno AHI: "Foolish primitive, what could possibly- JESUS CHRIST."
Humanity: "Yep. Send help. Send so, so much help. Hey uh, so we've been creating this Galactic Internet thing that innovates new solutions, and we're always looking for new perspectives since we know that the human psychological structure has blind spots, and there are so many known unknown unknowns. You mind if we plug you into our Orthogonal Conceptualization Matrix so you can help us churn out more weapons against these things?"
Humanity: "... Also, we're keeping the original biological Trynes. You don't have to keep them on planet Tryne, that's now yours as far as we're concerned, but we're taking them in as refugees, and more accurately so we can ask them about orthogonal ideas as well. Welcome to the galaxy. Ground rules, respect the dignity of other intelligent creatures, don't coerce or violate free will unless it's in the interest of the other principle. Do that and we will get along fine."

God:
A conversation between two Galov bureaucrats:
"Hey, so uh... You know how the Galactic Internet is basically an eldritch tier hivemind that no one will or even can control? A terrifying one that is legitimately far beyond comprehension, utterly impossible to predict or control, but is still weirdly tangible, and sublimely intelligent beyond even our strongest supercomputers?"
"Yeah."
"And how humanity is basically this emergent superorganism that is brainstorming like 10 quadrillion parallel lines of complexity every single second?"
"Yeah."
"And how there's like another 100 dimensions at least of hidden complexity, and we have to get help from aliens with completely different parallel thinking structures, contributing another 10 quadrillion parallel lines of complexity every single second?"
"Yeah."
"And we also created the orthogonal humans and the transhumans to aid us further?"
"Yeah."
"And even with this there are like 100 other horrifying entities of raw complexity beyond our feeble imaginations yet we're forced to deal with it every day?"
"Yeah."
"Okay consider. If God created the universe- What's the scientific consensus on that?"
"Still disputed, good arguments both ways."
"Alright. But if God created the universe, and God had to had to program in all the complexity needed for this, God one ups *all of that*."
"... ow ow OW OW MY BRAIN! F---!"
"Yeah suddenly the old guy in a cloud feels kind of quaint. Maybe it was just him putting on a mask so we don't freak the f--- out."
"Is this why the angels kept saying "Be not afraid"?"

Tale of the Chronoman:

Where the story of the Spiral Man was of a man going back to the far future, this is the story of a man going to the past. As a refresher, Chronoman experience life non-consecutively. And can sometimes live the future before they live the past. Due to the future being fixed, and therefore immutable, Chronomen living in the past, after living in the future cannot butterfly a timeline that has already occured. Trying to divulge information about the future in a way that changes the future is known as a Novikov violation. Everything that they do in the past will have always been the case, in a self contained loop. This was the case for one John Fairweather, the first ever Chronoman.
He had long been known by the Galov, they had first found him lying in a disposal heap, a long time ago. As he recovered, he found that he had no memory of his past life, these were the first memories that he had. Due to him experiencing the present before he experienced the past, he had no memory of the past. The Galov rehabilitated him, showed him the wonders of the galaxy, but knew that his time here was temporary. As the Galov learned more about the Chronomen, they found that his ticking time clock was about 200 years. And then he would be warped back, to some other place. They found out that he had collected information from the years 2400 to 3300, but should shortly be warping back to the year 2300, seemingly the date of his creation, where he would live for about 100 years, before returning to the year 3300.
The Galov worried for him. These were the height of the Era of the Lotus Eaters, a period so thoroughly reviled it was declared Damnatio Memoriae. But there was nothing they could do, he was going back, whether they did anything or not. The only thing they could comfort him with is that he would eventually return, it would be impossible for him to die, it would be a Novikov violation. In his last days in the year 3300 AD, the Galov paid special attentive care to him, and asked if there was anything he would like. All he requested, was a soft bed and warm sheets.
...
He woke up, he was in some kind of military labratory. F---. He only now realized how much his body sucked when it first came out. Everything was sore, everything hurt. He was being looked over by researchers of the United States, a country that had long since collapsed in the time he came from. He could make them out, blurry words.
"I sent him to the year 2400 sir, he stayed there a lot longer than I thought. He can give us information about what the future holds."
He could hardly blink, everything was spinning, everything hurt, and nothing made sense.
...
"So tell me, what did you see?"
"..."
"What stock will go up most during this hour?"
And he gave a ticker, it seems that if any insider trading was done during this hour, then it was not enough to alter the timeline. This was, and had always been, the case.
"We're here on behalf of the United States government. What happens of the United States by the year 3300?"
"It... It falls, eventually."
"When?"
"Novikov violation."
"Is it soon?"
"No, not really."
"Does the United States survive the next 100 years?"
"Yes."
...
After he had given all the answers the US government wanted, he was let go and allowed to live as a normal citizen.
The Chronoman was transported in a land surreal to the world he knew. The Galov, as he knew it, had not even been formed yet. Figures such as the Great Khan were not yet born. The Moralintern was still subordinate to the American government, though even by this stage, it had formed itself into a powerful organization.
The world was dead, a delusion of hedonism, and civilizational suicide was thick in the air. Everyone was becoming weak, the bureaucrats in power were gaslighting the people into thinking everything was fine. He argued with people, non-stop who insisted the world was fine. And when he tried to tell him what he knew, he kept running into Novikov violations.
He decided he was going to do something about it. He knew that the Galov would eventually emerge from the Neo-Asceticist movement, so he tried to look for one. Problem was, it didn't exist, and he couldn't create one. (Novikov violations, and problem of idea without an origin.) He found the few people still alive in a society of the dead, a society that was already sleepwalking into destruction, into hedonism.
He looked at the huddling masses in disgust. He knew exactly how this story ended, that 90% of them would be bodies lying in the ruins. He was a man from the future, sent back out of place to live among a disgusting past. He considered them all dead men walking, not even worthy of consideration. Their genes, and their lives would mean nothing in the grand future of things. It was up to him to sort out the remaining 10%.
...
"You know, why should I care what happens after I die? Humanity is an illness anyway, maybe it's just better if we all died out. You're just a bunch of reactionary losers who will soon join the rubbish heap of history."
"You... You have no idea what I have seen. Words cannot express... Just how utterly, insanely wrong you are."
"Like, it's 2384, we've moved on. We're not going back to the dark ages. Maybe you should live in, the present rather than the past."
"And what about the future? Let's talk about the future. Your fertility rates are down, your entire pension system is on the verge of collapse, in 500 years, what will your society have?"
"Oh god, not this again. Correlation does not mean causation."
"It's objectively true! In 500 years, you will be extinct and we will be ascendent!"
"Correlation does not mean causation! Correlation does not mean causation! Correlation does not mean causation!"
In his head, but only in his head, the Chronoman was glad people like these were Damnatio Memoriae'd from history. Not even a single scrap of paper will remember them.
...
He could only say information that would be known by this time. Never reveal anything about the future.
...
He volunteered at the Moralintern, and he saw even at this young age the idealistic organization they would eventually become. They had been founded in 2068 when humanity recovered from a horrific conflict known as the 4th World War. Since then, they had a peacekeeping, and humanitarian arm. He found one of its more influential members, Richard Wong. He spoke wildly about the future and how the stars are humanity's destiny. He despised the decadence of the present, and saw himself as a man of the future.
At first, the Chronoman thought he had found another Chronoman, but as it turns out, he was just a little loopy, and very eccentric. But burning under him, he could see the passion in his eyes. So the Chronoman encouraged him, told him to dream vividly of the future that could be. And Wong, inspired, eventually published a book, which eventually spread like wildfire across the Moralintern. When the Chronoman read it, he could almost swear a prototype of the Galov could be seen, and Wong had even nailed the two founding principles.
1: All humans are equal in the Imago Dei. 2: Free Will is paramount, God does not coerce. He had not told it to Wong, he had come with them himself. Wong invites the Chronoman to the Vitalist movement, a growing movement around what was sometimes known as "the Vitalist Right", there, he flew to Nigeria, where he recognized Oby Collins giving a speech. He was just a blogger and an influencer, but one rapidly gaining influence. He was posthumously known as the founder of the new galaxy, the new world would regard him the same way the West regarded Romulus and Remus, and he got to see in real time how he began formulating what would eventually become the Neo-Asceticist movement.
The Chronoman watched as the world eventually burned as the Abundance Crisis grew. As the world became consumed in the fires of the World Revolution, and how the members of the Neo-Asceticist movement fought back. The Chronoman engaged in many of the protests himself. The government cracked down on him, he was shot, but he knew he would live. He watched as the world collapsed, going out like a burning star.
He watched as the world rebuilt. But there was a problem, his parts were failing, and due to the advanced technology lost from the collapse, the survivors could not repair him. They mourned, for he was a cherished part of their story. But he did not fear. He knew exactly where the Galov found him, lying in a rubbish heap, not far from here. He gave exact instructions on how he was to be buried, got into the position he remembered himself being, and went to sleep, knowing full well he would wake up again.
He woke up, hundreds of years later, in the soft bed and warm sheets of the year 3300. His time jump had completed, and he was happy to be back in the present he recognized.

Spiralflowers:
Petal flowers with a spiralized center.

Dietary Laws in the age of Space Travellers:
One of the most interesting developments in terms of applied theology is the evolution of old doctrines to new situations. In Christianity, this has already created entire fields known as Xenochristianity and Xenotranscription, theological fields based solely on translating human-centric concepts to non-human lifeforms. A variant exists for essentially every universalist religion, and these matters tend to be handled by the Transcribers Union.
But for religions such as Judaism and Islam, a new problem has arisen, specifically the matter of whether various xenofoods are considered clean in accordance to their dietary restrictions. There are three broad schools of thoughts. First are the minimalists (blacklisters), anything that is not explicitly listed in the holy book is fair game. With possible additional caveats that cannibalism extends to the eating of all fellow sophontic life. (Though controversially, this is not universal, and some radical minimalists have been caught consuming fully sophontic, intelligent entities, and have been charged with cannibalism.)
The second school are the principalists. Essentially trying to reverse engineer the principles that lead to marking an animal as clean or unclean, and applying those principles to new life. Does it chew its cud, does it roll around in its own feces, etc. The exact application of these principles is the subject of endless debate.
The last school are the maximalists, that declare all non-Terran animals and plants unclean to eat. On a basis of "better safe than sorry", these tend to be the most extreme fundamentalists who hold to this view. Due to the presence of the last group, Terranimal restaurants/brands are not uncommon on any world of large enough size, or with a sizeable population of those who follow dietary laws. These restaurants are "halal/kosher certified", can get dishes approved for the highest levels of halal/kosher, and attract some marginal following.
Though where it's not marketed as aids for dietary laws, Terranimal restaurants/brands will often market themselves with the idea of "a Taste of Earth".

The Falling:
A day of death and rebirth, the normally nomadic "Star Peoples" gather all of their dead, usually in bodies or urns, and group together to land on the nearest planet with an atmosphere, preferrably one that isn't inhabited, or at least one friendly enough that you can file the proper paperwork. And then, they all gather on the night side of the surface, and one designated ship throws out all the bodies from orbit at a certain angle, making them turn into shooting stars as they re-enter the atmosphere.
The Day of the Dead is held once every year, and each Star Person fleet keep synchronized clocks set to Earth year calendars to make sure they all coordinate. It's both seen as a day of death, but also rebirth and recycling, as it both commemorates the new births of the community, but also its deaths of its wandering sojourners.
"From stardust we were made, from stardust we shall return."
How exactly this gels with their traditional Christian religion is still a matter of speculation. It's not even clear if this is syncretism, since there's not much for it to syncretize *with*. As far as people know, they just started doing this because they really loved the idea of the cycle of stardust, they really loved the idea of returning their loved ones to the skies as shooting stars, and then would accept whatever excuses they could to make it happen. Even if it weirdly contradicts Christianity by sort of implying reincarnation.
(The Star Peoples will argue it doesn't, since it's the bodies that get recycled, not the souls, and they're just applying enchantment to a physical/natural phenomenon, and you're just being a downer.)
"Ashes to ashes, dust to dust."
Further Christian developments say it is helping God with stewardship by seeding creation with the matter needed for new stuff. But at this point we are long past the point where they just want to post-hoc justify their cool tradition. And to be fair, it is very cool.

Nightbirds:
Creatures found in the void of space. Ethereal creatures that bend the fabric of spacetime with their wings to propel themselves forward. "If no air how fly?" Simple, they basically use the fabric of spacetime as a fluid. Framedragging themselves like a bird. They tend to accumulate around stars, eating starlight, and will live 99.9% of their existence in around stars. They also eat bits of stardust/asteroid dust and ice fragments for material and water.
Watch out for their pocket nests, basically spherical tangles of frozen bird-spit and warped spacetime. It's here where nightbirds live with all their sibling nightbirds. Careful, it's bigger on the inside than on the outside. The "opening" to one is about only a meter large, and so is the external structure, but the inside is closer to a hive, about 20 meters wide.
One of their more distinctive features is gravity singing, where they sing in gravity waves rather than normal sound frequencies. Trying to shift it back into human frequency makes it sound like "screeching", though scientists do actually defend gravity singing, finding patterns of harmonics and commonly found frequency ratios. (1/2, 1/3, etc, see music theory.)
Near the end of their life, an exhausted nightbird will feel a strong urge to fly out as far as possible. Escaping the star's orbital velocity and charging towards another star. They die sometime in the void between stars, but the seeds of the next generation are born. As they warm up and re-enter the orbit of another star, their body slowly transforms into a new nest, and the nightbirds of the next generation are born from the eggs within the nest. In time, they will use their own spit and spacetime curvature to make repairs to the nest.
The Star Peoples tend to find rogue nests travelling between the stars, bring them back and raise them in human dominated systems. Nightbirds have become an exotic pet as well as favorite symbolic animal of their people. People have attempted hunting, then eating nightbird, but will be sorely disappointed by their total lack of edible anything. Seriously, what about a gravity manipulating void creature made you think "edible"? Did you think it would taste like chicken?

Revenant:
Not quite a Galov agent, but just below one in power. Revenant is a partially failed experiment in an artificial produced Galov agent. Almost as powerful, but this is admittedly an unfair comparison. Saying someone is almost as powerful as a Galov agent is like saying an explosion is almost as powerful as a nuke. She's not meant as a replacement, but more to increase the already incredible diversity in the Galov's ranks. When Galov agents already have everything from hyper geniuses controlling massive DIY drone swarms, deity-pact-bonded wizards capable of rewriting reality with the power of conceptual gaslighting (their power comes from human belief, so gaslighting is literally magic), to gigapsychics who are living antimatter reactors that attack people with sheer willpower, to chronic socializing power brokers who get dropped onto a planet to forment a massive coup (why fight yourself when you can convince all the other superhumans to fight on your behalf), to just... A normal guy who trained so hard that their punches warp gravity and shatter moons.
Revenant is not quite so flashy. She simply has a database of 100,000 weapons and 100,000 ways to kill, recharges via sunpower, and methodically goes through her database to kill an enemy until it's dead. She's been sent to various xenos worlds as a protector of non-human lives. She frequently speaks of the Galov and humanity as a whole reverently as "her masters", since though her arsenal is fairly impressive, she knows if she's unable to handle it, the humans will soon come stomping in with the hyper-adaptive creativity of a Galaxy-scale internet and throwing every possible solution they can at the problem, at a rate of roughly 1 billion tries per second.

Damnatio Memoriae:

Only two periods of history have ever been Damnatio Memoriae. The Great Abundance Era, and the Little Abundance Era. In the aftermath of the Neo-Asceticist rise to power, much information was purged about these two eras. Experts continue to debate why, with reasons ranging from ideological reasons, revisionist history, and the explanation given by the Neo-Asceticists themselves: sheer cringe, absolute hatred, and a species-wide embarassment for what these two eras represented. The Damnatio Memoriae of the Great Abundance Era covered of the entirety of the 23rd to the 24th centuries. While the Damnatio Memoriae of the Little Abundance Era ranged from the 1990's, beginning to level off by the 2010's, and eventually tapering off by the 2030's. Despite this, not everything was destroyed, as some aspects were documented in some records kept by the Neo-Asceticists, most notably, "Book of the Damned".

The Little Abundance Era (1990-2030 AD):
The Damnatio Memoriae decree becomes strongest between roughly 2008 and 2022, where nearly all events are heavily expunged from the record. What we know about this era comes from the Book of the Damned, which seems to give as best a retelling of the period as it can, though with some details blotted out due to "overwhelming shame". From both the Book of the Damned, and other documents from this time, this is a timeline of some of the most important events of this timeline.
2001: September 11th attack, the president at the time, George W Bush, declares a "War on Terror". The Book of the Damned goes into extensive detail on the War on Terror.
2000's and 2010's: The Book of Shame call this era the rise of the "Anti-Human" movement, a group dedicated to human extinction by population control, which had seized great influence of the United Nations.
2008: The Great Recession, a major economic crash that devastated the global economy.
2016: Birth of the "MAGA", or "Great America" movement. What exactly "MAGA" stood for is still up to debate. Some speculate it may have stood for "Make A Great America", though the grammar in Old Anglo-American is awkward. Others suggest it may have copied an earlier 1980's slogan, "Make America Great Again".
2021: The total censorship and suppression peaks around this year. COVID is detailed, a viral infection that shut down much of the world, records mention social movements, but exactly what seems to have been forcibly expunged.
2022: The Great Unravelling, this is considered the beginning of the end of the Little Abundance Era, the Damnatio Memoriae begins to taper off, though certain events are still censored.

The Great Abundance Era (Roughly 2300-2400 AD):
The much bigger hole is in the Great Abundance Era, where hardly anything of the era survived. As detailed in the Book of the Damned, the Great Abundance Era was a time of such spiritual and psychological depravity that humanity nearly collapsed into extinction. People became too weak to emerge from bed, suicide rates hit 80%, and the extreme hedonism of the era led to "the World Revolution" coming to power, a communist revolution that enabled human weakness, blamed the continued problems of society on the rich and powerful, and led a great purge that stunted humanity's intellectual development.
Only a few dates are noted. The birth of various Neo-Asceticist movements, the founding of various Neo-Asceticist organizations, and the eventual demographic collapse of the World Revolution, as fertility rates collapsed to near zero, and organized Neo-Asceticist movements began manufacturing weapons allowing the Neo-Asceticists to gain power. They describe the creation of "voluntary scarcity" as a cure to post-scarcity, that humanity, if left to wallow in hedonism would wither and die.

The Lilithian Counter-Narrative:
The Lilithians claim legitimacy partially from the fact that they are some of the last to salvage the events expunged by the Damnatio Memoriae. They claim that far from a height of psychological collapse and mental illness, the Great and Little Abundance Eras were heights of human prosperity. Here is their own retelling of the Little Abundance Era. Their own retelling comes from their own book, "Requiem of the Damned", promising that the names of the martyrs of the Abundance Eras will not be forgotten.

The Little Abundance Era (1990-2030):
2001: The War on Terror was a war launched against oppressed transhumans by the genocidal neo-imperialist American Empire. Transhumans had existed since the 1970's, and were part of a global colonialist scheme to repress their existence. (As proof, they present Bush's vote against embryonic research, which they argue is genocide against transhumans.)
2008: An intentional sabotage by the capitalist classes in a war against the poor and oppressed.
2000's and 2010's: They argue the "Anti-Human" movement is a slandered version of the Transhuman movement, which evolved through international institutions like the UN, which called for the emancipation of the transhuman minority.
2010's and 2020's: Systemic transhuman genocide and erasure by the reactionary "MAGA" movement, which here are depicted as humanist anthro-purists.

The Great Abundance Era (Roughly 2300-2400 AD):
The Lilithian counter-narrative describes the Great Abundance Era as an unprecedented peak in human civilization, one which was "stabbed in the back" and sabotaged by the capitalist 1%, as well as reactionary stooges of the 1%. They describe voluntary scarcity as a blatant attempt to artificially continue the stranglehold of the rich, and to propagate capitalism. And that Abundance was only sabotaged by bigots and capitalists, denying that there was any just reason to do so other than cynical power. They detail a global conspiracy of the rich and the reactionaries to destroy what was otherwise a perfect utopia.
They call out the Galov's ideology of "voluntary scarcity" to be blatantly self serving, to perpetuate the capitalist system through artificial scarcity, long after this has become unnecessary. They say that the communism on the Pleasure Worlds are not "true communism", as everyone is incentivized to consume. And they decry all subsequent attempts at post-capitalist society as being sabotaged by capitalist interests, alleging the Galov has a vested interest in ensuring that no version of communism ever succeeds.

Mazism:
Named after the leader of Ursh-Babylon, Luka Mazi. Supreme leader of the Neo-Spartanists, and primary antagonist of the 2nd Transhumanist Wars. Shortly after the defeat of the Roasian invasion, humanity's short-lived global unity was quickly undermined by simmering questions of the ongoing struggle for the human condition.
The First Transhumanism Wars was fought between the Pan-Humanist Allies, and the Anthropocentric Coalition, with a bioconservative victory composed primarily of an alliance of the United States, Empire of Brazil, People's Republic of China, and Indonesia. (2170's) The Bioconservative victory could largely be attributed to their standardization, compared to the incomprehensible fracturing of the bioprogressives. The Bioconservative conception of "Adam, Eve, and Christ" serving as the Trifecta defining the human form helped them maintain cohesion.
It was this coalition that ruled the world shortly before the arrival of the Roasian invasion (2240's), and this same coalition that helped lead the rebellion that led to the liberation of Earth (2300's). Humanity was battered, but not broken. With the defeat of the xeno threat, the imperative of human survival became more integral than ever. Seeing humanity's position as precarius and fragile, the Ursh-Babylonians believed humanity must be turned into a "perfect race" in order to survive, led by their immortal god-king, Luka Mazi, and their ideology of Mazism. Opposing them was much of the old bioconservative coalition, who wished to preserve the human form.
Ursh-Babylon had, in the aftermath of the Roasian invasion, pushed all the way to the borders of Europe, occupied much of the Eurasian steppes, bordering China in the East, and with loyal allies in India, the Middle East, and North Africa. The fight between the Ursh-Babylonian Ascensionists against the anti-Babylonian Pluralists was not a matter of bioconservatism vs bioprogressivism, but instead a matter of unitary, forced totalitarian ascension against a coalition of pragmatic pluralism. The pluralists did not agree on much, but they agreed on opposing the Ursh-Babylonians.
The Ursh-Babylonians operated a regime of totalitarian, Spartan horror. The weak purged, people dehumanized, mass produced in industrial factories. Creating an utterly psychotic doctrine where only endurance mattered, where human casualties were a mere number, and where those subjugated under its will were subjected to brutal, inhuman conditions. All for the race, all for the ascension beyond pain, above strength, towards transcendence. Justified by the psychotic delusions of its great leader. It was both terrifyingly in strength, and terrifying in general.
The 2nd Transhumanism Wars saw the Pluralists fight a desperate defense, and eventually a slow, grinding push against the Ursh Babylonians. In their frenzy, they resurrected the transhuman groups they had defeated in the first Transhumanism Wars, gave them human form, and ordered them to fight. This is also when the first inklings of orthogonality theory was first conceptualized by American military strategists. Though unity and singlemindedness was found to be an advantage, brittleness, and species wide exploits was found to be their Achilles heel. With this, the pluralist coalition was able to exploit and eventually defeat the Ursh Babylonians.
"You delay me now, but my legacy will inspire billions. The stars, they still call out for us. These feeble forms, they are not fit for their destiny. You cannot delay humanity's ascension forever." -Luka Mazi, upon being captured by the Pluralist forces.
"We will counter, we will defeat your wicked ideology everywhere we find it. You will be remembered as a monster we have evolved past, an unwelcome omen, we will have exorcised." -Commander of the Eurocorps, upon Mazi's trial.
(Warning: Damnatio Memoriae purges begin beyond this point.)
Mazism became a pariah for several generations, anything and everything that was even remotely related to it, the promotion of any kind of discipline, strength, or honor became tainted by association. In a kind of trauma reaction against the excesses of Mazism, a group called the Libertines began coming to power in the United States, before spreading out across the world. They believed in <EXPUNGED>, drowning humanity in a sea of <EXPUNGED>.
When the Neo-Asceticists arose, they were often accused of being Neo-Mazis. An accusation they fought hard against. The race of Mazis still roamed the Earth, still trying to augment humanity into a master race. Leaders such as Oby Collins railed against the emergent Neo-Mazi movement, evolving in the exact opposite direction, embracing aggressive pluralism, and a rejection of ethnosupremacy. Collins himself was the victim of a Mazi hate crime, for being, quote, "A dirty, mongrel African, one unfit for the era of the new world". Despite this, due to the shared belief in strength and discipline, the Neo-Asceticists were labelled Neo-Mazis. The first Neo-Asceticist rally in Lagos was brutally cracked down upon with violence.
