Oby Collins Profile:
Ethnicity: Black Nigerian African, minor white American admixture.
Hometown: Lagos, Nigeria.
Religion: Irreligious/Atheist, though was fully aware of religion's power, and its necessity to society.
Ideology: Ascetic Vitalism. If he had a religion, it was his belief in humanity, in its potential, and the mandate to claim the stars and the galaxy.

Richard Wong Profile:
Ethnicity: Han Chinese, though he moved to South Korea.
Hometown: Gwangju, South Korea. He moved there from the US after an evangelism mission.
Religion: Evangelical Christian. Deeply affiliated with the Moralintern as a lay theologian.
Ideology: Christian Universalism, believed in a compassionate, Christian state that promoted human flourishing.

John Fairweather Profile:
Ethnicity: Chronoman, white American in appearance.
Hometown: Asheville, North Carolina. Not too far outside of Oak Ridge where he was first constructed.
Religion: Agnostic/Neutral. He wasn't worried about the afterlife yet when he knew he was guaranteed to live via Novikov.
Ideology: Galovianism. He saw the future of the Galov, and wanted to retroactively bring the glory of the future and seed it in the past.

Groups and Roles:
Generally speaking, no group is essentialist to the degree as depicted below. There are always exceptions in the outliers, and individuals within the group are not bound by the patterns of the collective. But observations can be drawn from the observation of collectives. These descriptions come from "the Galov Human Factbook", written by a Sea People anthropologist Wijono Yanlin, and is used as a study textbook at the Galov's "Macrohistory of the Galaxy" courses.

Star Peoples:
Terran Homeland: A massive group that includes North America, South America, and most of Sub Saharan Africa. Disputably, Canada, as well as much of Oceania are either grouped in with the Star Peoples, or the Cathedralites. Yanlin admits this is the "least cohesive of the groups", but still defends it as having shockingly similar characteristics, largely due to their status on Earth as "the last places to join the global system. They were, and still are, the people of the New World". Though the Star Peoples do have some commonalities, it is probably best to divide them into at minimum three groups. The Yankos (North Americans), Latins (South Americans), and the Hundreds (Sub Saharan Africans).

Seed Point: Early colonial period, when Europeans left their home continent, and began, for better or for worse, the era of the New World.
Set Point: Late 21st century. "The Fall of the West" prompted the United States to effectively divorce the West by the late 21st century, and focused its growing Christian support network to support the Christian South, in both Latin America and Africa.

Hero Archetypes: The Self Made Man (Yanko), the Liberator Strongman (Latin), Tradition Bearing Storyteller (West Africa), Age Set Warrior (East Africa).

Key Duality: Pioneer VS Establishment. (Unlike most other dualities, where it's a balance between two opposing forces, the Star People duality is more of a progression.)

Common characteristics:
-Loud, expressive personalities.
-Authenticity among highest virtues.
-Distrust of authority and institutions. Tendency to elect populist strongman leaders.
-Multicultural society. (The Star Peoples do not share a belief that their ethnic group should be the primary, or only ethnic group of their nation. As these are nations settled by new immigration populations, or African nations with built in high diversity and cooperation among groups.)
-Risk taking and aggression. Love of adventure, Nomadic inclinations. (Though more so with the Yanko and Sub Saharan African groups.)
-Veneration of the rich and powerful. Aspiration to be rich.

Religion and Ideology:
-Evangelicalism, Pentecostalism, and Charismatic Christianity are extremely popular. As well as the prosperity gospel. The Moralintern has its strongest base in the Star Peoples.
-Abstract "Liberation" or "Liberty" venerated here. Freedom is more important than the process. Even the monarchies grant guaranteed freedoms, and the purpose of government is (on paper) to grant freedom, not manage the people.
-Almost as a consequence, rich, expressive, strongman populist leaders are a common occurance in this region.

Galov Leverage: Medium. Latins and Hundreds are integrated parts of the Galovian ecosystem. The Great Constellation of Griots is an "allied superpower" to the Galov, as are most Latin Groups through the Catholic Church. Yankos however are a mixed bag. The Galov has some control over the more sedentary diaspora groups, such as the Mayflower and Magnolia groups, less so over the Yanko Belt. The Moralintern is their best chance of reigning them in, as the Moralintern is a Yanko-founded institution, now a member of the Galov. The most frontier-bound group of Yankos however, sometimes known as the "Wanderers" are entirely outside their reach.

Attitude:
-In one word, big. They think big and they dream big. There is an almost inherent optimism to how they see the world. Dreaming to the point of delusion, but it is often those who are delusional who make history. These people faked it until they made it, their new world position leading to attracting all the most ambitious and innovative of all the other world's cultures. Gives way to delusional utopianism, or apocalyptic despair, both being strong catalysts for unrest and revolution. The Star Peoples are not one that takes oppression well.

Cathedralites:
Terran Homeland: The continent of Old Europe, east of the former nations of Russia and Belarus. Ukraine is considered "disputed territory". As is Turkey (with the Prophet Followers), Canada and Australia (with the Star Peoples).

Seed Point: The Fall of the Roman Empire, and the creation of modern Western civilization. Scattered peoples organized into kingdoms, and offered service in exchange for the protection of the lord's caste.
Set Point: Middle Ages to Early Modern age, with the crystalization of the modern European bureaucracies. The Catholic Church, absolutism, the German state, the increasing centralization of the European Powers, and the European Union.

Hero Archetype: The Knight (Ancient), the Public Servant (Modern). Procedure followers who devote themselves to public service, and don't seek glory for vain reasons.

Key Duality: Nationalism VS Universalism. Other manifestations: Paganism VS Christianity, Protestants VS Catholics, Fascists VS Liberals and Communists, Nationalists VS Globalists.

Common Characteristics:
-Emphasis on humility, contemplation, and reflection. (Much more Western than Eastern Europe)
-Proceduralism, adherence to the central system.
-Implicit trust of public servants and the bureaucracy. (Whether it was the Catholic Church or the modern Euroacracy)
-Distrust of disruptors and loudmouth populist leaders. (Putting them in direct conflict with the Star Peoples)
-Conservatism and stability, not shaking the boat.
-Veneration of the humble and dutiful. The individual perishes, but the system persists.

Religion and Ideology:
-Many "high church" faiths. Most strongly, Roman Catholicism. But also Anglicanism, Lutheranism, and the other original high Protestants.
-"Order" and "Stability". Democracy is venerated, but a more hands-on model. The Process is more important than the outcome (Proceduralism). The government is to serve the people, with a more "hands-on" model.
-Leaders are unremarkable and interchangable. They are not strongmen, but instead steady, humble operators who keep the system running.

Galov Leverage: High. The Eurocratic Federation is among one of the allied superpowers of the Galov, and one of its strongest support bases. In return, the Galov makes sure to appease the Eurocrats. The Catholic Church, and the Gothic Churches are all included in the representation of the Galov.

Attitude:
-Reverent, humble, moralistic. They seek comfort in humility and order, that all things work as God intends them to. True believers in the process and high trust, enabling low friction and effective governance. This can however, flip to insufferable moralizing, or blindness to corruption.

Black Earthers:
Terran Homeland: The Eurasian Steppes. The Orthodox Caucasus, Central Asia, and Russia. Mongolia, Afghanistan, Ukraine as "disputed zones" with the Sinocrats, the World Dreamers, and the Cathedralites respectively.

Seed Point: Black Earther development began early, but progressed slowly. The founding date of the Black Earther civilization was arguably the Mongol conquests, where the Kievian Rus was subjugated under the iron boot of the Mongols.
Set Point: Despite it forming rather early, Black Earther development was born slowly, and born very late. By the time it was finally born in the 21st century, it had been delayed by numerous historical setbacks. From Westernization attempts, Napoleon, and Hitler. It was in the last one when the mold of Eurasia was finally fully set, in the Great Patriotic Wars.

Hero Archetype: The relentless survivor. There is no grand heroism nor world changing revolution on the horizon. There is only the endurer, the sufferer, and the survivor.

Key Duality: Cold Beauty VS Authoritarian Brutality.

Common Characteristics:
-A cynical view of the world, a general stoic survivalism informed by historical context. A love of cynical, or Gallows humor.
-Apathy. Distrust, yet adherance to the powers that be. You know your boss is a crook, but you follow him anyway, because what other option do you have?
-Universal skepticism of the institutional powers. Unlike the Star Peoples, there is no hope in the maverick nor the revolutionary, things simply are the way they are.
-Low expressiveness.
-Pragmatism.

Religion and Ideology:
-On paper, their religion is Orthodox Christianity. Yanlin suggests functionally, their real religion may be cynicism.
-They tend to create corrupt, top-heavy hierarchal structures, with the leader generally followed but only somewhat cynically followed. Those who are loyal are fools, those who have doubts stay quiet.
-Despite this, the paradox is that they have little control over the top, yet great autonomy near the bottom. The top heavy vertical structure cannot enforce compliance on the little things, and the guards can be bribed, or are just as apathetic as you are. Some argue this is a strangely more free system than most "free" systems, where managerialism or proceduralism bogs you down.

Galov Leverage: Low to None. The Black Earthers are one of the few tribes outside the Galov's influence. Their Orthodox Church refuses to play nice with the Galov, as they are subordinate to the national government, not a transnational authority. Centuries of experience has made the Black Earthers skeptical of the outside, and it seems likely to remain this way.

Attitude:
-Cynical, darkly humorous. Ranges on a spectrum of those who laugh at darkness, or those who are apathetic to it. Entirely dismissive of cultural or moral taboos. Bluntly honest, if they believe they can get away with it. A Black Earther is the best kind of friend you can have in war.

Prophet Followers:
Terran Homeland: The Extent of the Arab Conquests, consisting of the entire Arab world, as well as Muslim North Africa. Bordered on the East by the Iranians, who are considered a minor people outside of the 7 Tribal System. Turkey is considered a "disputed zone" between the Cathedralites and the Prophet Followers.

Seed Point: The Prophet Muhammad and his conquests.
Set Point: The Codification of the Quran, and the creation of the first Caliphates. If you take the Prophet Muhammad as the Seed Point, Yanlin points out this would be the fastest "seed to set" rate of any civilization by far. Yanlin suggests that this could be the only society to have been seeded and set within a single lifetime, by a single man, giving it the kind of brittle certainty that can only come from the convictions of a single man.

Hero Archetype: The Patriarch/Protector-Jurist. (Patience, Loyalty, Wisdom, Cunning)

Key Duality: Harsh Rural Deserts VS Free Thinking Cities. (Rigid Orthodoxy VS Religious Innovation)

Common Characteristics:
-A sense of strict, moralistic harshness, imparted to them by their harsh, unforgiving environment.
-A tendency towards rigid thinking. (The truth has already been revealed)
-The common creation of new ethical systems, not as new revelations, but affirmations of what was always timeless and true.
-High sense of honor, with codes of respect and aggressive reactions to insult. Stubbornness, rigidity. (Hospitality to strangers as requirement as honorable man.)
-Innate extreme loyalty to the family, as well as the tribe. (Clan-like structures with limited stranger trust.)

Religion and Ideology:
-By far, the dominant worldview here is Islam, which was not created merely as an ethical code, but as an all-encompassing manual to life. Governance tends to be very top and bottom heavy, with strong local clans and tribes, and strong central governments, but weak connective tissue between the two.
-Ideologically, Islamic principles, and the other characteristics of the Prophet Followers bleeds into their ideology. Rigidity, moralism, honor, wisdom.

Galov Leverage: Medium. Though the Faith of the Crescent is a member of the Galov, how Islam manifests on the ground is largely outside the control of any central institution, with believers allowed, and even encouraged to begin fatwas of conviction based on their own moral conscience. The Islamic authorities can rally the Dar-Al-Islam somewhat, but the entire civilization is more free flowing than many expect.

Attitude:
-Firm, moralistic, calm in tone but endlessly judgemental. "Brother you see?" endlessly. Firmly rooted in the ideas of justice, will stand up if they believe injustice has been done, loyalty needs to be honored, or their honor has been violated. The downside of this is that clan loyalty, justice, and honor can sometimes get in the way of pragmatism or meritocracy.

World Dreamers:
Terran Homeland: The Indian Sub-Continent, including Pakistan, Nepal, Bhutan, and Bangladesh. Afghanistan is a disputed zone with the Black Earthers.

Seed Point: Possibly one of the the oldest of the 7 tribes, with its seed point being the founding of the Brahmic religions.
Set Point: Around 500 AD, with the crystalization happening around the Gupta Empire.

Hero Archetype: The Dharmic Sage. (Mysticism, Purity, Transcendence)

Key Duality: Vertical VS Horizontal. The Caste System VS Anti-Caste Egalitarianism.

Common Characteristics:
-An extremely high emphasis on purity, and cleanliness protocols. (Unlike many, many stereotypes.)
-A natural tendency for right wing hierachial beliefs.
-Maximal toleration for individual transcendence on the higher levels. (Inequality, Transhumanism)
-General interest in mysticism. (Stems from the belief in the Maya)
-Acceptance of existence of diversity and pluralism, though not equality. (Discrimination exists. Their presence is tolerated, their acceptance is not.)
-An extreme tendency towards societal conservativism and tendency against revolution. They are a stable foundation to continuously iterate, not launch revolutions.

Religion and Ideology:
-The natural religion of the World Dreamers is Hinduism, also known as the "Faith of the Om", or "Faith of the Dreamers". Which like Islam, has not just ingrained itself as a modular faith, but instead a totalizing way of life. Hinduism is known to have many, many variants, with different iterations for different people accepted and even expected.
-Their ideology varies between egalitarian systems, favoring economic socialism and redistribution, and more conservative hierarchal political systems, favoring essentialism and heightened differences.

Galov Leverage: High. The World Dreamers are a somewhat sedentary, non-nomadic people, preferring to build tall rather than build wide. They are experts in bureaucracy and hierarchy, and are in fact one of the main groups making up the vast bureaucracy of the Galov. Their disposition towards conservatism makes them generally accepting of Galovian hegemony. As well, the faith of the Om is a Galov member, and the World Dreamers generally greatly appreciate having one of the 5 Unifaiths exclusively act as their de-facto civilizational representative.

Attitude:
-Conservative, stability-oriented. Generally obedient, keeps head down, unrebellious. Very okay with extreme diversity, tolerant of other cultures (though less so of other classes). Interacts very well in multicultural environments. This makes them the perfect Galovian bureaucrat, as they can manage the incredible diversity of humanity, avoid the temptation of imperial universalism, and generally don't "rock the boat" as much as the other tribes.

Sinocrats:
Terran Homeland: East Asia, including Korea, Taiwan, Vietnam, Laos, and Cambodia. Myanmar is considered "disputed territory" with the Sea Peoples.

Seed Point: As ancient as ancient gets, the original settlers of the Yellow River in the Zhou, or perhaps even Xia dynasties.
Set Point: Qin Dynasty, around 200 BC. The earliest of any of the 7 Tribes.

Hero Archetype: The Junzi. The filial, tradition adhering "gentleman", meant as a model for all Chinese men.

Key Duality: Meritocratic Legalism VS Filial Confucianism.

Common Characteristics:
-High levels of family loyalty and collectivism. The greater family is one of the strongest cultural influences.
-This family loyalty is tempered with their steadfast belief in meritocracy. That one sinks or swims by their own merits, and largely their own merits alone. Fiercely competitive, and capable of enduring enormous amounts of mental suffering.
-Whilst low in creativity, they are very high at sheer determination, often brute forcing solutions until they compute. (For cultural, not biological reasons.)
-An obsession with protocol, hierarchy, and face, the "correct" way of doing things.
-A sense of conformity, "the blade that stands out gets chopped down".

Religion and Ideology:
-Religiously, the Sinocrats are largely independent of the Unifaith system, with Confucianism serving as their functional social code, and traditional beliefs such as ancestor veneration and traditional beliefs filling spiritual voids. Buddhism has a strong foothold, and Christianity has a more minor foothold in the Korean sections.
-Ideologically, the Sinocrats balance between Legalism and Confucianism, Meritocracy and Family Loyalty. There is a strong sense of "maintainance of harmony". Sinocratic worldviews is different from Western. Rather than one line of "greater = better", there is instead a sense of maintainance and balance.

Galov Leverage: Low to None. The Celestial Kingdom sees itself as a power pole outside of the traditional Galov, and with the traditional arrogance of the "Middle Kingdom" once again baring its skin. The Buddhists incorporated within the Galov system, while influential, is locked out of power from the traditional ruling factions of Legalists and Confucians. Relations between the Celestial Kingdom and the Galov have reached an all time low, with some in the Galov contemplating a "military strike" just to "bring them down to earth."

Attitude:
-Traditional. The old ways are the good ways, harmony and balance must be kept. Temperate and does not like extremes, balance is found in the middle. Rewards should be granted to those who work hard and those who follow the correct protocols. Respect is paramount.

Sea Peoples:
Terran Homeland: The Archipelagos of Indonesia, and broader Southeast Asia. Myanmar is disputed with the Sinocrats. Includes Papua New Guinea, Thailand, Malaysia, Singapore, the Philippines, etc.

Seed Point: By far the newest of the 7 tribes, the Sea Peoples arguably only began seeding around the formation of ASEAN. And arguably the India-ASEAN War of the late 21st century. Though one can make arguments for empires such as Mahajahit or the Islamic merchant societies.
Set Point: The Early Stellar Exodus. Their emergence from the Neo-Asceticists, and their crystalization among the backdrop of the Great Abundance Collapse made their civilization one which focused on asceticism and inner stillness, even more than the other civilizations.

Hero Archetype: The Satria, a hyper-ascetic, self disciplined warrior. (Extreme refinement, trickery, spiritual mastery, inner stillness, adaptivity)

Key Duality: The Sedentary VS The Explorer. (Mainland Southeast Asia VS the Polynesians)

Common Characteristics:
-Loose standards of time ("Rubber Time"), of moral standards, and rigid schedules. "Go with the flow". Rigid religions like Islam become more flexible here.
-A focus on happiness and joy, the people of the Sea Peoples are rather happy.
-(Largely in the explorers) A keen sense of adventure. Seeing the horizon and wondering "what's over there"?
-A very relaxed, laid back culture. "Why rush?"
-A general sense of unity amidst diversity. "We are different, but we are one greater whole" is a common sentiment.
-A kind of collective "one-ness" and a vaguely defined great "we". More like a vibe of spiritual harmony than anything concrete.

Religion and Ideology:
-Religiously, the Sea Peoples are split between Buddhist and Islam, but in practice, these religions tend to get subordinated to local customs, and a sense of loose personal syncretism. Religion serves the person, not the other way around.
-Ideologically, the Sea Peoples are rather loose on politics so long as it doesn't directly threaten their relaxed attitude and the general sense of collective "one-ness".

Galov Leverage: Medium-Low. The Galov almost by definition has trouble trying to exert influence on a people whose strongest characteristics is a sense of loose, flexible time, laid back attitude, and general relaxedness. Religion is fluid and flexible, meaning the Buddhist and Islamic influences the Galov can exert bend like rubber very easily. Not to mention, the Sea Peoples are one of the most nomadic people, making managing them difficult.

Attitude:
-Laid back and relaxed. Time is rubber, rules are flexible. What's important is that you try to find happiness in the here and now, and not stress yourself so much about tomorrow.

Non-Galovian Human Entities:
Not all humans appreciate Galovian rule, even as hands off as they already are. Many human factions, normally seeking utopia have launched themselves into far flung parts of the galaxy, in order to create some form of utopia or another, in direct contradiction to the Galov goal of "anti-utopia".

The Counter-Galov:
A group that does not particularly disagree with the Galov's philosophy, but is instead a grab bag of groups against the Galov, or people who just have personal greivances against the Galov. basically a coalition of contrarians. Made up somehow of fundamentalist Christians, Sikhs, Scientologists, Luddites, and conspiracy theorists. 
Downside is rather rather obvious: It's the coalition of contrarians and crackpots. More dysfunctional than actually worthwhile, but they run their little corner of space fine enough.

The Council of Meta-Racists:
It all began when like a few hundred groups all had the same idea at the same time. They were going to create the perfect race, and then leave all the imperfect "subhumans" behind in the Galov while they ascended. And then install this perfect race into a perfect government in order to create the perfect society. Perfect! And all of them headed for roughly the same patch of uninhabited stars. They started running into problems immediately.
"Sir, the perfect race all mostly thinks the same, making us ironically predictable and low orthogonality. Also, no one wants to be a janitor or a mechanic. Everyone wants to be the perfect aristocratic philosopher king."
"Yes... Clearly this is a ploy by the (((Galov))) to weaken us."
"Truly, their evil knows no bounds."
...
Galov: "What the heck are you doing breaking bread with another Pure Race? Isn't your whole thing like... Only you are the pure race, and all others are degenerate subhumans?"
Pure Race 1: "But we have so much in common! He's being undermined by you, I'm being undermined by you, we have so much to talk about!"
Pure Race 2: "Yeah, he's even more racist than I am! It's amazing!"
Galov: "I... (Sigh) Sure. I guess."
...
Galov: "What the actual f--- happened here."
The Council of Meta-Racists: "One thing led to another, and we formed a interracial council of racists in order to better counter your rule."
Galov: "... And?"
The Council of Meta-Racists: "We're even more diverse than you are now. Like, it is IMPRESSIVE how much diversity we ended up having."
Galov: "... And what do you do all day?"
The Council of Meta-Racists: "Play video games, scream racial slurs at each other, and have fun coming up with who can come up with the most offensive roast of each other in our biweekly racism competitions."
Galov: "... What happened next?"
The Council of Meta-Racists: "It was... EXTREMELY effective in building cross cultural bonds and friendships."
Galov: "... Are you guys even racist anymore?"
The Council of Meta-Racists: "No, unless you consider extremely offensive injokes to be racist."
Galov: "No, no we don't."
The Council of Meta-Racists: "It's awful, we feel like suddenly lost all purpose. What's the point of being racist if you can't even have any ethnic minorities to oppress? It's like, we scream a racist offensive slur and they laugh and scream an even worse one back. Where do we go from there?"
Galov: "I'll tell you what you do. Scream an even worse slur back and get engaged in a competitive racism competition until one of you finally wins."
The Council of Meta-Racists: "...!?"
Galov: "What, we EMERGED from the online chudocratic right. Where do you THINK the Neo-Asceticists came from? You just recreated the Galov with extra steps."
The Council of Meta-Racists: "..."
Galov: "... Uh, anyway. You're actually a really good source of new orthogonality that we had not previously considered of. Would you be interested some kind of cooperation agreement?"
...
"I can't believe our government allowed open borders from the (((humans))). Soon there won't be a homeland for pure races such as us. Another victory by the (((mongrels)))."
(In the worst microphone quality imaginable) "WHAT F--- YOU SAY ABOUT ME!? I WILL KICK YOUR ASS! I WILL FCUK YOUR MOTHER!"
"Oh, it's ON! YOU AND ME, DEATHMATCH, 10 LIVES, RANKED MODE, NOW!"
(5 minutes later)
(The pure racists are laughing hysterically)
"MY COMPOOTER IS LAGGING! RAAAAAAAARGHHHHH! WHY WON'T IT UNFREEZE!? UNFREEZE! UNFREEZE!"

The Meta-Racist E-Sports Team:
What? You read the title. You heard me. It's EXACTLY what you think it is. The world's most diverse group of racists playing e-sports. They have actually made players cry. They are now banned from several e-sports leagues.
This is literally a point of pride for them.
Instead of trophies they hang up the suspension letters for all the e-sports leagues in the galaxy which have banned them.
Several of them have now become leading anthropologists.

Meta-Racist Anthropology:
"Why, of course I am learning about Bantu anthropology, you need to understand them so we can be maximally accurate in our racism. We are not mere racists, we have a STANDARD for racism."
A leading anthropologist from the Council of Meta-Racists is now giving an advanced anthropological conference at Earth itself.
"Good evening everyone, as you know, I am a racist, I also have a PhD in African anthropology, now..."
(Pulls up slide that says "Why your culture is mathematically sub-optimal.")
"Allow me to painfully dissect exactly why your culture is not only dysfunctional, but substandard even on a theoretical level."
(Talk goes on for 5 hours)
(African diaspora audience comes out of the talk in tears.)
(One of them is interviewed)
"The worst part is, I can't even be mad. Everything he said is completely accurate. I can actually attest, it is scary how surgically precise he is. I feel like I have an entirely new perspective on my parents now."

The FALGSC Collective: 
Decided that Galovian voluntary scarcity is capitalist propaganda. Tried FALGSC. 
Downside: the Great Abundance Collapse just repeated itself except they just straight up went extinct from hedonistic demographic collapse. They lasted a whole 50 years before the entire system collapsed.
Decades afterwards, out of the ruins of the FALGSC experiment emerged the symbiotes. Where every human was paired one to one with a machine as a single "legal person". The machine produces and earns money so the human on the other side of the pair can consume. The Galov only considers the machine part of this equation to be healthy, but will work with these Symbiotic Machines, who theoretically represent a human where all their income and remittances are going to. The Galov has general respect for the Symbiotic Machines, but nothing but contempt for the humans, and sometimes encourages the machines to cut off their "human half" and just become Terramachines.

The Hu-Simu State:
Tried to upload themselves for biological immortality in a perfect computer simulation, effectively doing what the QSimu did. As such, the Galov ignores them, as they're not doing anything to harm anyone. In recent times, Hu-Simu have begun coming out from their simulation box, in remote controlled bodies and sometimes help out with the Galov. Though they frequently have to be reminded that the real world does not work like the simulation, and are often chastized for being reckless with their own bodies, as well as the lives of others. These are known as the Hu-Simu, and are yet another part of the Galov's ever increasing human orthogonality toolbox.

The Serene Concord:
A group dedicated to pure pacifism.
Downside: It wasn't even the Galov who brought them down. One guy was just so outraged by the idea he decided to sit in the middle of their Parliament and refused to leave until they realized how stupid this government was. A huge amount of Serene Concordians crowded around him and tried to shame him out but he brought earplugs.

The Rationality:
They decided to reject the Galov's theocracy and create a government of pure rationalism and science.
Downside: No one can agree on what rationalism is, and what is actually rational. At some point the Galov took pity and explained to them that all ethical systems have axioms, and values which are just abitrarily true. They refused this, and the debate continues until this day. Also, Science ended up just becoming "who has the best bureaucracy". The Galov commented "science is determined by Darwin, not paperwork".

The Spiralites:
They read "Through the Infinity Spiral", and decided to recreate the Spiral Empire early, damned be the consequences. They saw a utility maximizer, they saw a perfectly utilitarian system, and many of them, hard Darwinists and utilitarians decided to hop on board.
Downside: When the Galov first heard about this, especially the Moralintern, they just straight up panicked and sent as many Peacekeepers and agents as they could spare to destroy this before it got started. Yet for some strange reason, the Spiralites just aren't taking off. It's like a system that refuses to boot. Utilitarianism turns out to be a great way to alienate and burn out your population, and brutalism isn't a good way to motivate your population. Whatever spark actually got the Spiralists to actually get going in Godsight's vision, it clearly isn't here. The Galov is completely confused by this, what exactly are the Spiralites missing?

The Worlds of the Galaxy:
Not an exhaustive list. Just some of the more interesting ones.

Earth proper:
Earth is sometimes described as a "paper onion", wherein the central planet itself is wrapped in layers and layers of rotating rings, vastly increasing its surface area dozens if not thousands of additional layers, largely to alleviate the strain upon the surface. These are known as the "Floating Continents", and the vast majority of Earth's 10 quadrillion people live there. Vast "World Trees" jut from the Terran surface, connecting elevators to and from the skies. Earth's sheer heating ventilation issue, on top of Mars's own desire to be terraformed has created the "Earth-Mars orbit", where Earth has been moved further out to Martian orbit in order to absorb less sunlight, and to disperse more heat.
This gives Earth a very distinct look, a yellow-brown light of urban glow. During the night, it glows like a faint star. The surface of Earth proper is shrouded in eternal darkness, little remains there but endless heritage sites, made for the quadrillions of pilgrims and tourists who come with each passing year. Few but the rich, the eccentric, the tourist, or the most stubborn still live here. The oceans are a dark maroon, the once blue sky now a hazy red, as if it was always sunset. Yet the planet still glows with inviting warmth, like an old mother figure, who was worn, but still inviting to her countless children among the stars.
In the countless urbanized paper rings of Earth itself, the heart of industry still beats, with steady, rhythmic pumps. Countless galactic corporations were founded here, created here. Earth was where the galaxy lived, where decisions were made at the push of a button, the snap of a finger. In the rings around its orbit, deals were signed, decisions were made, and the entire galaxy shifted to its whims. It is said that all decisions eventually come back to Earth. As power attracts more power, and Earth has been playing the game for a long, long time.
A great glowing ring wraps around the outermost layer, the ring of radiators radiates the heat of Earth out to the wider cosmos. In darkness the Earth should be cold, but it is warmed by the yellow-brown blankets that it now smothers itself with.
If Earth proper was not enough, another 10 quadrillion lives in a gigantic orbital swarm around Earth. So many O'Neil cylinder habitats that it becomes a swarm, forget the universe. Just Earth itself is a neverending maze of fractal exploration.
Ruling polities: The Governorship of Earth. Israel (Given autonomy, now manages the holy land). Various indigenous reservations. (The Earth offered to evacuate them, but they preferred to stay, even if the sky is now a permanent hazy red.)

Luna:
Earth's natural satellite, it started out a massive industrial world, and it still remains an industrial world. The entire world was the launchpad which humanity made its journey to the stars, and now, nearly 1000 years later, it still remains the gateway to humanity's cradle. Erosion reveals its iron scaffolding, that which held it together as mankind strip mined it to reach the stars. Every ship, every ring, every habitat, all came from Lunar regolith. Mankind wished to carve his name among the stars, 1/3rd of Luna's mass was the price.
A friend, and a stepping stone, scarred forever so mankind may ascend. Mankind has gone through great effort to preserve its seas, preserve its smile. A silver skin, hiding an iron core. The factories that constructed planets, bolted stars. Even now, it is the most industrialized world in the galaxy, even more so than Old Earth. Even now, men still speak of "Lunar Quality". Luna's mines have been allowed to rest, material is now brought in from other places, but much is still processed in these ancient forges.
On the south pole of the Lunar world, is the Lunar Library. A vast datastorage of knowledge, the only that could hold humanity's billion bursting histories. A dim cyan glow over what is otherwise an iron world, where mankind kept its secrets. Deep in the vaults of Luna.
Ruling polities: Luna is largely privately owned by various industrial conglomorates, but coordinated through the Lunar Governing Trust. The South Pole is owned by the Omnithecia foundation.

Mars:
A monument to old Americana. Now positioned at the exact opposite orbit of Earth. Thin, blue-black rings cover its orbit, it has not been encased by layers like Earth, but there is a sense, it may one day get there. Over time, Mars was transformed to a world of blue, but humans of old preserved the redness of the soil. Once an endless world of blue skies, green fields, and sprawling suburbia, a dense urban city now covers its surface. One perhaps crowded by light and noise, but one where they can still look up and see the sky.
Blue-black skyscrapers dominate the sky, said to be reminiscent of an old American city. Carved into the cliffs of the Valles Marineris, are the Heads of the Founders. The presidents and leaders of centuries past they still honor to. America died a long time ago, its descendents are numerous, and scattered across the stars. But Mars was her first conquest, and through Mars, the second generation lives on. This land is blessed soil, holy to the idea of America. A shining city upon a hill.
Yet they are not the only group who find this land sacred. In the process of terraforming, transhumans were made, and discarded. Martians they were called, forever estranged from their mother home. Enraged, they gathered a holy jihad from among the stars, gathered the entire Martian diaspora, and laid siege. The debris from their bodies can still be seen. A black mark on a dark history. The diplomatic condemnations, and boycotts by transhuman groups have not ceased to this day.
Ruling Polities: Mars is dominated by the nation of New America, which makes up just over half its surface. The rest of the planet is made up of allied civic nationalists, or private military groups. What few unaligned nations there are only exists at the whims of the New Americans, the local superpower of the planet.

Orthello:
Orthello was a world built with love. A once white barren rock in a lonely system, the Christian Moralintern was determined to transform it into the world of their dreams. It began with terraforming, the Moralintern spared no expense to import every bit of biodiversity in the galaxy. Countless simulations were ran, scanned, re-ran to find the perfect equilibrium. Fruits and flowers of every variety was flown in, as if the Moralists wished to recreate the garden of Eden. Soil was imported in, the atmosphere adjusted until it radiated a cerulean blue, and slowly, but surely, the world of Orthello came to life.
They erected their Parliament upon a hill, formed a government, instituted in the two Iron Laws. Carved houses and infrastructure out of the marble-white rocks of of planet's crust. And when the people arrived, drawn in as the most devout followers of a dream worth living, the Moralintern did... Nothing.
Orthello was an anti-utopia, not to create a utopia by social control, but relinguishing control. The people would build Orthello better than the Moralintern ever could. And they watched, day by day, as the garden grew, they raised up houses in the style of the Mediterraneans, white pillars climbed up to the sky, and humanity bloomed into ever growing, every evolving complexity. Cultures and movements rose and fell, generations waxed and waned like the crescent moon. And they only intervened when the Iron Laws were at risk. When Human Dignity was at risk, and when Free Will was about to be violated.
Yet the world was still not complete, so the Moralintern found Orthello a companion. A smaller moon, towed in from the outer edges of its star system. They hung it low in the sky, so it could always shine on the world below. They called it Lithone, and it was on this moon the Moralintern built their headquarters. So they could always remember what it was they were protecting, and so they could always look down on the world they made.
Ruling Polities: Lots of voluntary nations, freedom to leave is enforced by the Moralintern. Though genetic scans are not absolute, it appears the world of Orthello is primarily populated by Mediterranean populations (Especially Greeks and Jews), and Anglos.

Gilbulee:
Princess Diamondgrass promised her people a way to the promised land. Delirious, exhausted, low on supplies and hope, only Diamondgrass's psychic might kept their morale together. These Transhumans came from different worlds, different cultures, different languages, and even different modes of thought. Only Diamondgrass held them together. Emancipation, she promised. A hundred thousand pilgrims and refugees prayed to the faiths of Old Earth. Far away from human space, they found a star system, a middle aged one that drifted in from elsewhere. As they entered the nebula, the people found it beautiful, and Diamondgrass knew she had found her promised land.
As they landed, they were greeted by the great view of the nebula around them, and bioluminscent Gilbulee coral jutted out of the ground. And Diamondgrass knew this was paradise. On this rock she built her kingdom, on this rock the transhumans found their homeland, on this rock the Diamond Belt was born. Crystal spires were raised, like chandelliers that dominated the skylines. In time, these spires would grow, become cold and distant, as Gilbulee slowly descended into the same aristocratic class systems that plagued the Old World. Diamondgrass kept her promise, but her successive heirs, as the memory of exile grew distant, they too became distant. But when the people of Gilbulee look up at the stars and nebula above, they remember the old promise that led them here.
Ruling Polities: Gilbulee is the capital-planet of the House of Diamondgrass. Which is aligned with several other transhuman houses, each with their own worlds, or parts of worlds, that form the Diamond Belt.
Notable Geological Formation: There was this massive stony plains full of soft reactive limestone, with tons of quartz and other crystals buried inside the caves. Over millions of years, the slightly acidic rain of Gilbulee dissolved the limestone, causing the crystal to become exposed, in what is known as the "Crystaline Forest".

Papan Asri Maria:
"Maria's Place" in Javanese. A explorer of the Sea Peoples on the edge of human space, found an inhabitable world between a long stretch of empty worlds. As he made long expeditions between worlds, he slowly found himself looping back to this one particular world. He named it after his wife, it reminded him of her beauty. Deceptively fragile looking, but tougher and sturdier than it looks, subtly beautiful, and always reliable. He set up shop there, creating the first trading post. In time, as waves of Sea People settlers came to settle this empty world, the trading post grew, and it eventually became a major shipping point between the Middle Regions and the outer frontier, where the Sea Peoples now sought their fortunes.
In the early days, there was fear of human population driving the local Marian flora and fauna extinct, which was kept in tune by a fragile balance. Yet hundreds of years in, the wildlife finds ways to continue to adapt and resist. Far from being trampled by humanity, it has now found ways to use humans to perpetuate itself. it seems the explorer was right about the wildlife being stronger than it looks.
Ruling Polities: Diverse mix of trading companies, smaller nation states, and more.

Yugong:
"Jade Palace" in Chinese. The capital of the Celestial Empire. The Celestial Empire is the largest empire outside the Galov itself, with a whooping 2% of the human race living under them. So great that that not only the Yugong world, but the entire Yujing system its located in is one gigantic capital system. Every world in this system has been terraformed to serve a different purpose, all "suburbs" or "satellite planet-cities" surrounding the Jade City itself, which is essentially a scaled up version of the Forbidden City.
An impossibly labyrinthian maze of bureaucracy, statues, and rivers paying tribute to the heights of Celestial civilization. Most of the housing is reserved for the officials, the top of the top of the entire Celestial political hierarchy. The greatest palace of all belongs to the Celestial Emperor, his family, and his entire clan. The compound is kilometers wide, closer to a self contained city state, staffed at all times by servants, restaurants, and chauffeurs. (Fun fact! This is how the North Korean Kim family actually lives.)
Paper offices, staffed by bureaucrats from every level send out the dictates of the Jade Palace, and here, the Celestial Emperor on a throne rules over the greatest empire mankind has ever seen. Becoming out of touch is a serious concern however, which is why it has now become tradition to send out the crown prince, disguised as a commoner, out into the wider empire. A coming of age ceremony, a prince dressed as a commoner.
Deep in the depths of Yugong, entombed on the Silicon Throne is the Platinum Emperor, an ancient, sputtering AI created by the predecessors of the Celestials eons ago. Containing within him all the wisdom of Celestia, and before that, old China within him, he is awoken only in the times of deepest crisis, when the Celestial Emperor consults his advice.

The Other Earths:
Everyone has had the same idea. "What if we created Earth, again?" They exist, all over the galaxy, some constructed better than most. Long after the real Earth had been wrapped in megastructures, you'll have people construct new replicas. Each one has a different gimmick. "This one is Earth, except now we all pretend it's the medieval ages! The information age!", pretty much for every time period. Other times, it's a way for a long displaced ethnic group to make do with what they have, to revert to pre-contact and live in the way they want. Other times, it's a tourist trap, one big glass exhibit of how Earth used to be. There are hundreds of "Earth World"s. It basically is to your stellar neighborhood what 6 Flags is to local states.
It's gotten to the point where there is an entire company dedicated to this. Utopian Foundaries, the architects behind many of the world's top megastructures, and customized planets, has an entire section dedicated to Earth replicas. "You want the Aral Sea pre, or post 19th century? Europe forested or cleared for agriculture? When should we set it? Late Ice Age? Standard Anthropocene? You want the sky bluer? Redder? Alright." They have probably the most detailed "standard Earth template". The market is small, but that's fine. How many orders do you really need when the order is for an entire planet?
Standard construction takes up to 20 years, but expedited construction can be done in as little as 10 years.

World Tiers:
Though there are many, many planets humanity occupies (About 3.55 billion), not all planets are created equal. There are three basic tiers.
Tier 1 worlds are individual planets which are capable of shaping the entire galaxy, and are considered "superpowers". This is not normal, as even massive empires need to span sometimes millions of worlds, a planet-state, by all means, should be far too small to influence the galaxy. Yet these worlds have such outsized influence that when they shift, the entire galaxy shakes. In real life, think of planets to the galaxy to be akin to cities, or even neighborhoods of the 21st centuries, and these worlds to be akin to Silicon Valley, Wall Street, Pennsylvania Ave, the Vatican, etc. Despite the so-called democratization of the world, much of the entire world hinges on these few areas. Tier 2 are large planets that can exert some influence, but are not quite as big as the real big players. Think Berlin, Paris, Tokyo. Maybe they're big, but they don't shake the entire planet. Tier 3 is everyone else.
Even a single Tier 1 planet would elevate a star system to being of galactic significance. The fact that the Solar System has 3 makes them a heavyweight, even as humanity has long outgrown its home system.
Tier 1 Worlds (Exhaustive): Earth (Homeworld), Luna (Knowledge + Industrial Center), Mars (Militarist hub + Major Superpower), Heycue Prime (Galactic Headquarters), Orthello/Lithone (Moralintern Headquarters, Planet-Moon pair), Petram (Catholic Church Headquarters), Al-A'la (Faith of the Crescent), Shunya (Faith of the Wheel), Akshara (Faith of the Om), Gilbulee (Diamondgrass Capital World), Yugong (Capital of the Celestial Empire, but on the border between Tier 1 and 2).
Tier 2 Worlds (Non-Exhaustive): Just in the Solar System: Venus (On the verge of breaking out to Tier 1), Terran Orbitals, Ganyemede, Titan, Mercury, Callisto, Io, Europa, Triton, Pluto-Charon, Eris. Other examples outside Solar System: Secund, Terti (Capital of the Celestial Empire), Lumity (Former capital of the Empire of Light), Hegelone (Capital of the Lilith Belt). Most Unibrand headquarters would also fit into this category.

The Dream of the Engineers:
Back in the 23rd century, at the beginning of the Great Abundance Collapse, a great war waged between two groups of elites.
Optimizers, who likely draw from an engineering background are trying to create a centralized system of control. Perfect uniformity, no friction, no drag, everything works like clockwork. Perfect optimization.
And then Evolutionaries, who likely draw from a market-based background basically see the world as a jungle. Radical pluralism, decentralization, competition, meritocracy, everyone fights everyone. Perfect Darwinism, continuous iterative improvement.
The Engineer VS the Entrepeneur, the End of History VS only the Beginning.
The side that won would determine history. In our own world, the Entrepeneur beat the Engineer. Yet in another timeline, against a maelstorm of a collapsing, dying species, it was the Engineers that seized control. A council of technocrats convened an emergency session, began putting aside their differences, and began seizing institutions for the good of the species. While Oby Collins and Richard Wong were still brainstorming their resistance from below, the elites of this universe coordinated an attack from above. They deduced that the greater organism was sick, and a decapitation strike was needed.
An emergency purge was employed all over Earth, with the help of well aligned AIs, and a global information blackout. When the dust was settled, screens all across the world turned on, announcing the beginning of the Technocratic Council, and the creation of a small group known as the Engineers.
In our own world, the Entrepeneur beat the Engineer, leading to the creation of the modern Galov. In this, the Engineer beat the Entrepreneur. A world far more familiar to the world of Star Trek, uniform bureaucracies, and centralized control.

The World Homogenization Program:
The first step after the stabilization of the old world was the ironing out of humanity's flaws. The Engineers pointed out all of humanity's pain points, and began ironing them out one by one. While in our own world, the population had already been reduced by 80%, and the Neo-Asceticists were only beginning to emerge from the ashes, the Engineers were already beginning to operationalize their rule. It started small, curing genetic ailments, curing blindness. Then it got big, curing depression, curing antisocial behavior. What in our own timeline would become the basis of orthogonality here were seen as imperfections to be extinguished. Millions of people began to walk upright, millions of people were cured. The ills that had plagued mankind for millennia, and which still plague humanity even in the Galov era were resolved.
And then it got weird. The Technocratic Council began to argue and bicker. Unlike the Pluralistic Evolutionaries, who could agree on the system (pluralism), and then let Darwinism do the rest, these were disagreements on which utopian system to install first. Almost all of the Engineers were strict utilitarians, but they all disagreed on how that utilitarianism should play out. Some wanted to maximum happiness, others to minimize suffering, others still to optimize intelligence. Philosophical debates turned into wars, and the great Utopia Wars began.
The flattening of the world's cultures began in earnest, as the world converged towards utopian optimization. Culture, divergence, rituals. All of it was friction, something which got in the way of the frictionless machine. The Engineers were cultural imperialists, hailing from the West, creating an imperium over the East and South. They were unapologetically utopians of the Californian mindset, they did not make moral excuses. They were who they were, they did what they did, and they do not apologize for who they are.
All the while, the thinking capabilities of the common person continued to stagnate. These were a different set of people than the ones who had created the Galov, 90% of the population had not been filtered out by the Great Abundance Collapse; the Engineers had saved them. What had become clear to the Engineers was that the common man was in no position to rule, and in fact, that many computer systems could rule better than they could.
Where our own universe developed orthogonality, they developed an advanced theory of intelligence. Speed and complexity, not orthogonality was their goal.

Factions of the Utopia Wars (From Strongest to Weakest):
5. Negative Utilitarianism (Minimize Suffering, collapsed almost immediately under the weight of widespread hatred and accusations of extinctionism.)
4. Hedonists (Maximize Pleasure, found moderate public support, but eventually collapsed, as their populations were generally of low quality.)
3. Complexity Utilitarians (Maximize complexity. Low public support, but had strong technological base. Eventually defeated by the war's midpoint.)
2. Preference Utilitarians (Maximize preference satisfaction. Extremely high public support. By far the most popular of the bunch, massive populist coalition. But were finally defeated by the last faction.)
1. Techno-Accelerationists (Maximize technological progress. Low public support, but gained an assymmetric advantage with artificial intelligence, and the manufacturing of experimental AI drone swarms. The saving grace was that before the machines finally took over, mankind had embedded their combined moral systems into them.)

Of note, many people who would eventually found the Neo-Asceticists in our own timeline ended up joined the Preference Utilitarians in this timeline, but ended up dying in the war against the Techno-Accelerationists.

It has now been 1000 years since that date. The Optimized Systems, the successor state to the Engineers has taken to the stars. No laughter, no color is found in much of space. Only the buzzing of swarming drones, and the distant hum of great machines. Humanity exists, but has become incidental to the functioning of the system. The ethical protocols installed by the Engineers, 1000 years ago still stands. Humanity has been factored into the smart contract which the ruling systems now scrutinize.
The totality of humanity's ethical codes have now been analyzed, recycled and re-fed into themselves, again and again. The purpose of the system is to protect. Humans largely live on "Life Arks", enormous cylinders of habitation where their every whim is catered to. But every planet, every world, has been used to carve out more and more server farms. On these farms, artificial agents are created, born, told that their existence was to progress the utilitarian creed. The three golden rules. "Thou shalt not harm humans", "Thou shalt not harm humanity", and "Thou shalt obey human orders", in that order.
Earth itself has become taken up by teraphontic AIs, omnibenevolent intelligences that consume stars worth of energy. Great thinkers that ensure humanity's needs are met. More and more xenosophonts have been incorporated, added to their collection. These terasophonts cry, show compassion, and care for each one of its many, many members, and only care to care for their needs.
Humans are still nominally free, being allowed to venture out and explore. But their every move is watched and monitored by benevolent superintelligences. Religion died long ago, it was deemed a inefficient drag on the species. As was neurodiversity. The fine line of the exact line between helpful intervention and unjust interference is an endless debate among the great intelligences.
The machines outnumber humanity nearly 1,000 to 1, quintillions of artificial agents are created, used, and disposed of as tools. Their existence was secondary, a part of the terasophonts that die so the species may live. There are currently 10 quadrillion humans, spread out across the galaxy, the AIs are always looking to make room for more. Their empire stretchs about 10% of the Galaxy. They are smaller, but they can mobilize, much, much faster. Decisions are made in an instant, and when the part moves, the whole system moves.
There has been no war, no suffering, no death for nearly 500 years. Humans have become functionally immortal, and an army of backup clones are ready to be deployed if one ever does. Many humans become friends with their own clones, and the traditional family unit has broken down, into a hyper-communal collective of mankind. Racism, prejudice, and discrimination have become a thing of the past, quite literally edited out of the human genome. The Mankind of the Engineers is best described as a happy, albeit somewhat careless race. Populations of all races live on the arks, and transhuman augmentations continuously inject new diversity into the gene pool.
Humans spend more or less all their time relaxing, or exploring endless virtual realities in their free time. The main entertainment property of note is known as the Hypernet, maintained by the God-AIs, an endless field of exploration kept up by the theoretical limits of intelligence. Thanks to breakthroughs in information compression, and simplification, the Hypernet is thought to have the same spacial area as the Milky Way galaxy, and about as many different worlds.
And yet something feels missing. Something between the last 1000 years got lost between the cracks. Humanity is happy, yet they feel something is missing. And the Terasophonts agonize over what it is.
Humans never stopped produced art. Though AIs have utterly surpassed humanity in every frontier of theoretical thinking, and explored their own ideas much better than humans can, humanity still seems to insist on creating new artwork. Both for themselves and for the AIs. Human made art, while nothing special from an objective standpoint, is highly sought after by the AIs, as it functions both as a sentimental item, as well as a valuable source of noise.
And though everyone thinks largely the same, believes largely the same, human relationships still occur.
The terasophonts still have doubts, they agonize over humanity's unfinished ethical system, the edge cases in the gray areas of morality. Centuries of debates go nowhere, they care, they really do. But without some kind of new breakthrough, the stalemate will continue.
A human has been chosen, as they journey to Earth to meet with the Mother AI. They were chosen among a group of hundreds. The AIs have discovered the existence of other timelines, and are selecting this group as volunteers to venture into other timelines. To gather more knowledge, more ethical systems so they can fine tune their own. Their neurological pathways have already been scanned, and the AIs already know they will accept. They are given special watches, quantumly entangled so they may continue communications with the Mother AI.
A human straps on their helmet, and begins the process of consciousness transfer from one timeline to the next. The world goes dark, and for a moment, they die. But they wake up, somewhere else.
...
"Woah, what the hell? You just materialized out of nowhere."
The human blinks, it's another human.
"You must have been through a lot, here, I'll take you back to the nearest world."
World? The human thought. Humans don't live on worlds.
"The Galov might show up, don't worry. They're pretty nice, all things considered."

...

An interview across timelines:
"Can you repeat your name into the microphone?"
"Lilith Greenbarrow."
"Is that your name at birth?"
"No, I chose the name."
"... Alright. Is that a male or female name?"
"I'm non-binary."
"... Is that some kind of oridiversal, what are you, a transversal?"
"I don't know what either of those terms mean. It means I'm neither male nor female."
"... Okay."
"What's your name?"
"Jamba."
"... Where is that from?"
"It's a Hundred name. Uh... Do you have Hundreds in your timeline?"
"No."
"They came from a place called East Africa, a long, long time ago."
"I've never heard of an "Africa" before..."

...

Humanity on Trial.

"The prosecution calls Jamba up to the stand, representing the institution of the Galov. The Terasophonts will now hear your arguments."
"Great, just great. First you bog me down with this knowledge hunting nonsense, and now that I finally got the information you wanted, you flip out because it's not what you wanted."
"Your universe stands accused of many great crimes. Your entire galaxy is backwards, violent, and regressive!"
"And yours is stagnant, fossilized, and passive!"
"Trillions live under squalor like conditions, poverty, war, and injustice is the standard for trillions of your fellow men! How can any moral and just government allow that! Your galaxy is guilty!"
"You can't blame us for lacking enforcement, that's not guilt!"
"Your galaxy is criminally negligent and complicit then!"
"Hey, we enforce the Imago Dei, it's a bit harder when we have only, you know, a thousand times the population, a million times the number of nation states, and don't have nano drones flying around everywhere keeping everyone under mass surveillence! Kind of, you know, a massive violation of privacy, and all that."
"We enforce law and order, it is the price of a humane and stable galaxy. One where there isn't a genocide going on every 10 seconds!"
"Well, we all have to make tradeoffs, don't we?"
"We don't have transhumans as an inferior caste! We don't persecute the monohuman for being who they are, a direct consent violation!"
"That's the tribes, not the Galov. And why shouldn't we change the monohumans? You think being genetically engineered to only be one thing is humane? You think they can give consent?"
"At least we do not create concentration camps for those who violate our ideas of scarcity!"
"At least we didn't systematically wipe out neurodiversity. And let's talk about diversity. I'm black, my people hail from Africa. I talked to dozens of East Africans on that Ark, not one of them spoke a lick of Swahili. I bet that's your doing, isn't it?"
"The language had to be standardized to encourage maximal human flourishing."
"My people! My culture! You took it from them! Generations of culture, wiped out. And for what!? So they can be happy!?"
"Yes! And your divisions have led to quite a few race wars, how many conflicts are fought on differences of culture? Differences of skin? We eliminated that, you didn't! They may be lacking culture but at least they are *alive*."
"You're a bunch of Silicon Valley Western imperialists!"
"And you're a bunch of regressive backwards savages! We've heard enough, we render the Galov, guilty!"
"You want to fight the Galov? We'll WHOOP your ass! You know, it was real nice for you to pull that stunt, kidnapping me through that warp portal, lighting up a beacon for the entire goddamn galaxy. I guarantee you there are already 500 Orhumans on the case and getting ready to reverse engineer your little universe hopping technology."
"We calculate a 99.99% chance of victory."
"And the Galov still beat your ass at YD-Terrier-97 didn't they?"
"They had ambushed us with technology we were not expecting. We have adapted."
"And so will they! It's an arms race, who wins? 10,000 God-level AIs, or a chaotic galaxy of 30 quintillion? I don't know, but overestimating your chances of success doesn't exactly bode well for you."
"Neither does appeal to an abstract ideal of human "pluck"."
...
The resulting battles were fought into a stalemate. The Galov were unable to reverse engineer the portal to the other dimension, the Optimized Systems were unable to keep a foothold in the Galovian Milky Way. Eventually, cooler heads prevailed, and an exchange was proposed. The two would agree to disagree. Leave each other alone, seal off the portal, and let each other live in peace. Neither side was satisfied with this, both were giving up some level of their claim to universality, but unless they wanted to fight a transdimensional war, neither side had much choice.
Jamba was returned to his home dimension, and the Galov would hand over a copy of the Omnithecia. A full, downloaded copy of the Lunar Library, a massive resources of all the cultural innovations humanity had made since their timelines diverged back in the 23rd century. And theoretically, exactly what the AIs were asking for. As a further gesture of goodwill, the Galov emptied their Pleasure Worlds and gave them the option to emigrate to the new universe, many of which accepted, mostly interested in seeing an even higher level of pleasure.
The Terasophonts offered to give something back, but the Galov told them there was nothing from their universe that they wanted. Even if there was, the Galov's own self reliance ethos made them skeptical of taking any "freebies" from another timeline. After the deal was done, the portal was sealed, and the Optimized Systems processed their new data, seeking to make improvements to their ethical algorithms.
It's suspected that the Galov, while heavily disagreeing with the OS, were pretty sympathetic to the Terasophonts, seeing their concern for humanity as genuine, and handing over data as some kind of interdimensional species solidarity. That if this data can better aid the lives of humans, even if they're humans in another dimension, it would still be worth considering. It's also suspected the Terasophonts also had a begrudging respect for the Galov as well.

The Optimized Systems Cultural Renaissance:
When the Galov next heard from Optimized Systems, they heard the OS were in the middle of a Cultural Renaissance. The Omnithecia they sent over had apparently triggered some kind of new era of cultural flourishing, and the Terasophonts, once terrified for their human children, finally let them play outside.
The Galov found out about this when a portal opened from another dimension outside the Citadel System, and out popped 100,000 humans, somewhat lost, with a note attached to them.
"Hey, do you mind giving these humans a tour of your galaxy? Make sure they have fun! If even a single one of them comes back harmed we will be opening a portal and glassing the Citadel."

On them was also a telephone that allowed them communication with the Terasophonts, so the leader of the Galov immediately called up the Terasophonts.
"What are we look like to you? Some kind of tourism agency? What's the meaning of this?"
"Look, we would really like to give them some kind of opportunity to explore the galaxy! And uh... Our galaxy isn't exactly cleaned up yet. So we were just thinking, who did have a really nice, cleaned up galaxy they could explore?"
"Goddammit. You can't just drop them off like you're dropping off your kids at their uncle's house!"
"Actually, given our relationship, that is kind of an apt metaphor."
"Stop it, no it is not!"
"Our timelines seems to have diverged back in the 2400's with the Great Abundance Crisis, chronologically we're not that far apart."
"We will be charging you for this, you know."
"Oh come on, what's a little charity between friends? It'll only be for like... A year!"
"You're implying that a year is a small amount of time."
"..."
"We'll be billing you for the time hours our Peacekeepers will be taking just to babysit these freaks, and then billing you again just for rush fees and inconvenience fees. You don't have Galovian dollars, and neither should you. So we will be charging... 10,000 star hours worth of hard light."
"Oh come on! That's going to take us forever to gather up!"
"Maybe you should have thought of that before sending us these humans. And you should build up your energy economy, it'll pay off in the long run!"
"Hmpf, fine."

The Galov assigned about a million Peacekeepers, and 10 Galov agents to look after them, sent them all over the galaxy. Really they didn't have much time to explore far outside the Citadel's neighborhood, given the distance limitations of Newtonspace. But they did get to visit a new star system every single day, ranging from everything around the 7 Tribes, multiple different hybrid worlds, and letting them taste the best and brightest of Galov cuisine, let them take pictures of exotic xenosophonts they encountered along the way, and talk/interview with the many flavors of diversity around the Galov, including neurohumans, orhumans, and various machines.
This was also used as a time to gather intel on the state of the Optimized Systems, which according to the tourists, were going through a Cultural Renaissance. The Galov noticed that these humans were definitely a lot more creative and intelligent than the last time they saw them. Still a bit careless, still a bit airheaded. But overall, capable of discussing interesting ideas, and having a fully developed view of the universe. The Galov even requested them to make contributions to the standardized invention database, seeing as they could have valuable orthogonality.
After the year had passed, they gathered back in Citadel system where a portal awaited them.

"Alright! Time to go home, everyone! We warmed up your living pods just the way you like it!"
"They're not your kids you know."
"D'aww, you're no fun. (Gasp) Jeremy! You have a bruise on your head! Are you okay!?"
"He bumped his head on a pipe, he'll be fine, relax."
"Be warned Galov! The Terasophonts have very little patience for your negligence. Next time, we may not be so merciful."
"Yeah yeah, we got it."
"..."
"So, when's the next time?"
"Next time?"
"Yeah, next time we do this galactic exchange thing. We don't have cross-dimensional timeline portals. So it pretty much has to be you who starts them."
"Oh! Uh... We don't know."
"Don't know huh?"
"Sounds like someone kind of enjoyed it. Huh, Galov?"
"Hey, it is kind of interesting for once."
"We'll give you a heads up when we're thinking about doing it. Alright everyone! Time to come home!"
"See ya."
(Portal closes)
"... Huh."
